package main

import (
	"fmt"
)

const mod = 100000007

func nQueens(size int) int {
	cols := make([]int, size)
	pos := make([]int, size*2+1)
	neg := make([]int, size*2+1)
	placement := make([]int, size)
	count := 0
	checksum := 0

	var recordSolution func()
	recordSolution = func() {
		count++
		serial := count
		for row := 0; row < size; row++ {
			checksum = (checksum + serial*(row+1)*(placement[row]+1)) % mod
		}
	}

	var backtrack func(int)
	backtrack = func(row int) {
		if row == size {
			recordSolution()
			return
		}
		for col := 0; col < size; col++ {
			p := row + col
			q := row - col + size - 1
			if cols[col] == 0 && pos[p] == 0 && neg[q] == 0 {
				cols[col] = 1
				pos[p] = 1
				neg[q] = 1
				placement[row] = col
				backtrack(row + 1)
				cols[col] = 0
				pos[p] = 0
				neg[q] = 0
			}
		}
	}

	backtrack(0)
	return (checksum + count*101) % mod
}

N-Queens / Haskell

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/haskell/workloads/n_queens.hs 

{-# LANGUAGE BangPatterns #-}

module Main where

import Control.Monad (when)
import Data.Array.IO (IOUArray)
import Data.Array.MArray (newArray, readArray, writeArray)
import Data.IORef (modifyIORef', newIORef, readIORef)

modValue :: Int
modValue = 100000007

nQueens :: Int -> IO Int
nQueens size = do
  cols <- newArray (0, size - 1) 0 :: IO (IOUArray Int Int)
  pos <- newArray (0, size * 2) 0 :: IO (IOUArray Int Int)
  neg <- newArray (0, size * 2) 0 :: IO (IOUArray Int Int)
  placement <- newArray (0, size - 1) 0 :: IO (IOUArray Int Int)
  countRef <- newIORef 0
  checksumRef <- newIORef 0

  let recordSolution = do
        modifyIORef' countRef (+ 1)
        serial <- readIORef countRef
        let loop row
              | row >= size = pure ()
              | otherwise = do
                  col <- readArray placement row
                  modifyIORef' checksumRef (\acc -> (acc + serial * (row + 1) * (col + 1)) `mod` modValue)
                  loop (row + 1)
        loop 0

      backtrack row
        | row >= size = recordSolution
        | otherwise = tryCol 0
        where
          tryCol col
            | col >= size = pure ()
            | otherwise = do
                let p = row + col
                    q = row - col + size - 1
                colUsed <- readArray cols col
                posUsed <- readArray pos p
                negUsed <- readArray neg q
                if colUsed == 0 && posUsed == 0 && negUsed == 0
                  then do
                    writeArray cols col 1
                    writeArray pos p 1
                    writeArray neg q 1
                    writeArray placement row col
                    backtrack (row + 1)
                    writeArray cols col 0
                    writeArray pos p 0
                    writeArray neg q 0
                    tryCol (col + 1)
                  else tryCol (col + 1)

  backtrack 0
  count <- readIORef countRef
  checksum <- readIORef checksumRef
  pure ((checksum + count * 101) `mod` modValue)

main :: IO ()
main = do
  let n = 12
  result <- nQueens n
  print result

N-Queens / Java

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/java/workloads/NQueens.java 

public final class NQueens {
    private static final int MOD = 100000007;

    private NQueens() {}

    private static int nQueens(int size) {
        final int[] cols = new int[size];
        final int[] pos = new int[size * 2 + 1];
        final int[] neg = new int[size * 2 + 1];
        final int[] placement = new int[size];
        final int[] count = new int[] {0};
        final int[] hash = new int[] {0};

        backtrackQueens(0, size, cols, pos, neg, placement, count, hash);
        return (hash[0] + count[0] * 101) % MOD;
    }

    private static void backtrackQueens(
        int row,
        int size,
        int[] cols,
        int[] pos,
        int[] neg,
        int[] placement,
        int[] count,
        int[] hash
    ) {
        if (row == size) {
            count[0] += 1;
            final int serial = count[0];
            for (int rowIx = 0; rowIx < size; rowIx += 1) {
                hash[0] = (hash[0] + serial * (rowIx + 1) * (placement[rowIx] + 1)) % MOD;
            }
            return;
        }

        for (int col = 0; col < size; col += 1) {
            final int p = row + col;
            final int q = row - col + size - 1;
            if (cols[col] == 0 && pos[p] == 0 && neg[q] == 0) {
                cols[col] = 1;
                pos[p] = 1;
                neg[q] = 1;
                placement[row] = col;
                backtrackQueens(row + 1, size, cols, pos, neg, placement, count, hash);
                cols[col] = 0;
                pos[p] = 0;
                neg[q] = 0;
            }
        }
    }
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        final int n = 12;
        final int result = nQueens(n);
        System.out.println(result);
    }
}

N-Queens / JavaScript

const MOD = 100000007;

function nQueens(size) {
  const cols = Array(size).fill(0);
  const pos = Array(size * 2 + 1).fill(0);
  const neg = Array(size * 2 + 1).fill(0);
  const placement = Array(size).fill(0);
  let count = 0;
  let hash = 0;

  function recordSolution() {
    count += 1;
    const serial = count;
    for (let row = 0; row < size; row += 1) {
      hash = (hash + serial * (row + 1) * (placement[row] + 1)) % MOD;
    }
  }

  function backtrack(row) {
    if (row === size) {
      recordSolution();
      return;
    }
    for (let col = 0; col < size; col += 1) {
      const p = row + col;
      const q = row - col + size - 1;
      if (cols[col] === 0 && pos[p] === 0 && neg[q] === 0) {
        cols[col] = 1;
        pos[p] = 1;
        neg[q] = 1;
        placement[row] = col;
        backtrack(row + 1);
        cols[col] = 0;
        pos[p] = 0;
        neg[q] = 0;
      }
    }
  }

  backtrack(0);
  return (hash + count * 101) % MOD;
}

const N = 12;
const result = nQueens(N);
process.stdout.write(`${result}
`);

local MOD = 100000007

local function n_queens(size)
  local cols = {}
  local pos = {}
  local neg = {}
  local placement = {}
  for i = 1, size do
    cols[i] = 0
    placement[i] = 0
  end
  for i = 1, size * 2 + 1 do
    pos[i] = 0
    neg[i] = 0
  end

  local count = 0
  local checksum = 0

  local backtrack
  backtrack = function(row)
    if row == size then
      count = count + 1
      local serial = count
      for row_ix = 1, size do
        checksum = (checksum + serial * row_ix * (placement[row_ix] + 1)) % MOD
      end
      return
    end

    for col = 0, size - 1 do
      local p = row + col + 1
      local q = row - col + size
      local col_ix = col + 1
      if cols[col_ix] == 0 and pos[p] == 0 and neg[q] == 0 then
        cols[col_ix] = 1
        pos[p] = 1
        neg[q] = 1
        placement[row + 1] = col
        backtrack(row + 1)
        cols[col_ix] = 0
        pos[p] = 0
        neg[q] = 0
      end
    end
  end

  backtrack(0)
  return (checksum + count * 101) % MOD
end

print(result)

let mod_value = 100000007

let imod x = x mod mod_value

let n_queens size =
  let cols = Array.make size 0 in
  let pos = Array.make ((size * 2) + 1) 0 in
  let neg = Array.make ((size * 2) + 1) 0 in
  let placement = Array.make size 0 in
  let count = ref 0 in
  let checksum = ref 0 in
  let rec backtrack row =
    if row = size then (
      incr count;
      let serial = !count in
      for row_ix = 0 to size - 1 do
        checksum := imod (!checksum + (serial * (row_ix + 1) * (placement.(row_ix) + 1)))
      done
    ) else
      for col = 0 to size - 1 do
        let p = row + col in
        let q = row - col + size - 1 in
        if cols.(col) = 0 && pos.(p) = 0 && neg.(q) = 0 then (
          cols.(col) <- 1;
          pos.(p) <- 1;
          neg.(q) <- 1;
          placement.(row) <- col;
          backtrack (row + 1);
          cols.(col) <- 0;
          pos.(p) <- 0;
          neg.(q) <- 0)
      done
  in
  backtrack 0;
  imod (!checksum + (!count * 101))

use strict;
use warnings;

use constant MOD => 100000007;

sub parse_args {
    my (@argv) = @_;
    return \@argv;
}

sub n_queens {
    my ($size) = @_;
    my @cols = (0) x $size;
    my @pos = (0) x ($size * 2 + 1);
    my @neg = (0) x ($size * 2 + 1);
    my @placement = (0) x $size;
    my $count = 0;
    my $checksum = 0;

    my $backtrack;
    $backtrack = sub {
        my ($row) = @_;
        if ($row == $size) {
            $count += 1;
            my $serial = $count;
            for (my $row_ix = 0; $row_ix < $size; $row_ix += 1) {
                $checksum = ($checksum + $serial * ($row_ix + 1) * ($placement[$row_ix] + 1)) % MOD;
            }
            return;
        }
        for (my $col = 0; $col < $size; $col += 1) {
            my $p = $row + $col;
            my $q = $row - $col + $size - 1;
            if ($cols[$col] == 0 && $pos[$p] == 0 && $neg[$q] == 0) {
                $cols[$col] = 1;
                $pos[$p] = 1;
                $neg[$q] = 1;
                $placement[$row] = $col;
                $backtrack->($row + 1);
                $cols[$col] = 0;
                $pos[$p] = 0;
                $neg[$q] = 0;
            }
        }
    };

    $backtrack->(0);
    return ($checksum + $count * 101) % MOD;
}

my $N = 12;
my $result = n_queens(0 + $N);
print "$result\n";

const MOD = 100000007;

function n_queens(int $size): int {

    $neg = array_fill(0, $size * 2 + 1, 0);

    $count = 0;
    $checksum = 0;

    $backtrack = function (int $row) use ($size, &$cols, &$pos, &$neg, &$placement, &$count, &$checksum, &$backtrack): void {
        if ($row === $size) {
            $count += 1;
            $serial = $count;
            for ($rowIx = 0; $rowIx < $size; $rowIx += 1) {
                $checksum = ($checksum + $serial * ($rowIx + 1) * ($placement[$rowIx] + 1)) % MOD;
            }
            return;
        }

        for ($col = 0; $col < $size; $col += 1) {
            $p = $row + $col;
            $q = $row - $col + $size - 1;
            if ($cols[$col] === 0 && $pos[$p] === 0 && $neg[$q] === 0) {
                $cols[$col] = 1;
                $pos[$p] = 1;
                $neg[$q] = 1;
                $placement[$row] = $col;
                $backtrack($row + 1);
                $cols[$col] = 0;
                $pos[$p] = 0;
                $neg[$q] = 0;
            }
        }
    };

    $backtrack(0);
    return ($checksum + $count * 101) % MOD;
}

#!/usr/bin/env python3

from __future__ import annotations

import sys


MOD = 100000007


def n_queens(size: int) -> int:
    cols = [0] * size
    pos = [0] * (size * 2 + 1)
    neg = [0] * (size * 2 + 1)
    placement = [0] * size
    count = 0
    checksum = 0

    def record_solution() -> None:
        nonlocal count, checksum
        count += 1
        serial = count
        for row in range(size):
            checksum = (checksum + serial * (row + 1) * (placement[row] + 1)) % MOD

    def backtrack(row: int) -> None:
        if row == size:
            record_solution()
            return
        for col in range(size):
            p = row + col
            q = row - col + size - 1
            if cols[col] == 0 and pos[p] == 0 and neg[q] == 0:
                cols[col] = 1
                pos[p] = 1
                neg[q] = 1
                placement[row] = col
                backtrack(row + 1)
                cols[col] = 0
                pos[p] = 0
                neg[q] = 0

    backtrack(0)
    return (checksum + count * 101) % MOD

N-Queens / R

#!/usr/bin/env Rscript

MOD <- 100000007

n_queens <- function(size) {
  cols <- integer(size)
  pos <- integer(size * 2 + 1)
  neg <- integer(size * 2 + 1)
  placement <- integer(size)
  count <- 0
  checksum <- 0

  record_solution <- function() {
    count <<- count + 1
    serial <- count
    for (row in 0:(size - 1)) {
      checksum <<- (checksum + serial * (row + 1) * (placement[[row + 1]] + 1)) %% MOD
    }
  }

  backtrack <- function(row) {
    if (row == size) {
      record_solution()
      return()
    }
    for (col in 0:(size - 1)) {
      p <- row + col
      q <- row - col + size - 1
      if (cols[[col + 1]] == 0 && pos[[p + 1]] == 0 && neg[[q + 1]] == 0) {
        cols[[col + 1]] <<- 1
        pos[[p + 1]] <<- 1
        neg[[q + 1]] <<- 1
        placement[[row + 1]] <<- col
        backtrack(row + 1)
        cols[[col + 1]] <<- 0
        pos[[p + 1]] <<- 0
        neg[[q + 1]] <<- 0
      }
    }
  }

  backtrack(0)
  (checksum + count * 101) %% MOD
}

args <- commandArgs(trailingOnly = TRUE)
size <- 12
result <- n_queens(size)
cat(as.integer(result), "\n", sep = "")

N-Queens / Ruby

MOD = 100_000_007

def n_queens(size)
  cols = Array.new(size, 0)
  pos = Array.new(size * 2 + 1, 0)
  neg = Array.new(size * 2 + 1, 0)
  placement = Array.new(size, 0)
  count = 0
  checksum = 0

  backtrack = lambda do |row|
    if row == size
      count += 1
      serial = count
      row_ix = 0
      while row_ix < size
        checksum = (checksum + serial * (row_ix + 1) * (placement[row_ix] + 1)) % MOD
        row_ix += 1
      end
      next
    end

    col = 0
    while col < size
      p = row + col
      q = row - col + size - 1
      if cols[col].zero? && pos[p].zero? && neg[q].zero?
        cols[col] = 1
        pos[p] = 1
        neg[q] = 1
        placement[row] = col
        backtrack.call(row + 1)
        cols[col] = 0
        pos[p] = 0
        neg[q] = 0
      end
      col += 1
    end
  end

  backtrack.call(0)
  (checksum + count * 101) % MOD
end

N = 12
result = n_queens(N)
puts(result)

N-Queens / Rust

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/rust/src/bin/n_queens.rs 

const MOD: i32 = 100_000_007;

fn n_queens(size: i32) -> i32 {
    let mut cols = vec![0_i8; size as usize];
    let mut pos = vec![0_i8; (size * 2 + 1) as usize];
    let mut neg = vec![0_i8; (size * 2 + 1) as usize];
    let mut placement = vec![0_i32; size as usize];
    let mut count = 0_i32;
    let mut hash = 0_i32;

    fn backtrack(
        row: i32,
        size: i32,
        cols: &mut [i8],
        pos: &mut [i8],
        neg: &mut [i8],
        placement: &mut [i32],
        count: &mut i32,
        hash: &mut i32
    ) {
        if row == size {
            *count += 1;
            let serial = *count;
            for row_ix in 0..size as usize {
                *hash =
                    (*hash + serial * ((row_ix as i32) + 1) * (placement[row_ix] + 1)) % MOD;
            }
            return;
        }

        for col in 0..size {
            let p = (row + col) as usize;
            let q = (row - col + size - 1) as usize;
            if cols[col as usize] == 0 && pos[p] == 0 && neg[q] == 0 {
                cols[col as usize] = 1;
                pos[p] = 1;
                neg[q] = 1;
                placement[row as usize] = col;
                backtrack(row + 1, size, cols, pos, neg, placement, count, hash);
                cols[col as usize] = 0;
                pos[p] = 0;
                neg[q] = 0;
            }
        }
    }

    backtrack(0, size, &mut cols, &mut pos, &mut neg, &mut placement, &mut count, &mut hash);
    (hash + count * 101) % MOD
}


fn main() {
    let n = 12;
    let result = n_queens(n);
    println!("{}", result);
}

object NQueens {
  private final val Mod = 100000007

  private def nQueens(size: Int): Int = {
    val cols = Array.fill(size)(0)
    val pos = Array.fill(size * 2 + 1)(0)
    val neg = Array.fill(size * 2 + 1)(0)
    val placement = Array.fill(size)(0)
    val count = Array(0)
    val hash = Array(0)

    def backtrack(row: Int): Unit = {
      if (row == size) {
        count(0) += 1
        val serial = count(0)
        var rowIx = 0
        while (rowIx < size) {
          hash(0) = (hash(0) + serial * (rowIx + 1) * (placement(rowIx) + 1)) % Mod
          rowIx += 1
        }
      } else {
        var col = 0
        while (col < size) {
          val p = row + col
          val q = row - col + size - 1
          if (cols(col) == 0 && pos(p) == 0 && neg(q) == 0) {
            cols(col) = 1
            pos(p) = 1
            neg(q) = 1
            placement(row) = col
            backtrack(row + 1)
            cols(col) = 0
            pos(p) = 0
            neg(q) = 0
          }
          col += 1
        }
      }
    }

    backtrack(0)
    (hash(0) + count(0) * 101) % Mod
  }

let mod = 100_000_007

func nQueens(_ size: Int) -> Int {

                checksum = (checksum + serial * (rowIx + 1) * (placement[rowIx] + 1)) % mod
                rowIx += 1

                placement[row] = col
                backtrack(row + 1)
                cols[col] = 0
                pos[p] = 0
                neg[q] = 0

Game of Life / Gliders / Que (my language)

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/que/gof_glider.que 

(let MOD 100000007)

(let idx (lambda size x y (+ x (* y size))))

(let wrap1 (lambda v n
  (if (< v 0)
      (+ v n)
      (if (>= v n) (- v n) v))))

(let new-board (lambda size (do
  (let board [])
  (mut i 0)
  (while (< i (* size size)) (do
    (set! board (length board) 0)
    (alter! i (+ i 1))))
  board)))

(let set-cell! (lambda board size x y value (do
  (set! board (idx size (wrap1 x size) (wrap1 y size)) value)
  nil)))

(let add-glider! (lambda board size y x (do
  (set-cell! board size (+ x 1) (+ y 2) 1)
  (set-cell! board size (+ x 2) (+ y 2) 1)
  (set-cell! board size (+ x 3) (+ y 2) 1)
  (set-cell! board size (+ x 3) (+ y 1) 1)
  (set-cell! board size (+ x 2) (+ y 0) 1)
  nil)))

(let neighbor-count (lambda board size x y (do
  (mut sm 0)
  (mut dy -1)
  (while (<= dy 1) (do
    (mut dx -1)
    (while (<= dx 1) (do
      (if (or (not (= dx 0)) (not (= dy 0)))
          (do
            (let nx (wrap1 (+ x dx) size))
            (let ny (wrap1 (+ y dy) size))
            (alter! sm (+ sm (get board (idx size nx ny)))))
          nil)
      (alter! dx (+ dx 1))))
    (alter! dy (+ dy 1))))
  sm)))

(let step-and-hash (lambda board size weight (do
  (let next (new-board size))
  (mut acc weight)
  (mut y 0)
  (while (< y size) (do
    (mut x 0)
    (while (< x size) (do
      (let i (idx size x y))
      (let alive (get board i))
      (let n (neighbor-count board size x y))
      (let out (cond
        (and (= alive 1) (or (= n 2) (= n 3))) 1
        (and (= alive 0) (= n 3)) 1
        0))
      (set! next i out)
      (if (= out 1)
          (alter! acc (mod (+ acc (* (+ i 1) weight) 1) MOD))
          nil)
      (alter! x (+ x 1))))
    (alter! y (+ y 1))))
  { next (mod acc MOD) })))

(let STEPS 1200)
(let SIZE 96)

(let initial (new-board SIZE))
(add-glider! initial SIZE 0 0)
(add-glider! initial SIZE 5 3)
(add-glider! initial SIZE 1 3)
(add-glider! initial SIZE 6 4)
(variable STATE initial)
(mut step 0)
(mut acc 0)
(while (< step STEPS) (do
  (let { a b } (step-and-hash (get STATE) SIZE (+ step 1)))
  (set STATE a)
  (alter! acc (mod (+ acc b) MOD))
  (alter! step (+ step 1))))
acc

Game of Life / Gliders / Clojure

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/clojure/workloads/gof_glider.clj 

(set! *unchecked-math* true)

(def mod-value 100000007)

(defn parse-int ^long [^String text]
  (Long/parseLong text))

(defn wrap1 ^long [^long value ^long size]
  (cond
    (< value 0) (+ value size)
    (>= value size) (- value size)
    :else value))

(defn idx ^long [^long size ^long x ^long y]
  (+ x (* y size)))

(defn add-glider! [^ints board ^long size ^long y ^long x]
  (aset-int board (int (idx size (wrap1 (+ x 1) size) (wrap1 (+ y 2) size))) 1)
  (aset-int board (int (idx size (wrap1 (+ x 2) size) (wrap1 (+ y 2) size))) 1)
  (aset-int board (int (idx size (wrap1 (+ x 3) size) (wrap1 (+ y 2) size))) 1)
  (aset-int board (int (idx size (wrap1 (+ x 3) size) (wrap1 (+ y 1) size))) 1)
  (aset-int board (int (idx size (wrap1 (+ x 2) size) (wrap1 y size))) 1))

(defn step-life! ^long [^ints board ^ints next-board ^long size ^long weight]
  (loop [y 0
         acc weight]
    (if (= y size)
      acc
      (let [row-acc
            (loop [x 0
                   inner-acc acc]
              (if (= x size)
                inner-acc
                (let [sm
                      (loop [dy -1
                             total 0]
                        (if (> dy 1)
                          total
                          (recur
                            (unchecked-inc-int dy)
                            (loop [dx -1
                                   dx-total total]
                              (if (> dx 1)
                                dx-total
                                (recur
                                  (unchecked-inc-int dx)
                                  (if (or (not= dx 0) (not= dy 0))
                                    (+ dx-total
                                       (aget board
                                             (int (idx size (wrap1 (+ x dx) size) (wrap1 (+ y dy) size)))))
                                    dx-total)))))))
                      i (idx size x y)
                      alive (aget board (int i))
                      out (if (or (and (= alive 1) (or (= sm 2) (= sm 3)))
                                  (and (= alive 0) (= sm 3)))
                            1
                            0)
                      _ (aset-int next-board (int i) out)
                      next-acc (if (= out 1)
                                 (mod (+ inner-acc (* (inc i) weight) 1) mod-value)
                                 inner-acc)]
                  (recur (unchecked-inc-int x) next-acc))))]
        (recur (unchecked-inc-int y) row-acc)))))

(defn gof-glider ^long [^long steps ^long size]
  (let [board0 (int-array (int (* size size)))
        board1 (int-array (int (* size size)))]
    (add-glider! board0 size 0 0)
    (add-glider! board0 size 5 3)
    (add-glider! board0 size 1 3)
    (add-glider! board0 size 6 4)
    (loop [step 0
           ^ints board board0
           ^ints next-board board1
           acc 0]
      (if (= step steps)
        acc
        (let [frame-hash (step-life! board next-board size (unchecked-inc-int step))]
          (recur
            (unchecked-inc-int step)
            next-board
            board
            (mod (+ acc frame-hash) mod-value)))))))

(let [steps 1200
      size 96
      result (gof-glider steps size)]
  (println result))

Game of Life / Gliders / C++

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/cpp/workloads/gof_glider.cpp 

#include <cstdint>
#include <iostream>
#include <stdexcept>
#include <string>
#include <utility>
#include <vector>

namespace {

constexpr int MOD = 100000007;

int wrap1(int value, int size) {
    if (value < 0) {
        return value + size;
    }
    if (value >= size) {
        return value - size;
    }
    return value;
}

int idx(int size, int x, int y) {
    return x + y * size;
}

void add_glider(std::vector<int>& board, int size, int y, int x) {
    board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 1, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1;
    board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 2, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1;
    board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1;
    board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 1, size))] = 1;
    board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 2, size), wrap1(y + 0, size))] = 1;
}

std::pair<std::vector<int>, int> step_life(const std::vector<int>& board, int size, int weight) {
    std::vector<int> next_board(board.size(), 0);
    int acc = weight;
    for (int y = 0; y < size; ++y) {
        for (int x = 0; x < size; ++x) {
            int sum = 0;
            for (int dy = -1; dy <= 1; ++dy) {
                for (int dx = -1; dx <= 1; ++dx) {
                    if (dx != 0 || dy != 0) {
                        int nx = wrap1(x + dx, size);
                        int ny = wrap1(y + dy, size);
                        sum += board[idx(size, nx, ny)];
                    }
                }
            }
            int i = idx(size, x, y);
            int alive = board[i];
            int out = ((alive == 1 && (sum == 2 || sum == 3)) || (alive == 0 && sum == 3)) ? 1 : 0;
            next_board[i] = out;
            if (out == 1) {
                acc = (acc + (i + 1) * weight + 1) % MOD;
            }
        }
    }
    return {std::move(next_board), acc};
}

int gof_glider(int steps, int size) {
    std::vector<int> board(size * size, 0);
    add_glider(board, size, 0, 0);
    add_glider(board, size, 5, 3);
    add_glider(board, size, 1, 3);
    add_glider(board, size, 6, 4);
    int acc = 0;
    for (int step = 0; step < steps; ++step) {
        auto [next_board, frame_hash] = step_life(board, size, step + 1);
        board = std::move(next_board);
        acc = (acc + frame_hash) % MOD;
    }
    return acc;
}

}  // namespace

int main() {
    constexpr int steps = 1200;
    constexpr int size = 96;
    int result = gof_glider(steps, size);
    std::cout << result << '\n';
    return 0;
}

Game of Life / Gliders / C#

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/csharp/workloads/gof_glider.cs 

using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;

public static class GofGlider
{
    private const int Mod = 100000007;


    private static int Wrap1(int value, int size)
    {
        if (value < 0) return value + size;
        if (value >= size) return value - size;
        return value;
    }

    private static int Idx(int size, int x, int y) => x + y * size;

    private static void AddGlider(int[] board, int size, int y, int x)
    {
        board[Idx(size, Wrap1(x + 1, size), Wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1;
        board[Idx(size, Wrap1(x + 2, size), Wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1;
        board[Idx(size, Wrap1(x + 3, size), Wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1;
        board[Idx(size, Wrap1(x + 3, size), Wrap1(y + 1, size))] = 1;
        board[Idx(size, Wrap1(x + 2, size), Wrap1(y, size))] = 1;
    }

    private static int Benchmark(int steps, int size)
    {
        var board = new int[size * size];
        AddGlider(board, size, 0, 0);
        AddGlider(board, size, 5, 3);
        AddGlider(board, size, 1, 3);
        AddGlider(board, size, 6, 4);
        var acc = 0;

        for (var step = 0; step < steps; step += 1)
        {
            var next = new int[board.Length];
            var frameHash = step + 1;
            for (var y = 0; y < size; y += 1)
            {
                for (var x = 0; x < size; x += 1)
                {
                    var sm = 0;
                    for (var dy = -1; dy <= 1; dy += 1)
                    {
                        for (var dx = -1; dx <= 1; dx += 1)
                        {
                            if (dx != 0 || dy != 0)
                            {
                                sm += board[Idx(size, Wrap1(x + dx, size), Wrap1(y + dy, size))];
                            }
                        }
                    }

                    var i = Idx(size, x, y);
                    var alive = board[i];
                    var output = ((alive == 1 && (sm == 2 || sm == 3)) || (alive == 0 && sm == 3)) ? 1 : 0;
                    next[i] = output;
                    if (output == 1)
                    {
                        frameHash = (frameHash + (i + 1) * (step + 1) + 1) % Mod;
                    }
                }
            }
            board = next;
            acc = (acc + frameHash) % Mod;
        }

        return acc;
    }

    public static void Main(string[] args)
    {
        const int steps = 1200;
        const int size = 96;
        var result = Benchmark(steps, size);
        Console.WriteLine(result);
    }
}

Game of Life / Gliders / Dart

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/dart/workloads/gof_glider.dart 

import 'dart:io';

const int modValue = 100000007;

int wrap1(int value, int size) {
  if (value < 0) {
    return value + size;
  }
  if (value >= size) {
    return value - size;
  }
  return value;
}

int idx(int size, int x, int y) {
  return x + y * size;
}

void addGlider(List<int> board, int size, int y, int x) {
  board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 1, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1;
  board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 2, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1;
  board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1;
  board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 1, size))] = 1;
  board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 2, size), wrap1(y + 0, size))] = 1;
}

List<Object> stepLife(List<int> board, int size, int weight) {
  final nextBoard = List<int>.filled(board.length, 0);
  var acc = weight;
  var y = 0;
  while (y < size) {
    var x = 0;
    while (x < size) {
      var sum = 0;
      var dy = -1;
      while (dy <= 1) {
        var dx = -1;
        while (dx <= 1) {
          if (dx != 0 || dy != 0) {
            final nx = wrap1(x + dx, size);
            final ny = wrap1(y + dy, size);
            sum += board[idx(size, nx, ny)];
          }
          dx += 1;
        }
        dy += 1;
      }
      final i = idx(size, x, y);
      final alive = board[i];
      final out = ((alive == 1 && (sum == 2 || sum == 3)) || (alive == 0 && sum == 3)) ? 1 : 0;
      nextBoard[i] = out;
      if (out == 1) {
        acc = (acc + (i + 1) * weight + 1) % modValue;
      }
      x += 1;
    }
    y += 1;
  }
  return <Object>[nextBoard, acc];
}

int gofGlider(int steps, int size) {
  var board = List<int>.filled(size * size, 0);
  addGlider(board, size, 0, 0);
  addGlider(board, size, 5, 3);
  addGlider(board, size, 1, 3);
  addGlider(board, size, 6, 4);
  var acc = 0;
  var step = 0;
  while (step < steps) {
    final frame = stepLife(board, size, step + 1);
    board = frame[0] as List<int>;
    acc = (acc + (frame[1] as int)) % modValue;
    step += 1;
  }
  return acc;
}

void main(List<String> argv) {
  const steps = 1200;
  const size = 96;
  final result = gofGlider(steps, size);
  stdout.writeln(result);
}

Game of Life / Gliders / Go

package main

import (
	"fmt"
)

const mod = 100000007

func wrap1(value int, size int) int {
	if value < 0 {
		return value + size
	}
	if value >= size {
		return value - size
	}
	return value
}

func idx(size int, x int, y int) int {
	return x + y*size
}

func addGlider(board []int, size int, y int, x int) {
	board[idx(size, wrap1(x+1, size), wrap1(y+2, size))] = 1
	board[idx(size, wrap1(x+2, size), wrap1(y+2, size))] = 1
	board[idx(size, wrap1(x+3, size), wrap1(y+2, size))] = 1
	board[idx(size, wrap1(x+3, size), wrap1(y+1, size))] = 1
	board[idx(size, wrap1(x+2, size), wrap1(y+0, size))] = 1
}

func stepLife(board []int, size int, weight int) ([]int, int) {
	nextBoard := make([]int, len(board))
	acc := weight
	for y := 0; y < size; y++ {
		for x := 0; x < size; x++ {
			sum := 0
			for dy := -1; dy <= 1; dy++ {
				for dx := -1; dx <= 1; dx++ {
					if dx != 0 || dy != 0 {
						nx := wrap1(x+dx, size)
						ny := wrap1(y+dy, size)
						sum += board[idx(size, nx, ny)]
					}
				}
			}
			i := idx(size, x, y)
			alive := board[i]
			out := 0
			if (alive == 1 && (sum == 2 || sum == 3)) || (alive == 0 && sum == 3) {
				out = 1
			}
			nextBoard[i] = out
			if out == 1 {
				acc = (acc + (i+1)*weight + 1) % mod
			}
		}
	}
	return nextBoard, acc
}

func gofGlider(steps int, size int) int {
	board := make([]int, size*size)
	addGlider(board, size, 0, 0)
	addGlider(board, size, 5, 3)
	addGlider(board, size, 1, 3)
	addGlider(board, size, 6, 4)
	acc := 0
	for step := 0; step < steps; step++ {
		var frameHash int
		board, frameHash = stepLife(board, size, step+1)
		acc = (acc + frameHash) % mod
	}
	return acc
}


func main() {
	const steps = 1200
	const size = 96
	result := gofGlider(steps, size)
	fmt.Println(result)
}

Game of Life / Gliders / Haskell

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/haskell/workloads/gof_glider.hs 

{-# LANGUAGE BangPatterns #-}

module Main where

import Control.Monad (when)
import Data.Array.IO (IOUArray)
import Data.Array.MArray (newArray, readArray, writeArray)

modValue :: Int
modValue = 100000007

wrap1 :: Int -> Int -> Int
wrap1 value size
  | value < 0 = value + size
  | value >= size = value - size
  | otherwise = value

idx :: Int -> Int -> Int -> Int
idx size x y = x + y * size

addGlider :: IOUArray Int Int -> Int -> Int -> Int -> IO ()
addGlider board size y x = do
  writeArray board (idx size (wrap1 (x + 1) size) (wrap1 (y + 2) size)) 1
  writeArray board (idx size (wrap1 (x + 2) size) (wrap1 (y + 2) size)) 1
  writeArray board (idx size (wrap1 (x + 3) size) (wrap1 (y + 2) size)) 1
  writeArray board (idx size (wrap1 (x + 3) size) (wrap1 (y + 1) size)) 1
  writeArray board (idx size (wrap1 (x + 2) size) (wrap1 (y + 0) size)) 1

stepLife :: IOUArray Int Int -> IOUArray Int Int -> Int -> Int -> IO Int
stepLife board nextBoard size weight = rowLoop 0 weight
  where
    rowLoop y !acc
      | y >= size = pure acc
      | otherwise = colLoop y 0 acc >>= rowLoop (y + 1)

    colLoop y x !acc
      | x >= size = pure acc
      | otherwise = do
          sumNeighbors <- neighborLoop y x (-1) (-1) 0
          let i = idx size x y
          alive <- readArray board i
          let out
                | (alive == 1 && (sumNeighbors == 2 || sumNeighbors == 3)) || (alive == 0 && sumNeighbors == 3) = 1
                | otherwise = 0
              acc'
                | out == 1 = (acc + (i + 1) * weight + 1) `mod` modValue
                | otherwise = acc
          writeArray nextBoard i out
          colLoop y (x + 1) acc'

    neighborLoop y x dy dx !acc
      | dy > 1 = pure acc
      | dx > 1 = neighborLoop y x (dy + 1) (-1) acc
      | dx == 0 && dy == 0 = neighborLoop y x dy (dx + 1) acc
      | otherwise = do
          let nx = wrap1 (x + dx) size
              ny = wrap1 (y + dy) size
          value <- readArray board (idx size nx ny)
          neighborLoop y x dy (dx + 1) (acc + value)

gofGlider :: Int -> Int -> IO Int
gofGlider steps size = do
  boardA <- newArray (0, size * size - 1) 0 :: IO (IOUArray Int Int)
  boardB <- newArray (0, size * size - 1) 0 :: IO (IOUArray Int Int)
  addGlider boardA size 0 0
  addGlider boardA size 5 3
  addGlider boardA size 1 3
  addGlider boardA size 6 4
  let loop step !acc current next
        | step >= steps = pure acc
        | otherwise = do
            frameHash <- stepLife current next size (step + 1)
            let acc' = (acc + frameHash) `mod` modValue
            loop (step + 1) acc' next current
  loop 0 0 boardA boardB

main :: IO ()
main = do
  let steps = 1200
      size = 96
  result <- gofGlider steps size
  print result

public final class GofGlider {

            return value - size;
        }

    }

        board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1;
        board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 1, size))] = 1;
        board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 2, size), wrap1(y, size))] = 1;
    }

    private static int gofGlider(int steps, int size) {
        int[] board = new int[size * size];

        addGlider(board, size, 5, 3);
        addGlider(board, size, 1, 3);

                        for (int dx = -1; dx <= 1; dx += 1) {
                            if (dx != 0 || dy != 0) {
                                final int nx = wrap1(x + dx, size);
                                final int ny = wrap1(y + dy, size);
                                sm += board[idx(size, nx, ny)];
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    final int i = idx(size, x, y);
                    final int alive = board[i];
                    final int out = ((alive == 1 && (sm == 2 || sm == 3)) || (alive == 0 && sm == 3)) ? 1 : 0;
                    next[i] = out;
                    if (out == 1) {
                        frameHash = (frameHash + (i + 1) * (step + 1) + 1) % MOD;
                    }
                }
            }
            board = next;
            acc = (acc + frameHash) % MOD;
        }
        return acc;
    }

Game of Life / Gliders / JavaScript

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/javascript/workloads/gof_glider.js 

const MOD = 100000007;

function wrap1(v, n) {
  if (v < 0) return v + n;
  if (v >= n) return v - n;
  return v;
}

function idx(size, x, y) {
  return x + y * size;
}

function addGlider(board, size, y, x) {
  board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 1, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1;
  board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 2, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1;
  board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1;
  board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 1, size))] = 1;
  board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 2, size), wrap1(y + 0, size))] = 1;
}

function stepLife(board, size, weight) {
  const next = Array(board.length).fill(0);
  let acc = weight;
  for (let y = 0; y < size; y += 1) {
    for (let x = 0; x < size; x += 1) {
      let sm = 0;
      for (let dy = -1; dy <= 1; dy += 1) {
        for (let dx = -1; dx <= 1; dx += 1) {
          if (dx !== 0 || dy !== 0) {
            const nx = wrap1(x + dx, size);
            const ny = wrap1(y + dy, size);
            sm += board[idx(size, nx, ny)];
          }
        }
      }
      const i = idx(size, x, y);
      const alive = board[i];
      const out =
        (alive === 1 && (sm === 2 || sm === 3)) || (alive === 0 && sm === 3)
          ? 1
          : 0;
      next[i] = out;
      if (out === 1) {
        acc = (acc + (i + 1) * weight + 1) % MOD;
      }
    }
  }
  return [next, acc % MOD];
}

function gofGlider(steps, size) {
  let board = Array(size * size).fill(0);
  addGlider(board, size, 0, 0);
  addGlider(board, size, 5, 3);
  addGlider(board, size, 1, 3);
  addGlider(board, size, 6, 4);
  let acc = 0;
  for (let step = 0; step < steps; step += 1) {
    const [next, hash] = stepLife(board, size, step + 1);
    board = next;
    acc = (acc + hash) % MOD;
  }
  return acc;
}

const STEPS = 1200;
const SIZE = 96;
const result = gofGlider(STEPS, SIZE);
process.stdout.write(`${result}
`);

Game of Life / Gliders / Lua

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/lua/workloads/gof_glider.lua 

local MOD = 100000007

local function wrap1(value, size)
  if value < 0 then
    return value + size
  end
  if value >= size then
    return value - size
  end
  return value
end

local function idx(size, x, y)
  return x + y * size + 1
end

local function add_glider(board, size, y, x)
  board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 1, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1
  board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 2, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1
  board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1
  board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 1, size))] = 1
  board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 2, size), wrap1(y + 0, size))] = 1
end

local function step_life(board, size, weight)
  local next_board = {}
  for i = 1, #board do
    next_board[i] = 0
  end
  local acc = weight
  for y = 0, size - 1 do
    for x = 0, size - 1 do
      local sum = 0
      for dy = -1, 1 do
        for dx = -1, 1 do
          if dx ~= 0 or dy ~= 0 then
            local nx = wrap1(x + dx, size)
            local ny = wrap1(y + dy, size)
            sum = sum + board[idx(size, nx, ny)]
          end
        end
      end
      local i = idx(size, x, y)
      local alive = board[i]
      local out = ((alive == 1 and (sum == 2 or sum == 3)) or (alive == 0 and sum == 3)) and 1 or 0
      next_board[i] = out
      if out == 1 then
        acc = (acc + i * weight + 1) % MOD
      end
    end
  end
  return next_board, acc
end

local function gof_glider(steps, size)
  local board = {}
  for i = 1, size * size do
    board[i] = 0
  end
  add_glider(board, size, 0, 0)
  add_glider(board, size, 5, 3)
  add_glider(board, size, 1, 3)
  add_glider(board, size, 6, 4)
  local acc = 0
  for step = 0, steps - 1 do
    local frame_hash
    board, frame_hash = step_life(board, size, step + 1)
    acc = (acc + frame_hash) % MOD
  end
  return acc
end

local STEPS = 1200
local SIZE = 96
local result = gof_glider(STEPS, SIZE)
print(result)

Game of Life / Gliders / OCaml

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/ocaml/workloads/gof_glider.ml 

let mod_value = 100000007

let imod x = x mod mod_value

let wrap1 value size =
  if value < 0 then value + size else if value >= size then value - size else value

let idx size x y = x + (y * size)

let add_glider board size y x =
  board.(idx size (wrap1 (x + 1) size) (wrap1 (y + 2) size)) <- 1;
  board.(idx size (wrap1 (x + 2) size) (wrap1 (y + 2) size)) <- 1;
  board.(idx size (wrap1 (x + 3) size) (wrap1 (y + 2) size)) <- 1;
  board.(idx size (wrap1 (x + 3) size) (wrap1 (y + 1) size)) <- 1;
  board.(idx size (wrap1 (x + 2) size) (wrap1 y size)) <- 1

let step_life board size weight =
  let next = Array.make (Array.length board) 0 in
  let acc = ref weight in
  for y = 0 to size - 1 do
    for x = 0 to size - 1 do
      let sm = ref 0 in
      for dy = -1 to 1 do
        for dx = -1 to 1 do
          if dx <> 0 || dy <> 0 then (
            let nx = wrap1 (x + dx) size in
            let ny = wrap1 (y + dy) size in
            sm := !sm + board.(idx size nx ny))
        done
      done;
      let i = idx size x y in
      let alive = board.(i) in
      let out = if (alive = 1 && (!sm = 2 || !sm = 3)) || (alive = 0 && !sm = 3) then 1 else 0 in
      next.(i) <- out;
      if out = 1 then acc := imod (!acc + ((i + 1) * weight) + 1)
    done
  done;
  (next, !acc)

let gof_glider steps size =
  let board = Array.make (size * size) 0 in
  add_glider board size 0 0;
  add_glider board size 5 3;
  add_glider board size 1 3;
  add_glider board size 6 4;
  let current = ref board in
  let acc = ref 0 in
  for step = 0 to steps - 1 do
    let next, hash = step_life !current size (step + 1) in
    current := next;
    acc := imod (!acc + hash)
  done;
  !acc

let parse_int s = int_of_string s

let () =
  let steps = 1200 in
  let size = 96 in
  let result = string_of_int (gof_glider steps size) in
  print_endline result

Game of Life / Gliders / Perl

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/perl/workloads/gof_glider.pl 

use strict;
use warnings;

use constant MOD => 100000007;

sub parse_args {
    my (@argv) = @_;
    return \@argv;
}

sub wrap1 {
    my ($value, $size) = @_;
    return $value + $size if $value < 0;
    return $value - $size if $value >= $size;
    return $value;
}

sub idx {
    my ($size, $x, $y) = @_;
    return $x + $y * $size;
}

sub add_glider {
    my ($board, $size, $y, $x) = @_;
    $board->[idx($size, wrap1($x + 1, $size), wrap1($y + 2, $size))] = 1;
    $board->[idx($size, wrap1($x + 2, $size), wrap1($y + 2, $size))] = 1;
    $board->[idx($size, wrap1($x + 3, $size), wrap1($y + 2, $size))] = 1;
    $board->[idx($size, wrap1($x + 3, $size), wrap1($y + 1, $size))] = 1;
    $board->[idx($size, wrap1($x + 2, $size), wrap1($y + 0, $size))] = 1;
}

sub step_life {
    my ($board, $size, $weight) = @_;
    my @next = (0) x scalar(@$board);
    my $acc = $weight;
    for (my $y = 0; $y < $size; $y += 1) {
        for (my $x = 0; $x < $size; $x += 1) {
            my $sum = 0;
            for my $dy (-1, 0, 1) {
                for my $dx (-1, 0, 1) {
                    if ($dx != 0 || $dy != 0) {
                        my $nx = wrap1($x + $dx, $size);
                        my $ny = wrap1($y + $dy, $size);
                        $sum += $board->[idx($size, $nx, $ny)];
                    }
                }
            }
            my $i = idx($size, $x, $y);
            my $alive = $board->[$i];
            my $out = (($alive == 1 && ($sum == 2 || $sum == 3)) || ($alive == 0 && $sum == 3)) ? 1 : 0;
            $next[$i] = $out;
            if ($out == 1) {
                $acc = ($acc + ($i + 1) * $weight + 1) % MOD;
            }
        }
    }
    return (\@next, $acc);
}

sub gof_glider {
    my ($steps, $size) = @_;
    my @board = (0) x ($size * $size);
    add_glider(\@board, $size, 0, 0);
    add_glider(\@board, $size, 5, 3);
    add_glider(\@board, $size, 1, 3);
    add_glider(\@board, $size, 6, 4);
    my $acc = 0;
    for (my $step = 0; $step < $steps; $step += 1) {
        my ($next, $frame_hash) = step_life(\@board, $size, $step + 1);
        @board = @$next;
        $acc = ($acc + $frame_hash) % MOD;
    }
    return $acc;
}

my $STEPS = 1200;
my $SIZE = 96;
my $result = gof_glider(0 + $STEPS, 0 + $SIZE);
print "$result\n";

Game of Life / Gliders / PHP

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/php/workloads/gof_glider.php 

<?php

const MOD = 100000007;

function wrap1(int $value, int $size): int {
    if ($value < 0) {
        return $value + $size;
    }
    if ($value >= $size) {
        return $value - $size;
    }
    return $value;
}

function idx(int $size, int $x, int $y): int {
    return $x + $y * $size;
}

function add_glider(array &$board, int $size, int $y, int $x): void {
    $board[idx($size, wrap1($x + 1, $size), wrap1($y + 2, $size))] = 1;
    $board[idx($size, wrap1($x + 2, $size), wrap1($y + 2, $size))] = 1;
    $board[idx($size, wrap1($x + 3, $size), wrap1($y + 2, $size))] = 1;
    $board[idx($size, wrap1($x + 3, $size), wrap1($y + 1, $size))] = 1;
    $board[idx($size, wrap1($x + 2, $size), wrap1($y + 0, $size))] = 1;
}

function step_life(array $board, int $size, int $weight): array {
    $nextBoard = array_fill(0, count($board), 0);
    $acc = $weight;
    for ($y = 0; $y < $size; $y += 1) {
        for ($x = 0; $x < $size; $x += 1) {
            $sum = 0;
            for ($dy = -1; $dy <= 1; $dy += 1) {
                for ($dx = -1; $dx <= 1; $dx += 1) {
                    if ($dx !== 0 || $dy !== 0) {
                        $nx = wrap1($x + $dx, $size);
                        $ny = wrap1($y + $dy, $size);
                        $sum += $board[idx($size, $nx, $ny)];
                    }
                }
            }
            $i = idx($size, $x, $y);
            $alive = $board[$i];
            $out = (($alive === 1 && ($sum === 2 || $sum === 3)) || ($alive === 0 && $sum === 3)) ? 1 : 0;
            $nextBoard[$i] = $out;
            if ($out === 1) {
                $acc = ($acc + ($i + 1) * $weight + 1) % MOD;
            }
        }
    }
    return [$nextBoard, $acc];
}

function gof_glider(int $steps, int $size): int {
    $board = array_fill(0, $size * $size, 0);
    add_glider($board, $size, 0, 0);
    add_glider($board, $size, 5, 3);
    add_glider($board, $size, 1, 3);
    add_glider($board, $size, 6, 4);
    $acc = 0;
    for ($step = 0; $step < $steps; $step += 1) {
        [$board, $frameHash] = step_life($board, $size, $step + 1);
        $acc = ($acc + $frameHash) % MOD;
    }
    return $acc;
}

$STEPS = 1200;
$SIZE = 96;
$result = gof_glider((int) $STEPS, (int) $SIZE);
echo $result, PHP_EOL;

Game of Life / Gliders / Python

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/python/workloads/gof_glider.py 

#!/usr/bin/env python3

from __future__ import annotations

import sys


MOD = 100000007


def wrap1(value: int, size: int) -> int:
    if value < 0:
        return value + size
    if value >= size:
        return value - size
    return value

def idx(size: int, x: int, y: int) -> int:
    return x + y * size

def add_glider(board: list[int], size: int, y: int, x: int) -> None:
    board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 1, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1
    board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 2, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1
    board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1
    board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 1, size))] = 1
    board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 2, size), wrap1(y + 0, size))] = 1

def step_life(board: list[int], size: int, weight: int) -> tuple[list[int], int]:
    next_board = [0] * len(board)
    acc = weight
    for y in range(size):
        for x in range(size):
            sm = 0
            for dy in (-1, 0, 1):
                for dx in (-1, 0, 1):
                    if dx != 0 or dy != 0:
                        nx = wrap1(x + dx, size)
                        ny = wrap1(y + dy, size)
                        sm += board[idx(size, nx, ny)]
            i = idx(size, x, y)
            alive = board[i]
            out = 1 if (alive == 1 and (sm == 2 or sm == 3)) or (alive == 0 and sm == 3) else 0
            next_board[i] = out
            if out == 1:
                acc = (acc + (i + 1) * weight + 1) % MOD
    return next_board, acc

def gof_glider(steps: int, size: int) -> int:
    board = [0] * (size * size)
    add_glider(board, size, 0, 0)
    add_glider(board, size, 5, 3)
    add_glider(board, size, 1, 3)
    add_glider(board, size, 6, 4)
    acc = 0
    for step in range(steps):
        board, frame_hash = step_life(board, size, step + 1)
        acc = (acc + frame_hash) % MOD
    return acc

if __name__ == '__main__':
    steps = 1200
    size = 96
    result = gof_glider(steps, size)
    print(result)

Game of Life / Gliders / R

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/r/workloads/gof_glider.R 

#!/usr/bin/env Rscript

MOD <- 100000007

wrap1 <- function(value, size) {
  if (value < 0) return(value + size)
  if (value >= size) return(value - size)
  value
}

idx0 <- function(size, x, y) {
  x + y * size
}

add_glider <- function(board, size, y, x) {
  board[[idx0(size, wrap1(x + 1, size), wrap1(y + 2, size)) + 1]] <- 1
  board[[idx0(size, wrap1(x + 2, size), wrap1(y + 2, size)) + 1]] <- 1
  board[[idx0(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 2, size)) + 1]] <- 1
  board[[idx0(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 1, size)) + 1]] <- 1
  board[[idx0(size, wrap1(x + 2, size), wrap1(y + 0, size)) + 1]] <- 1
  board
}

step_life <- function(board, size, weight) {
  next_board <- integer(length(board))
  acc <- weight
  for (y in 0:(size - 1)) {
    for (x in 0:(size - 1)) {
      sm <- 0
      for (dy in c(-1, 0, 1)) {
        for (dx in c(-1, 0, 1)) {
          if (dx != 0 || dy != 0) {
            nx <- wrap1(x + dx, size)
            ny <- wrap1(y + dy, size)
            sm <- sm + board[[idx0(size, nx, ny) + 1]]
          }
        }
      }
      i0 <- idx0(size, x, y)
      alive <- board[[i0 + 1]]
      out <- if ((alive == 1 && (sm == 2 || sm == 3)) || (alive == 0 && sm == 3)) 1 else 0
      next_board[[i0 + 1]] <- out
      if (out == 1) {
        acc <- (acc + (i0 + 1) * weight + 1) %% MOD
      }
    }
  }
  list(board = next_board, acc = acc)
}

gof_glider <- function(steps, size) {
  board <- integer(size * size)
  board <- add_glider(board, size, 0, 0)
  board <- add_glider(board, size, 5, 3)
  board <- add_glider(board, size, 1, 3)
  board <- add_glider(board, size, 6, 4)
  acc <- 0
  for (step in 0:(steps - 1)) {
    r <- step_life(board, size, step + 1)
    board <- r$board
    acc <- (acc + r$acc) %% MOD
  }
  acc
}

args <- commandArgs(trailingOnly = TRUE)
steps <- 1200
size <- 96
result <- gof_glider(steps, size)
cat(as.integer(result), "\n", sep = "")

MOD = 100_000_007

def wrap1(value, size)
  return value + size if value < 0
  return value - size if value >= size

  value
end

def idx(size, x, y)
  x + y * size
end

def add_glider(board, size, y, x)
  board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 1, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1
  board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 2, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1
  board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1
  board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 1, size))] = 1
  board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 2, size), wrap1(y, size))] = 1
end

def step_life(board, size, weight)
  next_board = Array.new(board.length, 0)
  acc = weight
  y = 0
  while y < size
    x = 0
    while x < size
      sm = 0
      dy = -1
      while dy <= 1
        dx = -1
        while dx <= 1
          if dx != 0 || dy != 0
            nx = wrap1(x + dx, size)
            ny = wrap1(y + dy, size)
            sm += board[idx(size, nx, ny)]
          end
          dx += 1
        end
        dy += 1
      end
      i = idx(size, x, y)
      alive = board[i]
      out = ((alive == 1 && (sm == 2 || sm == 3)) || (alive == 0 && sm == 3)) ? 1 : 0
      next_board[i] = out
      acc = (acc + (i + 1) * weight + 1) % MOD if out == 1
      x += 1
    end
    y += 1
  end
  [next_board, acc]
end

  add_glider(board, size, 6, 4)

  step = 0

Game of Life / Gliders / Rust

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/rust/src/bin/gof_glider.rs 

const MOD: i32 = 100_000_007;

fn wrap1(value: i32, size: i32) -> i32 {
    if value < 0 { value + size } else if value >= size { value - size } else { value }
}

fn idx(size: i32, x: i32, y: i32) -> usize {
    (x + y * size) as usize
}

fn add_glider(board: &mut [i32], size: i32, y: i32, x: i32) {
    board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 1, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1;
    board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 2, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1;
    board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1;
    board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 1, size))] = 1;
    board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 2, size), wrap1(y, size))] = 1;
}

fn step_life(board: &[i32], size: i32, weight: i32) -> (Vec<i32>, i32) {
    let mut next = vec![0; board.len()];
    let mut acc = weight;
    for y in 0..size {
        for x in 0..size {
            let mut sm = 0;
            for dy in -1..=1 {
                for dx in -1..=1 {
                    if dx != 0 || dy != 0 {
                        let nx = wrap1(x + dx, size);
                        let ny = wrap1(y + dy, size);
                        sm += board[idx(size, nx, ny)];
                    }
                }
            }
            let i = idx(size, x, y);
            let alive = board[i];
            let out = if (alive == 1 && (sm == 2 || sm == 3)) || (alive == 0 && sm == 3) {
                1
            } else {
                0
            };
            next[i] = out;
            if out == 1 {
                acc = (acc + ((i as i32) + 1) * weight + 1) % MOD;
            }
        }
    }
    (next, acc)
}

fn gof_glider(steps: i32, size: i32) -> i32 {
    let mut board = vec![0; (size * size) as usize];
    add_glider(&mut board, size, 0, 0);
    add_glider(&mut board, size, 5, 3);
    add_glider(&mut board, size, 1, 3);
    add_glider(&mut board, size, 6, 4);
    let mut acc = 0_i32;
    for step in 0..steps {
        let (next, hash) = step_life(&board, size, step + 1);
        board = next;
        acc = (acc + hash) % MOD;
    }
    acc
}


fn main() {
    let steps = 1_200;
    let size = 96;
    let result = gof_glider(steps, size);
    println!("{}", result);
}

Game of Life / Gliders / Scala

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/scala/workloads/GofGlider.scala 

object GofGlider {
  private final val Mod = 100000007

  private def wrap1(value: Int, size: Int): Int = {
    if (value < 0) value + size
    else if (value >= size) value - size
    else value
  }

  private def idx(size: Int, x: Int, y: Int): Int = x + y * size

  private def addGlider(board: Array[Int], size: Int, y: Int, x: Int): Unit = {
    board(idx(size, wrap1(x + 1, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))) = 1
    board(idx(size, wrap1(x + 2, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))) = 1
    board(idx(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))) = 1
    board(idx(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 1, size))) = 1
    board(idx(size, wrap1(x + 2, size), wrap1(y, size))) = 1
  }

  private def gofGlider(steps: Int, size: Int): Int = {
    var board = Array.fill(size * size)(0)
    addGlider(board, size, 0, 0)
    addGlider(board, size, 5, 3)
    addGlider(board, size, 1, 3)
    addGlider(board, size, 6, 4)
    var acc = 0
    var step = 0

    while (step < steps) {
      val next = Array.fill(board.length)(0)
      var frameHash = step + 1
      var y = 0
      while (y < size) {
        var x = 0
        while (x < size) {
          var sm = 0
          var dy = -1
          while (dy <= 1) {
            var dx = -1
            while (dx <= 1) {
              if (dx != 0 || dy != 0) {
                val nx = wrap1(x + dx, size)
                val ny = wrap1(y + dy, size)
                sm += board(idx(size, nx, ny))
              }
              dx += 1
            }
            dy += 1
          }
          val i = idx(size, x, y)
          val alive = board(i)
          val out = if ((alive == 1 && (sm == 2 || sm == 3)) || (alive == 0 && sm == 3)) 1 else 0
          next(i) = out
          if (out == 1) frameHash = (frameHash + (i + 1) * (step + 1) + 1) % Mod
          x += 1
        }
        y += 1
      }
      board = next
      acc = (acc + frameHash) % Mod
      step += 1
    }
    acc
  }

  def main(args: Array[String]): Unit = {
    val steps = 1200
    val size = 96
    val result = gofGlider(steps, size)
    println(result)
  }
}

Game of Life / Gliders / Swift

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/swift/workloads/gof_glider.swift 

let mod = 100_000_007

func wrap1(_ value: Int, _ size: Int) -> Int {
    if value < 0 {
        return value + size
    }
    if value >= size {
        return value - size
    }
    return value
}

func idx(_ size: Int, _ x: Int, _ y: Int) -> Int {
    return x + y * size
}

func addGlider(_ board: inout [Int], _ size: Int, _ y: Int, _ x: Int) {
    board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 1, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1
    board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 2, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1
    board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 2, size))] = 1
    board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 3, size), wrap1(y + 1, size))] = 1
    board[idx(size, wrap1(x + 2, size), wrap1(y + 0, size))] = 1
}

func stepLife(_ board: [Int], _ size: Int, _ weight: Int) -> ([Int], Int) {
    var nextBoard = Array(repeating: 0, count: board.count)
    var acc = weight
    var y = 0
    while y < size {
        var x = 0
        while x < size {
            var sum = 0
            var dy = -1
            while dy <= 1 {
                var dx = -1
                while dx <= 1 {
                    if dx != 0 || dy != 0 {
                        let nx = wrap1(x + dx, size)
                        let ny = wrap1(y + dy, size)
                        sum += board[idx(size, nx, ny)]
                    }
                    dx += 1
                }
                dy += 1
            }
            let i = idx(size, x, y)
            let alive = board[i]
            let out = ((alive == 1 && (sum == 2 || sum == 3)) || (alive == 0 && sum == 3)) ? 1 : 0
            nextBoard[i] = out
            if out == 1 {
                acc = (acc + (i + 1) * weight + 1) % mod
            }
            x += 1
        }
        y += 1
    }
    return (nextBoard, acc)
}

func gofGlider(_ steps: Int, _ size: Int) -> Int {
    var board = Array(repeating: 0, count: size * size)
    addGlider(&board, size, 0, 0)
    addGlider(&board, size, 5, 3)
    addGlider(&board, size, 1, 3)
    addGlider(&board, size, 6, 4)
    var acc = 0
    var step = 0
    while step < steps {
        let (nextBoard, frameHash) = stepLife(board, size, step + 1)
        board = nextBoard
        acc = (acc + frameHash) % mod
        step += 1
    }
    return acc
}

let steps = 1200
let size = 96
let result = gofGlider(steps, size)
print(result)

Mandelbrot Zoom / Que (my language)

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/que/mandel.que 

(let MOD 100000007)
(let SCALE 4096)
(let CX -6072)
(let CY 0)
(let SX 6144)

(let mandel-iter (lambda cx cy max-it (do
  (mut zx 0)
  (mut zy 0)
  (mut iter 0)
  (mut mag2 0)
  (while (and (< iter max-it) (< mag2 (* 4 SCALE))) (do
    (let x2 (/ (* zx zx) SCALE))
    (let y2 (/ (* zy zy) SCALE))
    (let xy2 (/ (* (* 2 zx) zy) SCALE))
    (alter! zy (+ xy2 cy))
    (alter! zx (+ (- x2 y2) cx))
    (alter! mag2 (+ (/ (* zx zx) SCALE) (/ (* zy zy) SCALE)))
    (alter! iter (+ iter 1))))
  iter)))

(let render-frame-hash (lambda width height center-x center-y span-x span-y max-it weight (do
  (let left (- center-x span-x))
  (let right (+ center-x span-x))
  (let top (- center-y span-y))
  (let bottom (+ center-y span-y))
  (let dx (- right left))
  (let dy (- bottom top))
  (mut acc weight)
  (mut y 0)
  (while (< y height) (do
    (let cy (+ top (/ (* y dy) (- height 1))))
    (mut x 0)
    (while (< x width) (do
      (let cx (+ left (/ (* x dx) (- width 1))))
      (let it (mandel-iter cx cy max-it))
      (alter! acc (mod (+ acc (* it (+ 1 x (* y width))) 1) MOD))
      (alter! x (+ x 1))))
    (alter! y (+ y 1))))
  (mod acc MOD))))

(let FRAMES 80)
(let WIDTH 100)
(let HEIGHT 36)
(let MAX-ITER 64)

(mut center-x CX)
(mut center-y CY)
(mut span-x SX)
(mut span-y (/ (* span-x HEIGHT) WIDTH))
(mut frame 0)
(mut acc 0)
(while (< frame FRAMES) (do
  (alter! acc (mod (+ acc (render-frame-hash WIDTH HEIGHT center-x center-y span-x span-y MAX-ITER (+ frame 1))) MOD))
  (alter! span-x (/ (* span-x 97) 100))
  (alter! span-y (/ (* span-y 97) 100))
  (if (< span-x 128)
      (do
        (alter! center-x CX)
        (alter! center-y CY)
        (alter! span-x SX)
        (alter! span-y (/ (* span-x HEIGHT) WIDTH)))
      nil)
  (alter! frame (+ frame 1))))
acc

Mandelbrot Zoom / Clojure

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/clojure/workloads/mandel.clj 

(def mod-value 100000007)
(def scale 4096)
(def cx0 -6072)
(def cy0 0)
(def sx0 6144)

(defn parse-int [text]
  (Integer/parseInt text))

(defn mandel-iter [cx cy max-it]
  (loop [zx 0
         zy 0
         iter 0
         mag2 0]
    (if (or (>= iter max-it) (>= mag2 (* 4 scale)))
      iter
      (let [x2 (quot (* zx zx) scale)
            y2 (quot (* zy zy) scale)
            xy2 (quot (* 2 zx zy) scale)
            next-zy (+ xy2 cy)
            next-zx (+ (- x2 y2) cx)
            next-mag2 (+ (quot (* next-zx next-zx) scale)
                         (quot (* next-zy next-zy) scale))]
        (recur next-zx next-zy (inc iter) next-mag2)))))

(defn mandel [frames width height max-it]
  (loop [frame 0
         center-x cx0
         center-y cy0
         span-x sx0
         span-y (quot (* sx0 height) width)
         acc 0]
    (if (= frame frames)
      acc
      (let [left (- center-x span-x)
            right (+ center-x span-x)
            top (- center-y span-y)
            bottom (+ center-y span-y)
            dx (- right left)
            dy (- bottom top)
            frame-acc
            (loop [y 0
                   acc1 (inc frame)]
              (if (= y height)
                acc1
                (let [cy (+ top (quot (* y dy) (dec height)))
                      next-acc
                      (loop [x 0
                             acc2 acc1]
                        (if (= x width)
                          acc2
                          (let [cx (+ left (quot (* x dx) (dec width)))
                                it (mandel-iter cx cy max-it)]
                            (recur (inc x)
                                   (mod (+ acc2 (* it (+ x 1 (* y width))) 1) mod-value)))))]
                  (recur (inc y) next-acc))))
            next-acc (mod (+ acc frame-acc) mod-value)
            next-span-x (quot (* span-x 97) 100)
            next-span-y (quot (* span-y 97) 100)]
        (if (< next-span-x 128)
          (recur (inc frame) cx0 cy0 sx0 (quot (* sx0 height) width) next-acc)
          (recur (inc frame) center-x center-y next-span-x next-span-y next-acc))))))

(let [frames 80
      width 100
      height 36
      max-iter 64
      result (mandel frames width height max-iter)]
  (println result))

Mandelbrot Zoom / C++

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/cpp/workloads/mandel.cpp 

#include <cstdint>
#include <iostream>
#include <stdexcept>
#include <string>
#include <vector>

namespace {

constexpr int MOD = 100000007;
constexpr int SCALE = 4096;
constexpr int CX = -6072;
constexpr int CY = 0;
constexpr int SX = 6144;

int mandel_iter(int cx, int cy, int max_it) {
    int zx = 0;
    int zy = 0;
    int iteration = 0;
    int mag2 = 0;
    while (iteration < max_it && mag2 < 4 * SCALE) {
        int x2 = (zx * zx) / SCALE;
        int y2 = (zy * zy) / SCALE;
        int xy2 = (2 * zx * zy) / SCALE;
        zy = xy2 + cy;
        zx = x2 - y2 + cx;
        mag2 = (zx * zx) / SCALE + (zy * zy) / SCALE;
        ++iteration;
    }
    return iteration;
}

int mandel(int frames, int width, int height, int max_it) {
    int center_x = CX;
    int center_y = CY;
    int span_x = SX;
    int span_y = (span_x * height) / width;
    int acc = 0;
    for (int frame = 0; frame < frames; ++frame) {
        int left = center_x - span_x;
        int right = center_x + span_x;
        int top = center_y - span_y;
        int bottom = center_y + span_y;
        int dx = right - left;
        int dy = bottom - top;
        int frame_acc = frame + 1;
        for (int y = 0; y < height; ++y) {
            int cy = top + (y * dy) / (height - 1);
            for (int x = 0; x < width; ++x) {
                int cx = left + (x * dx) / (width - 1);
                int it = mandel_iter(cx, cy, max_it);
                frame_acc = (frame_acc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) % MOD;
            }
        }
        acc = (acc + frame_acc) % MOD;
        span_x = (span_x * 97) / 100;
        span_y = (span_y * 97) / 100;
        if (span_x < 128) {
            center_x = CX;
            center_y = CY;
            span_x = SX;
            span_y = (span_x * height) / width;
        }
    }
    return acc;
}

}  // namespace

int main() {
    constexpr int frames = 80;
    constexpr int width = 100;
    constexpr int height = 36;
    constexpr int max_it = 64;
    int result = mandel(frames, width, height, max_it);
    std::cout << result << '\n';
    return 0;
}

Mandelbrot Zoom / C#

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/csharp/workloads/mandel.cs 

using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;

public static class Mandel
{
    private const int Mod = 100000007;
    private const int Scale = 4096;
    private const int Cx0 = -6072;
    private const int Cy0 = 0;
    private const int Sx0 = 6144;


    private static int MandelIter(int cx, int cy, int maxIt)
    {
        var zx = 0;
        var zy = 0;
        var iteration = 0;
        var mag2 = 0;
        while (iteration < maxIt && mag2 < 4 * Scale)
        {
            var x2 = (zx * zx) / Scale;
            var y2 = (zy * zy) / Scale;
            var xy2 = (2 * zx * zy) / Scale;
            zy = xy2 + cy;
            zx = x2 - y2 + cx;
            mag2 = (zx * zx) / Scale + (zy * zy) / Scale;
            iteration += 1;
        }
        return iteration;
    }

    private static int Benchmark(int frames, int width, int height, int maxIt)
    {
        var centerX = Cx0;
        var centerY = Cy0;
        var spanX = Sx0;
        var spanY = (spanX * height) / width;
        var acc = 0;

        for (var frame = 0; frame < frames; frame += 1)
        {
            var left = centerX - spanX;
            var right = centerX + spanX;
            var top = centerY - spanY;
            var bottom = centerY + spanY;
            var dx = right - left;
            var dy = bottom - top;
            var frameAcc = frame + 1;
            for (var y = 0; y < height; y += 1)
            {
                var cy = top + (y * dy) / (height - 1);
                for (var x = 0; x < width; x += 1)
                {
                    var cx = left + (x * dx) / (width - 1);
                    var it = MandelIter(cx, cy, maxIt);
                    frameAcc = (frameAcc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) % Mod;
                }
            }
            acc = (acc + frameAcc) % Mod;
            spanX = (spanX * 97) / 100;
            spanY = (spanY * 97) / 100;
            if (spanX < 128)
            {
                centerX = Cx0;
                centerY = Cy0;
                spanX = Sx0;
                spanY = (spanX * height) / width;
            }
        }

        return acc;
    }

    public static void Main(string[] args)
    {
        const int frames = 80;
        const int width = 100;
        const int height = 36;
        const int maxIter = 64;
        var result = Benchmark(frames, width, height, maxIter);
        Console.WriteLine(result);
    }
}

Mandelbrot Zoom / Dart

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/dart/workloads/mandel.dart 

import 'dart:io';

const int modValue = 100000007;
const int scale = 4096;
const int cx0 = -6072;
const int cy0 = 0;
const int sx0 = 6144;

int idiv(int a, int b) {
  return a ~/ b;
}

int mandelIter(int px, int py, int maxIt) {
  var zx = 0;
  var zy = 0;
  var iteration = 0;
  var mag2 = 0;
  while (iteration < maxIt && mag2 < 4 * scale) {
    final x2 = idiv(zx * zx, scale);
    final y2 = idiv(zy * zy, scale);
    final xy2 = idiv(2 * zx * zy, scale);
    zy = xy2 + py;
    zx = x2 - y2 + px;
    mag2 = idiv(zx * zx, scale) + idiv(zy * zy, scale);
    iteration += 1;
  }
  return iteration;
}

int mandel(int frames, int width, int height, int maxIt) {
  var centerX = cx0;
  var centerY = cy0;
  var spanX = sx0;
  var spanY = idiv(spanX * height, width);
  var acc = 0;
  var frame = 0;
  while (frame < frames) {
    final left = centerX - spanX;
    final right = centerX + spanX;
    final top = centerY - spanY;
    final bottom = centerY + spanY;
    final dx = right - left;
    final dy = bottom - top;
    var frameAcc = frame + 1;
    var y = 0;
    while (y < height) {
      final py = top + idiv(y * dy, height - 1);
      var x = 0;
      while (x < width) {
        final px = left + idiv(x * dx, width - 1);
        final it = mandelIter(px, py, maxIt);
        frameAcc = (frameAcc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) % modValue;
        x += 1;
      }
      y += 1;
    }
    acc = (acc + frameAcc) % modValue;
    spanX = idiv(spanX * 97, 100);
    spanY = idiv(spanY * 97, 100);
    if (spanX < 128) {
      centerX = cx0;
      centerY = cy0;
      spanX = sx0;
      spanY = idiv(spanX * height, width);
    }
    frame += 1;
  }
  return acc;
}

void main(List<String> argv) {
  const frames = 80;
  const width = 100;
  const height = 36;
  const maxIter = 64;
  final result = mandel(frames, width, height, maxIter);
  stdout.writeln(result);
}

Mandelbrot Zoom / Go

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/go/workloads/mandel.go 

package main

import (
	"fmt"
)

const (
	mod   = 100000007
	scale = 4096
	cx    = -6072
	cy    = 0
	sx    = 6144
)

func mandelIter(px int, py int, maxIt int) int {
	zx := 0
	zy := 0
	iteration := 0
	mag2 := 0
	for iteration < maxIt && mag2 < 4*scale {
		x2 := (zx * zx) / scale
		y2 := (zy * zy) / scale
		xy2 := (2 * zx * zy) / scale
		zy = xy2 + py
		zx = x2 - y2 + px
		mag2 = (zx*zx)/scale + (zy*zy)/scale
		iteration++
	}
	return iteration
}

func mandel(frames int, width int, height int, maxIt int) int {
	centerX := cx
	centerY := cy
	spanX := sx
	spanY := (spanX * height) / width
	acc := 0
	for frame := 0; frame < frames; frame++ {
		left := centerX - spanX
		right := centerX + spanX
		top := centerY - spanY
		bottom := centerY + spanY
		dx := right - left
		dy := bottom - top
		frameAcc := frame + 1
		for y := 0; y < height; y++ {
			py := top + (y*dy)/(height-1)
			for x := 0; x < width; x++ {
				px := left + (x*dx)/(width-1)
				it := mandelIter(px, py, maxIt)
				frameAcc = (frameAcc + it*(x+1+y*width) + 1) % mod
			}
		}
		acc = (acc + frameAcc) % mod
		spanX = (spanX * 97) / 100
		spanY = (spanY * 97) / 100
		if spanX < 128 {
			centerX = cx
			centerY = cy
			spanX = sx
			spanY = (spanX * height) / width
		}
	}
	return acc
}


func main() {
	const frames = 80
	const width = 100
	const height = 36
	const maxIter = 64
	result := mandel(frames, width, height, maxIter)
	fmt.Println(result)
}

Mandelbrot Zoom / Haskell

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/haskell/workloads/mandel.hs 

{-# LANGUAGE BangPatterns #-}

module Main where

import Control.Monad (when)

modValue :: Int
modValue = 100000007

scale :: Int
scale = 4096

cx0 :: Int
cx0 = -6072

cy0 :: Int
cy0 = 0

sx0 :: Int
sx0 = 6144

idiv :: Int -> Int -> Int
idiv = quot

mandelIter :: Int -> Int -> Int -> Int
mandelIter px py maxIt = go 0 0 0 0
  where
    go !zx !zy !iteration !mag2
      | iteration >= maxIt || mag2 >= 4 * scale = iteration
      | otherwise =
          let x2 = idiv (zx * zx) scale
              y2 = idiv (zy * zy) scale
              xy2 = idiv (2 * zx * zy) scale
              zy' = xy2 + py
              zx' = x2 - y2 + px
              mag2' = idiv (zx' * zx') scale + idiv (zy' * zy') scale
           in go zx' zy' (iteration + 1) mag2'

mandel :: Int -> Int -> Int -> Int -> Int
mandel frames width height maxIt = frameLoop 0 cx0 cy0 sx0 spanY0 0
  where
    spanY0 = idiv (sx0 * height) width

    frameLoop !frame !centerX !centerY !spanX !spanY !acc
      | frame >= frames = acc
      | otherwise =
          let left = centerX - spanX
              right = centerX + spanX
              topV = centerY - spanY
              bottom = centerY + spanY
              dx = right - left
              dy = bottom - topV
              frameAcc = rowLoop left topV dx dy 0 (frame + 1)
              acc' = (acc + frameAcc) `mod` modValue
              spanX' = idiv (spanX * 97) 100
              spanY' = idiv (spanY * 97) 100
           in if spanX' < 128
                then frameLoop (frame + 1) cx0 cy0 sx0 spanY0 acc'
                else frameLoop (frame + 1) centerX centerY spanX' spanY' acc'

    rowLoop left topV dx dy !y !frameAcc
      | y >= height = frameAcc
      | otherwise =
          let py = topV + idiv (y * dy) (height - 1)
              frameAcc' = colLoop left py dx y 0 frameAcc
           in rowLoop left topV dx dy (y + 1) frameAcc'

    colLoop left py dx y !x !frameAcc
      | x >= width = frameAcc
      | otherwise =
          let px = left + idiv (x * dx) (width - 1)
              it = mandelIter px py maxIt
              frameAcc' = (frameAcc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) `mod` modValue
           in colLoop left py dx y (x + 1) frameAcc'

main :: IO ()
main = do
  let frames = 80
      width = 100
      height = 36
      maxIter = 64
      result = mandel frames width height maxIter
  print result

public final class Mandel {
    private static final int MOD = 100000007;
    private static final int SCALE = 4096;
    private static final int CX = -6072;
    private static final int CY = 0;
    private static final int SX = 6144;

    private Mandel() {}

    private static int mandelIter(int cx, int cy, int maxIt) {
        int zx = 0;
        int zy = 0;
        int iter = 0;
        int mag2 = 0;
        while (iter < maxIt && mag2 < 4 * SCALE) {
            final int x2 = (zx * zx) / SCALE;
            final int y2 = (zy * zy) / SCALE;
            final int xy2 = (2 * zx * zy) / SCALE;
            zy = xy2 + cy;
            zx = x2 - y2 + cx;
            mag2 = (zx * zx) / SCALE + (zy * zy) / SCALE;
            iter += 1;
        }
        return iter;
    }

    private static int mandel(int frames, int width, int height, int maxIt) {
        int centerX = CX;
        int centerY = CY;
        int spanX = SX;
        int spanY = (spanX * height) / width;
        int acc = 0;

        for (int frame = 0; frame < frames; frame += 1) {
            final int left = centerX - spanX;
            final int right = centerX + spanX;
            final int top = centerY - spanY;
            final int bottom = centerY + spanY;
            final int dx = right - left;
            final int dy = bottom - top;
            int frameAcc = frame + 1;
            for (int y = 0; y < height; y += 1) {
                final int cy = top + (y * dy) / (height - 1);
                for (int x = 0; x < width; x += 1) {
                    final int cx = left + (x * dx) / (width - 1);
                    final int it = mandelIter(cx, cy, maxIt);
                    frameAcc = (frameAcc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) % MOD;
                }
            }
            acc = (acc + frameAcc) % MOD;
            spanX = (spanX * 97) / 100;
            spanY = (spanY * 97) / 100;
            if (spanX < 128) {
                centerX = CX;
                centerY = CY;
                spanX = SX;
                spanY = (spanX * height) / width;
            }
        }
        return acc;
    }
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        final int frames = 80;
        final int width = 100;
        final int height = 36;
        final int maxIter = 64;
        final int result = mandel(frames, width, height, maxIter);
        System.out.println(result);
    }
}

Mandelbrot Zoom / JavaScript

const MOD = 100000007;
const SCALE = 4096;
const CX = -6072;
const CY = 0;
const SX = 6144;

function idiv(a, b) {
  return Math.trunc(a / b);
}

function mandelIter(cx, cy, maxIt) {
  let zx = 0;
  let zy = 0;
  let iter = 0;
  let mag2 = 0;
  while (iter < maxIt && mag2 < 4 * SCALE) {
    const x2 = idiv(zx * zx, SCALE);
    const y2 = idiv(zy * zy, SCALE);
    const xy2 = idiv(2 * zx * zy, SCALE);
    zy = xy2 + cy;
    zx = x2 - y2 + cx;
    mag2 = idiv(zx * zx, SCALE) + idiv(zy * zy, SCALE);
    iter += 1;
  }
  return iter;
}

function mandel(frames, width, height, maxIt) {
  let centerX = CX;
  let centerY = CY;
  let spanX = SX;
  let spanY = idiv(spanX * height, width);
  let acc = 0;
  for (let frame = 0; frame < frames; frame += 1) {
    const left = centerX - spanX;
    const right = centerX + spanX;
    const top = centerY - spanY;
    const bottom = centerY + spanY;
    const dx = right - left;
    const dy = bottom - top;
    let frameAcc = frame + 1;
    for (let y = 0; y < height; y += 1) {
      const cy = top + idiv(y * dy, height - 1);
      for (let x = 0; x < width; x += 1) {
        const cx = left + idiv(x * dx, width - 1);
        const it = mandelIter(cx, cy, maxIt);
        frameAcc = (frameAcc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) % MOD;
      }
    }
    acc = (acc + frameAcc) % MOD;
    spanX = idiv(spanX * 97, 100);
    spanY = idiv(spanY * 97, 100);
    if (spanX < 128) {
      centerX = CX;
      centerY = CY;
      spanX = SX;
      spanY = idiv(spanX * height, width);
    }
  }
  return acc;
}

const FRAMES = 80;
const WIDTH = 100;
const HEIGHT = 36;
const MAX_ITER = 64;
const result = mandel(FRAMES, WIDTH, HEIGHT, MAX_ITER);
process.stdout.write(`${result}

Mandelbrot Zoom / Lua

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/lua/workloads/mandel.lua 

local MOD = 100000007
local SCALE = 4096
local CX = -6072
local CY = 0
local SX = 6144

local function idiv(a, b)
  local q = a / b
  if q < 0 then
    return math.ceil(q)
  end
  return math.floor(q)
end

local function mandel_iter(cx, cy, max_it)
  local zx = 0
  local zy = 0
  local iteration = 0
  local mag2 = 0
  while iteration < max_it and mag2 < 4 * SCALE do
    local x2 = idiv(zx * zx, SCALE)
    local y2 = idiv(zy * zy, SCALE)
    local xy2 = idiv(2 * zx * zy, SCALE)
    zy = xy2 + cy
    zx = x2 - y2 + cx
    mag2 = idiv(zx * zx, SCALE) + idiv(zy * zy, SCALE)
    iteration = iteration + 1
  end
  return iteration
end

local function mandel(frames, width, height, max_it)
  local center_x = CX
  local center_y = CY
  local span_x = SX
  local span_y = idiv(span_x * height, width)
  local acc = 0
  for frame = 0, frames - 1 do
    local left = center_x - span_x
    local right = center_x + span_x
    local top = center_y - span_y
    local bottom = center_y + span_y
    local dx = right - left
    local dy = bottom - top
    local frame_acc = frame + 1
    for y = 0, height - 1 do
      local cy = top + idiv(y * dy, height - 1)
      for x = 0, width - 1 do
        local cx = left + idiv(x * dx, width - 1)
        local it = mandel_iter(cx, cy, max_it)
        frame_acc = (frame_acc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) % MOD
      end
    end
    acc = (acc + frame_acc) % MOD
    span_x = idiv(span_x * 97, 100)
    span_y = idiv(span_y * 97, 100)
    if span_x < 128 then
      center_x = CX
      center_y = CY
      span_x = SX
      span_y = idiv(span_x * height, width)
    end
  end
  return acc
end
