Mandelbrot Zoom / OCaml

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/ocaml/workloads/mandel.ml 

let mod_value = 100000007

let scale = 4096

let cx0 = -6072

let cy0 = 0

let sx0 = 6144

let imod x = x mod mod_value

let mandel_iter cx cy max_it =
  let zx = ref 0 in
  let zy = ref 0 in
  let iter = ref 0 in
  let mag2 = ref 0 in
  while !iter < max_it && !mag2 < 4 * scale do
    let x2 = (!zx * !zx) / scale in
    let y2 = (!zy * !zy) / scale in
    let xy2 = ((2 * !zx) * !zy) / scale in
    zy := xy2 + cy;
    zx := x2 - y2 + cx;
    mag2 := ((!zx * !zx) / scale) + ((!zy * !zy) / scale);
    incr iter
  done;
  !iter

let mandel frames width height max_it =
  let center_x = ref cx0 in
  let center_y = ref cy0 in
  let span_x = ref sx0 in
  let span_y = ref ((!span_x * height) / width) in
  let acc = ref 0 in
  for frame = 0 to frames - 1 do
    let left = !center_x - !span_x in
    let right = !center_x + !span_x in
    let top = !center_y - !span_y in
    let bottom = !center_y + !span_y in
    let dx = right - left in
    let dy = bottom - top in
    let frame_acc = ref (frame + 1) in
    for y = 0 to height - 1 do
      let cy = top + ((y * dy) / (height - 1)) in
      for x = 0 to width - 1 do
        let cx = left + ((x * dx) / (width - 1)) in
        let it = mandel_iter cx cy max_it in
        frame_acc := imod (!frame_acc + (it * (x + 1 + (y * width))) + 1)
      done
    done;
    acc := imod (!acc + !frame_acc);
    span_x := (!span_x * 97) / 100;
    span_y := (!span_y * 97) / 100;
    if !span_x < 128 then (
      center_x := cx0;
      center_y := cy0;
      span_x := sx0;
      span_y := (!span_x * height) / width)
  done;
  !acc

let parse_int s = int_of_string s

let () =
  let frames = 80 in
  let width = 100 in
  let height = 36 in
  let max_iter = 64 in
  let result = string_of_int (mandel frames width height max_iter) in
  print_endline result

Mandelbrot Zoom / Perl

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/perl/workloads/mandel.pl 

use strict;
use warnings;

use constant MOD => 100000007;
use constant SCALE => 4096;
use constant CX => -6072;
use constant CY => 0;
use constant SX => 6144;

sub parse_args {
    my (@argv) = @_;
    return \@argv;
}

sub idiv {
    my ($a, $b) = @_;
    my $q = $a / $b;
    return $q < 0 ? int($q + 0.0) : int($q);
}

sub mandel_iter {
    my ($cx, $cy, $max_it) = @_;
    my $zx = 0;
    my $zy = 0;
    my $iteration = 0;
    my $mag2 = 0;
    while ($iteration < $max_it && $mag2 < 4 * SCALE) {
        my $x2 = idiv($zx * $zx, SCALE);
        my $y2 = idiv($zy * $zy, SCALE);
        my $xy2 = idiv(2 * $zx * $zy, SCALE);
        $zy = $xy2 + $cy;
        $zx = $x2 - $y2 + $cx;
        $mag2 = idiv($zx * $zx, SCALE) + idiv($zy * $zy, SCALE);
        $iteration += 1;
    }
    return $iteration;
}

sub mandel {
    my ($frames, $width, $height, $max_it) = @_;
    my $center_x = CX;
    my $center_y = CY;
    my $span_x = SX;
    my $span_y = idiv($span_x * $height, $width);
    my $acc = 0;
    for (my $frame = 0; $frame < $frames; $frame += 1) {
        my $left = $center_x - $span_x;
        my $right = $center_x + $span_x;
        my $top = $center_y - $span_y;
        my $bottom = $center_y + $span_y;
        my $dx = $right - $left;
        my $dy = $bottom - $top;
        my $frame_acc = $frame + 1;
        for (my $y = 0; $y < $height; $y += 1) {
            my $cy = $top + idiv($y * $dy, $height - 1);
            for (my $x = 0; $x < $width; $x += 1) {
                my $cx = $left + idiv($x * $dx, $width - 1);
                my $it = mandel_iter($cx, $cy, $max_it);
                $frame_acc = ($frame_acc + $it * ($x + 1 + $y * $width) + 1) % MOD;
            }
        }
        $acc = ($acc + $frame_acc) % MOD;
        $span_x = idiv($span_x * 97, 100);
        $span_y = idiv($span_y * 97, 100);
        if ($span_x < 128) {
            $center_x = CX;
            $center_y = CY;
            $span_x = SX;
            $span_y = idiv($span_x * $height, $width);
        }
    }
    return $acc;
}

my $FRAMES = 80;
my $WIDTH = 100;
my $HEIGHT = 36;
my $MAX_ITER = 64;
my $result = mandel(0 + $FRAMES, 0 + $WIDTH, 0 + $HEIGHT, 0 + $MAX_ITER);
print "$result\n";

<?php

const MOD = 100000007;
const SCALE = 4096;
const CX = -6072;
const CY = 0;
const SX = 6144;

function mandel_iter(int $cx, int $cy, int $maxIt): int {
    $zx = 0;
    $zy = 0;
    $iteration = 0;
    $mag2 = 0;
    while ($iteration < $maxIt && $mag2 < 4 * SCALE) {
        $x2 = intdiv($zx * $zx, SCALE);
        $y2 = intdiv($zy * $zy, SCALE);
        $xy2 = intdiv(2 * $zx * $zy, SCALE);
        $zy = $xy2 + $cy;
        $zx = $x2 - $y2 + $cx;
        $mag2 = intdiv($zx * $zx, SCALE) + intdiv($zy * $zy, SCALE);
        $iteration += 1;
    }
    return $iteration;
}

function mandel(int $frames, int $width, int $height, int $maxIt): int {
    $centerX = CX;
    $centerY = CY;
    $spanX = SX;
    $spanY = intdiv($spanX * $height, $width);
    $acc = 0;
    for ($frame = 0; $frame < $frames; $frame += 1) {
        $left = $centerX - $spanX;
        $right = $centerX + $spanX;
        $top = $centerY - $spanY;
        $bottom = $centerY + $spanY;
        $dx = $right - $left;
        $dy = $bottom - $top;
        $frameAcc = $frame + 1;
        for ($y = 0; $y < $height; $y += 1) {
            $cy = $top + intdiv($y * $dy, $height - 1);
            for ($x = 0; $x < $width; $x += 1) {
                $cx = $left + intdiv($x * $dx, $width - 1);
                $it = mandel_iter($cx, $cy, $maxIt);
                $frameAcc = ($frameAcc + $it * ($x + 1 + $y * $width) + 1) % MOD;
            }
        }
        $acc = ($acc + $frameAcc) % MOD;
        $spanX = intdiv($spanX * 97, 100);
        $spanY = intdiv($spanY * 97, 100);
        if ($spanX < 128) {
            $centerX = CX;
            $centerY = CY;
            $spanX = SX;
            $spanY = intdiv($spanX * $height, $width);
        }
    }
    return $acc;
}

$HEIGHT = 36;
$MAX_ITER = 64;

Mandelbrot Zoom / Python

#!/usr/bin/env python3

from __future__ import annotations

import math
import sys


MOD = 100000007
SCALE = 4096
CX = -6072
CY = 0
SX = 6144


def idiv(a: int, b: int) -> int:
    return math.trunc(a / b)

def mandel_iter(cx: int, cy: int, max_it: int) -> int:
    zx = 0
    zy = 0
    iteration = 0
    mag2 = 0
    while iteration < max_it and mag2 < 4 * SCALE:
        x2 = idiv(zx * zx, SCALE)
        y2 = idiv(zy * zy, SCALE)
        xy2 = idiv(2 * zx * zy, SCALE)
        zy = xy2 + cy
        zx = x2 - y2 + cx
        mag2 = idiv(zx * zx, SCALE) + idiv(zy * zy, SCALE)
        iteration += 1
    return iteration

def mandel(frames: int, width: int, height: int, max_it: int) -> int:
    center_x = CX
    center_y = CY
    span_x = SX
    span_y = idiv(span_x * height, width)
    acc = 0
    for frame in range(frames):
        left = center_x - span_x
        right = center_x + span_x
        top = center_y - span_y
        bottom = center_y + span_y
        dx = right - left
        dy = bottom - top
        frame_acc = frame + 1
        for y in range(height):
            cy = top + idiv(y * dy, height - 1)
            for x in range(width):
                cx = left + idiv(x * dx, width - 1)
                it = mandel_iter(cx, cy, max_it)
                frame_acc = (frame_acc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) % MOD
        acc = (acc + frame_acc) % MOD
        span_x = idiv(span_x * 97, 100)
        span_y = idiv(span_y * 97, 100)
        if span_x < 128:
            center_x = CX
            center_y = CY
            span_x = SX
            span_y = idiv(span_x * height, width)
    return acc

if __name__ == '__main__':
    frames = 80
    width = 100
    height = 36
    max_iter = 64
    result = mandel(frames, width, height, max_iter)
    print(result)

#!/usr/bin/env Rscript

MOD <- 100000007
SCALE <- 4096
CX <- -6072
CY <- 0
SX <- 6144

idiv <- function(a, b) {
  trunc(a / b)
}

mandel_iter <- function(cx, cy, max_it) {
  zx <- 0
  zy <- 0
  iteration <- 0
  mag2 <- 0
  while (iteration < max_it && mag2 < 4 * SCALE) {
    x2 <- idiv(zx * zx, SCALE)
    y2 <- idiv(zy * zy, SCALE)
    xy2 <- idiv(2 * zx * zy, SCALE)
    zy <- xy2 + cy
    zx <- x2 - y2 + cx
    mag2 <- idiv(zx * zx, SCALE) + idiv(zy * zy, SCALE)
    iteration <- iteration + 1
  }
  iteration
}

mandel <- function(frames, width, height, max_it) {
  center_x <- CX
  center_y <- CY
  span_x <- SX
  span_y <- idiv(span_x * height, width)
  acc <- 0
  for (frame in 0:(frames - 1)) {
    left <- center_x - span_x
    right <- center_x + span_x
    top <- center_y - span_y
    bottom <- center_y + span_y
    dx <- right - left
    dy <- bottom - top
    frame_acc <- frame + 1
    for (y in 0:(height - 1)) {
      cy <- top + idiv(y * dy, height - 1)
      for (x in 0:(width - 1)) {
        cx <- left + idiv(x * dx, width - 1)
        it <- mandel_iter(cx, cy, max_it)
        frame_acc <- (frame_acc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) %% MOD
      }
    }
    acc <- (acc + frame_acc) %% MOD
    span_x <- idiv(span_x * 97, 100)
    span_y <- idiv(span_y * 97, 100)
    if (span_x < 128) {
      center_x <- CX
      center_y <- CY
      span_x <- SX
      span_y <- idiv(span_x * height, width)
    }
  }
  acc
}

args <- commandArgs(trailingOnly = TRUE)
frames <- 80
width <- 100
height <- 36
max_it <- 64
result <- mandel(frames, width, height, max_it)
cat(as.integer(result), "\n", sep = "")

MOD = 100_000_007
SCALE = 4096
CX = -6072
CY = 0
SX = 6144

def idiv(a, b)
  quotient = a / b
  remainder = a % b
  return quotient if remainder.zero? || (a >= 0) == (b >= 0)

  quotient + 1
end

def mandel_iter(cx, cy, max_it)
  zx = 0
  zy = 0
  iter = 0
  mag2 = 0
  while iter < max_it && mag2 < 4 * SCALE
    x2 = idiv(zx * zx, SCALE)
    y2 = idiv(zy * zy, SCALE)
    xy2 = idiv(2 * zx * zy, SCALE)
    zy = xy2 + cy
    zx = x2 - y2 + cx
    mag2 = idiv(zx * zx, SCALE) + idiv(zy * zy, SCALE)
    iter += 1
  end
  iter
end

def mandel(frames, width, height, max_it)
  center_x = CX
  center_y = CY
  span_x = SX
  span_y = idiv(span_x * height, width)
  acc = 0
  frame = 0
  while frame < frames
    left = center_x - span_x
    right = center_x + span_x
    top = center_y - span_y
    bottom = center_y + span_y
    dx = right - left
    dy = bottom - top
    frame_acc = frame + 1
    y = 0
    while y < height
      cy = top + idiv(y * dy, height - 1)
      x = 0
      while x < width
        cx = left + idiv(x * dx, width - 1)
        it = mandel_iter(cx, cy, max_it)
        frame_acc = (frame_acc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) % MOD
        x += 1
      end
      y += 1
    end
    acc = (acc + frame_acc) % MOD
    span_x = idiv(span_x * 97, 100)
    span_y = idiv(span_y * 97, 100)
    if span_x < 128
      center_x = CX
      center_y = CY
      span_x = SX
      span_y = idiv(span_x * height, width)
    end
    frame += 1
  end
  acc
end

HEIGHT = 36
MAX_ITER = 64

Mandelbrot Zoom / Rust

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/rust/src/bin/mandel.rs 

const MOD: i32 = 100_000_007;
const SCALE: i32 = 4096;
const CX: i32 = -6072;
const CY: i32 = 0;
const SX: i32 = 6144;

fn mandel_iter(cx: i32, cy: i32, max_it: i32) -> i32 {
    let mut zx = 0;
    let mut zy = 0;
    let mut iter = 0;
    let mut mag2 = 0;
    while iter < max_it && mag2 < 4 * SCALE {
        let x2 = (zx * zx) / SCALE;
        let y2 = (zy * zy) / SCALE;
        let xy2 = (2 * zx * zy) / SCALE;
        zy = xy2 + cy;
        zx = x2 - y2 + cx;
        mag2 = (zx * zx) / SCALE + (zy * zy) / SCALE;
        iter += 1;
    }
    iter
}

fn mandel(frames: i32, width: i32, height: i32, max_it: i32) -> i32 {
    let mut center_x = CX;
    let mut center_y = CY;
    let mut span_x = SX;
    let mut span_y = (span_x * height) / width;
    let mut acc = 0_i32;
    for frame in 0..frames {
        let left = center_x - span_x;
        let right = center_x + span_x;
        let top = center_y - span_y;
        let bottom = center_y + span_y;
        let dx = right - left;
        let dy = bottom - top;
        let mut frame_acc = frame + 1;
        for y in 0..height {
            let cy = top + (y * dy) / (height - 1);
            for x in 0..width {
                let cx = left + (x * dx) / (width - 1);
                let it = mandel_iter(cx, cy, max_it);
                frame_acc = (frame_acc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) % MOD;
            }
        }
        acc = (acc + frame_acc) % MOD;
        span_x = (span_x * 97) / 100;
        span_y = (span_y * 97) / 100;
        if span_x < 128 {
            center_x = CX;
            center_y = CY;
            span_x = SX;
            span_y = (span_x * height) / width;
        }
    }
    acc
}


fn main() {
    let frames = 80;
    let width = 100;
    let height = 36;
    let max_it = 64;
    let result = mandel(frames, width, height, max_it);
    println!("{}", result);
}

Mandelbrot Zoom / Scala

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/scala/workloads/Mandel.scala 

object Mandel {
  private final val Mod = 100000007
  private final val Scale = 4096
  private final val Cx = -6072
  private final val Cy = 0
  private final val Sx = 6144

  private def mandelIter(cx: Int, cy: Int, maxIt: Int): Int = {
    var zx = 0
    var zy = 0
    var iter = 0
    var mag2 = 0
    while (iter < maxIt && mag2 < 4 * Scale) {
      val x2 = (zx * zx) / Scale
      val y2 = (zy * zy) / Scale
      val xy2 = (2 * zx * zy) / Scale
      zy = xy2 + cy
      zx = x2 - y2 + cx
      mag2 = (zx * zx) / Scale + (zy * zy) / Scale
      iter += 1
    }
    iter
  }

  private def mandel(frames: Int, width: Int, height: Int, maxIt: Int): Int = {
    var centerX = Cx
    var centerY = Cy
    var spanX = Sx
    var spanY = (spanX * height) / width
    var acc = 0
    var frame = 0

    while (frame < frames) {
      val left = centerX - spanX
      val right = centerX + spanX
      val top = centerY - spanY
      val bottom = centerY + spanY
      val dx = right - left
      val dy = bottom - top
      var frameAcc = frame + 1
      var y = 0
      while (y < height) {
        val cy = top + (y * dy) / (height - 1)
        var x = 0
        while (x < width) {
          val cx = left + (x * dx) / (width - 1)
          val it = mandelIter(cx, cy, maxIt)
          frameAcc = (frameAcc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) % Mod
          x += 1
        }
        y += 1
      }
      acc = (acc + frameAcc) % Mod
      spanX = (spanX * 97) / 100
      spanY = (spanY * 97) / 100
      if (spanX < 128) {
        centerX = Cx
        centerY = Cy
        spanX = Sx
        spanY = (spanX * height) / width
      }
      frame += 1
    }
    acc
  }

  def main(args: Array[String]): Unit = {
    val frames = 80
    val width = 100
    val height = 36
    val maxIter = 64
    val result = mandel(frames, width, height, maxIter)
    println(result)
  }
}

func mandelIter(_ cx: Int, _ cy: Int, _ maxIt: Int) -> Int {
    var zx = 0
    var zy = 0

        let y2 = (zy * zy) / scale

        zy = xy2 + cy
        zx = x2 - y2 + cx
        mag2 = (zx * zx) / scale + (zy * zy) / scale
        iteration += 1
    }
    return iteration
}

func mandel(_ frames: Int, _ width: Int, _ height: Int, _ maxIt: Int) -> Int {

    var centerY = cy0

            let cy = top + (y * dy) / (height - 1)
            var x = 0
            while x < width {
                let cx = left + (x * dx) / (width - 1)

                frameAcc = (frameAcc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) % mod
                x += 1

            y += 1

        spanX = (spanX * 97) / 100
        spanY = (spanY * 97) / 100
        if spanX < 128 {
            centerX = cx0
            centerY = cy0
            spanX = sx0
            spanY = (spanX * height) / width
        }
        frame += 1
    }
    return acc

Mandelbrot Zoom / Decimal / Python

#!/usr/bin/env python3

from __future__ import annotations

MOD = 100000007
CX = -1.482421875
CY = 0.0
SX = 1.5


def mandel_iter(cx: float, cy: float, max_it: int) -> int:
    zx = 0.0
    zy = 0.0
    iteration = 0
    mag2 = 0.0
    while iteration < max_it and mag2 < 4.0:
        x2 = zx * zx
        y2 = zy * zy
        xy2 = 2.0 * zx * zy
        zy = xy2 + cy
        zx = x2 - y2 + cx
        mag2 = zx * zx + zy * zy
        iteration += 1
    return iteration


def mandel(frames: int, width: int, height: int, max_it: int) -> int:
    center_x = CX
    center_y = CY
    span_x = SX
    span_y = (span_x * height) / width
    acc = 0
    for frame in range(frames):
        left = center_x - span_x
        right = center_x + span_x
        top = center_y - span_y
        bottom = center_y + span_y
        dx = right - left
        dy = bottom - top
        frame_acc = frame + 1
        for y in range(height):
            cy = top + (y * dy) / (height - 1)
            for x in range(width):
                cx = left + (x * dx) / (width - 1)
                it = mandel_iter(cx, cy, max_it)
                frame_acc = (frame_acc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) % MOD
        acc = (acc + frame_acc) % MOD
        span_x = (span_x * 97.0) / 100.0
        span_y = (span_y * 97.0) / 100.0
        if span_x < 0.03125:
            center_x = CX
            center_y = CY
            span_x = SX
            span_y = (span_x * height) / width
    return acc


if __name__ == '__main__':
    frames = 80
    width = 100
    height = 36
    max_iter = 64
    result = mandel(frames, width, height, max_iter)
    print(result)

(def mod-value 100000007)
(def cx0 -1.482421875)
(def cy0 0.0)
(def sx0 1.5)

(defn mandel-iter [cx cy max-it]
  (loop [zx 0.0
         zy 0.0
         iter 0
         mag2 0.0]
    (if (or (>= iter max-it) (>= mag2 4.0))
      iter
      (let [x2 (* zx zx)
            y2 (* zy zy)
            xy2 (* 2.0 zx zy)
            next-zy (+ xy2 cy)
            next-zx (+ (- x2 y2) cx)
            next-mag2 (+ (* next-zx next-zx) (* next-zy next-zy))]
        (recur next-zx next-zy (inc iter) next-mag2)))))

(defn mandel [frames width height max-it]
  (loop [frame 0
         center-x cx0
         center-y cy0
         span-x sx0
         span-y (/ (* sx0 height) width)
         acc 0]
    (if (= frame frames)
      acc
      (let [left (- center-x span-x)
            right (+ center-x span-x)
            top (- center-y span-y)
            bottom (+ center-y span-y)
            dx (- right left)
            dy (- bottom top)
            frame-acc
            (loop [y 0
                   acc1 (inc frame)]
              (if (= y height)
                acc1
                (let [cy (+ top (/ (* y dy) (dec height)))
                      next-acc
                      (loop [x 0
                             acc2 acc1]
                        (if (= x width)
                          acc2
                          (let [cx (+ left (/ (* x dx) (dec width)))
                                it (mandel-iter cx cy max-it)]
                            (recur (inc x)
                                   (mod (+ acc2 (* it (+ x 1 (* y width))) 1) mod-value)))))]
                  (recur (inc y) next-acc))))
            next-acc (mod (+ acc frame-acc) mod-value)
            next-span-x (/ (* span-x 97.0) 100.0)
            next-span-y (/ (* span-y 97.0) 100.0)]
        (if (< next-span-x 0.03125)
          (recur (inc frame) cx0 cy0 sx0 (/ (* sx0 height) width) next-acc)
          (recur (inc frame) center-x center-y next-span-x next-span-y next-acc))))))

(let [frames 80
      width 100
      height 36
      max-iter 64
      result (mandel frames width height max-iter)]
  (println result))

Mandelbrot Zoom / Decimal / C++

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/cpp/workloads/mandel_dec.cpp 

#include <iostream>

namespace {

constexpr int MOD = 100000007;
constexpr double CX = -1.482421875;
constexpr double CY = 0.0;
constexpr double SX = 1.5;

int mandel_iter(double cx, double cy, int max_it) {
    double zx = 0.0;
    double zy = 0.0;
    int iteration = 0;
    double mag2 = 0.0;
    while (iteration < max_it && mag2 < 4.0) {
        const double x2 = zx * zx;
        const double y2 = zy * zy;
        const double xy2 = 2.0 * zx * zy;
        zy = xy2 + cy;
        zx = x2 - y2 + cx;
        mag2 = zx * zx + zy * zy;
        ++iteration;
    }
    return iteration;
}

int mandel(int frames, int width, int height, int max_it) {
    double center_x = CX;
    double center_y = CY;
    double span_x = SX;
    double span_y = (span_x * static_cast<double>(height)) / static_cast<double>(width);
    int acc = 0;
    for (int frame = 0; frame < frames; ++frame) {
        const double left = center_x - span_x;
        const double right = center_x + span_x;
        const double top = center_y - span_y;
        const double bottom = center_y + span_y;
        const double dx = right - left;
        const double dy = bottom - top;
        int frame_acc = frame + 1;
        for (int y = 0; y < height; ++y) {
            const double cy = top + (static_cast<double>(y) * dy) / static_cast<double>(height - 1);
            for (int x = 0; x < width; ++x) {
                const double cx = left + (static_cast<double>(x) * dx) / static_cast<double>(width - 1);
                const int it = mandel_iter(cx, cy, max_it);
                frame_acc = (frame_acc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) % MOD;
            }
        }
        acc = (acc + frame_acc) % MOD;
        span_x = (span_x * 97.0) / 100.0;
        span_y = (span_y * 97.0) / 100.0;
        if (span_x < 0.03125) {
            center_x = CX;
            center_y = CY;
            span_x = SX;
            span_y = (span_x * static_cast<double>(height)) / static_cast<double>(width);
        }
    }
    return acc;
}

}  // namespace

int main() {
    constexpr int frames = 80;
    constexpr int width = 100;
    constexpr int height = 36;
    constexpr int max_it = 64;
    int result = mandel(frames, width, height, max_it);
    std::cout << result << '\n';
    return 0;
}

Mandelbrot Zoom / Decimal / C#

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/csharp/workloads/mandel_dec.cs 

using System;

public static class MandelDec
{
    private const int Mod = 100000007;
    private const double Cx0 = -1.482421875;
    private const double Cy0 = 0.0;
    private const double Sx0 = 1.5;

    private static int MandelIter(double cx, double cy, int maxIter)
    {
        var zx = 0.0;
        var zy = 0.0;
        var iter = 0;
        var mag2 = 0.0;
        while (iter < maxIter && mag2 < 4.0)
        {
            var x2 = zx * zx;
            var y2 = zy * zy;
            var xy2 = 2.0 * zx * zy;
            zy = xy2 + cy;
            zx = x2 - y2 + cx;
            mag2 = zx * zx + zy * zy;
            iter += 1;
        }
        return iter;
    }

    private static int Benchmark(int frames, int width, int height, int maxIter)
    {
        var centerX = Cx0;
        var centerY = Cy0;
        var spanX = Sx0;
        var spanY = (spanX * height) / width;
        var acc = 0;
        for (var frame = 0; frame < frames; frame += 1)
        {
            var left = centerX - spanX;
            var right = centerX + spanX;
            var top = centerY - spanY;
            var bottom = centerY + spanY;
            var dx = right - left;
            var dy = bottom - top;
            var frameAcc = frame + 1;
            for (var y = 0; y < height; y += 1)
            {
                var cy = top + (y * dy) / (height - 1);
                for (var x = 0; x < width; x += 1)
                {
                    var cx = left + (x * dx) / (width - 1);
                    var it = MandelIter(cx, cy, maxIter);
                    frameAcc = (frameAcc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) % Mod;
                }
            }
            acc = (acc + frameAcc) % Mod;
            spanX = (spanX * 97.0) / 100.0;
            spanY = (spanY * 97.0) / 100.0;
            if (spanX < 0.03125)
            {
                centerX = Cx0;
                centerY = Cy0;
                spanX = Sx0;
                spanY = (spanX * height) / width;
            }
        }
        return acc;
    }

    public static void Main(string[] args)
    {
        const int frames = 80;
        const int width = 100;
        const int height = 36;
        const int maxIter = 64;
        var result = Benchmark(frames, width, height, maxIter);
        Console.WriteLine(result);
    }
}

import 'dart:io';

const modValue = 100000007;
const cx0 = -1.482421875;
const cy0 = 0.0;
const sx0 = 1.5;

int mandelIter(double cx, double cy, int maxIter) {
  var zx = 0.0;
  var zy = 0.0;
  var iter = 0;
  var mag2 = 0.0;
  while (iter < maxIter && mag2 < 4.0) {
    final x2 = zx * zx;
    final y2 = zy * zy;
    final xy2 = 2.0 * zx * zy;
    zy = xy2 + cy;
    zx = x2 - y2 + cx;
    mag2 = zx * zx + zy * zy;
    iter += 1;
  }
  return iter;
}

int mandel(int frames, int width, int height, int maxIter) {
  var centerX = cx0;
  var centerY = cy0;
  var spanX = sx0;
  var spanY = (spanX * height) / width;
  var acc = 0;
  for (var frame = 0; frame < frames; frame += 1) {
    final left = centerX - spanX;
    final right = centerX + spanX;
    final top = centerY - spanY;
    final bottom = centerY + spanY;
    final dx = right - left;
    final dy = bottom - top;
    var frameAcc = frame + 1;
    for (var y = 0; y < height; y += 1) {
      final cy = top + (y * dy) / (height - 1);
      for (var x = 0; x < width; x += 1) {
        final cx = left + (x * dx) / (width - 1);
        final it = mandelIter(cx, cy, maxIter);
        frameAcc = (frameAcc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) % modValue;
      }
    }
    acc = (acc + frameAcc) % modValue;
    spanX = (spanX * 97.0) / 100.0;
    spanY = (spanY * 97.0) / 100.0;
    if (spanX < 0.03125) {
      centerX = cx0;
      centerY = cy0;
      spanX = sx0;
      spanY = (spanX * height) / width;
    }
  }
  return acc;
}

void main(List<String> argv) {
  const frames = 80;
  const width = 100;
  const height = 36;
  const maxIter = 64;
  final result = mandel(frames, width, height, maxIter);
  stdout.writeln(result);
}

Mandelbrot Zoom / Decimal / Go

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/go/workloads/mandel_dec.go 

package main

import "fmt"

const (
	mod = 100000007
	cx  = -1.482421875
	cy  = 0.0
	sx  = 1.5
)

func mandelIter(px float64, py float64, maxIt int) int {
	zx := 0.0
	zy := 0.0
	iteration := 0
	mag2 := 0.0
	for iteration < maxIt && mag2 < 4.0 {
		x2 := zx * zx
		y2 := zy * zy
		xy2 := 2.0 * zx * zy
		zy = xy2 + py
		zx = x2 - y2 + px
		mag2 = zx*zx + zy*zy
		iteration++
	}
	return iteration
}

func mandel(frames int, width int, height int, maxIt int) int {
	centerX := cx
	centerY := cy
	spanX := sx
	spanY := (spanX * float64(height)) / float64(width)
	acc := 0
	for frame := 0; frame < frames; frame++ {
		left := centerX - spanX
		right := centerX + spanX
		top := centerY - spanY
		bottom := centerY + spanY
		dx := right - left
		dy := bottom - top
		frameAcc := frame + 1
		for y := 0; y < height; y++ {
			py := top + (float64(y)*dy)/float64(height-1)
			for x := 0; x < width; x++ {
				px := left + (float64(x)*dx)/float64(width-1)
				it := mandelIter(px, py, maxIt)
				frameAcc = (frameAcc + it*(x+1+y*width) + 1) % mod
			}
		}
		acc = (acc + frameAcc) % mod
		spanX = (spanX * 97.0) / 100.0
		spanY = (spanY * 97.0) / 100.0
		if spanX < 0.03125 {
			centerX = cx
			centerY = cy
			spanX = sx
			spanY = (spanX * float64(height)) / float64(width)
		}
	}
	return acc
}

func main() {
	const frames = 80
	const width = 100
	const height = 36
	const maxIter = 64
	result := mandel(frames, width, height, maxIter)
	fmt.Println(result)
}

Mandelbrot Zoom / Decimal / Haskell

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/haskell/workloads/mandel_dec.hs 

modValue :: Int
modValue = 100000007

cx0 :: Double
cx0 = -1.482421875

cy0 :: Double
cy0 = 0.0

sx0 :: Double
sx0 = 1.5

mandelIter :: Double -> Double -> Int -> Int
mandelIter cx cy maxIt = go 0.0 0.0 0 0.0
  where
    go zx zy iter mag2
      | iter >= maxIt || mag2 >= 4.0 = iter
      | otherwise =
          let x2 = zx * zx
              y2 = zy * zy
              xy2 = 2.0 * zx * zy
              nextZy = xy2 + cy
              nextZx = x2 - y2 + cx
              nextMag2 = nextZx * nextZx + nextZy * nextZy
           in go nextZx nextZy (iter + 1) nextMag2

mandel :: Int -> Int -> Int -> Int -> Int
mandel frames width height maxIt = go 0 cx0 cy0 sx0 ((sx0 * fromIntegral height) / fromIntegral width) 0
  where
    go frame centerX centerY spanX spanY acc
      | frame >= frames = acc
      | otherwise =
          let left = centerX - spanX
              right = centerX + spanX
              top = centerY - spanY
              bottom = centerY + spanY
              dx = right - left
              dy = bottom - top
              frameAcc = rowLoop left top dx dy frame 0 (frame + 1)
              acc' = (acc + frameAcc) `mod` modValue
              nextSpanX = (spanX * 97.0) / 100.0
              nextSpanY = (spanY * 97.0) / 100.0
           in if nextSpanX < 0.03125
                then go (frame + 1) cx0 cy0 sx0 ((sx0 * fromIntegral height) / fromIntegral width) acc'
                else go (frame + 1) centerX centerY nextSpanX nextSpanY acc'
    rowLoop left top dx dy frame y frameAcc
      | y >= height = frameAcc
      | otherwise =
          let py = top + (fromIntegral y * dy) / fromIntegral (height - 1)
              frameAcc' = colLoop left py dx y 0 frameAcc
           in rowLoop left top dx dy frame (y + 1) frameAcc'
    colLoop left py dx y x frameAcc
      | x >= width = frameAcc
      | otherwise =
          let px = left + (fromIntegral x * dx) / fromIntegral (width - 1)
              it = mandelIter px py maxIt
              frameAcc' = (frameAcc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) `mod` modValue
           in colLoop left py dx y (x + 1) frameAcc'

main :: IO ()
main = do
  let frames = 80
      width = 100
      height = 36
      maxIter = 64
      result = mandel frames width height maxIter
  print result

public final class MandelDec {
    private static final int MOD = 100000007;
    private static final double CX = -1.482421875;
    private static final double CY = 0.0;
    private static final double SX = 1.5;

    private MandelDec() {}

    private static int mandelIter(double cx, double cy, int maxIter) {
        double zx = 0.0;
        double zy = 0.0;
        int iter = 0;
        double mag2 = 0.0;
        while (iter < maxIter && mag2 < 4.0) {
            double x2 = zx * zx;
            double y2 = zy * zy;
            double xy2 = 2.0 * zx * zy;
            zy = xy2 + cy;
            zx = x2 - y2 + cx;
            mag2 = zx * zx + zy * zy;
            iter += 1;
        }
        return iter;
    }

    private static int mandel(int frames, int width, int height, int maxIter) {
        double centerX = CX;
        double centerY = CY;
        double spanX = SX;
        double spanY = (spanX * height) / width;
        int acc = 0;
        for (int frame = 0; frame < frames; frame += 1) {
            double left = centerX - spanX;
            double right = centerX + spanX;
            double top = centerY - spanY;
            double bottom = centerY + spanY;
            double dx = right - left;
            double dy = bottom - top;
            int frameAcc = frame + 1;
            for (int y = 0; y < height; y += 1) {
                double cy = top + (y * dy) / (height - 1);
                for (int x = 0; x < width; x += 1) {
                    double cx = left + (x * dx) / (width - 1);
                    int it = mandelIter(cx, cy, maxIter);
                    frameAcc = (frameAcc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) % MOD;
                }
            }
            acc = (acc + frameAcc) % MOD;
            spanX = (spanX * 97.0) / 100.0;
            spanY = (spanY * 97.0) / 100.0;
            if (spanX < 0.03125) {
                centerX = CX;
                centerY = CY;
                spanX = SX;
                spanY = (spanX * height) / width;
            }
        }
        return acc;
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        final int frames = 80;
        final int width = 100;
        final int height = 36;
        final int maxIter = 64;
        final int result = mandel(frames, width, height, maxIter);
        System.out.println(result);
    }
}

const MOD = 100000007;
const CX = -1.482421875;
const CY = 0.0;
const SX = 1.5;

function mandelIter(cx, cy, maxIt) {
  let zx = 0.0;
  let zy = 0.0;
  let iter = 0;
  let mag2 = 0.0;
  while (iter < maxIt && mag2 < 4.0) {
    const x2 = zx * zx;
    const y2 = zy * zy;
    const xy2 = 2.0 * zx * zy;
    zy = xy2 + cy;
    zx = x2 - y2 + cx;
    mag2 = zx * zx + zy * zy;
    iter += 1;
  }
  return iter;
}

function mandel(frames, width, height, maxIt) {
  let centerX = CX;
  let centerY = CY;
  let spanX = SX;
  let spanY = (spanX * height) / width;
  let acc = 0;
  for (let frame = 0; frame < frames; frame += 1) {
    const left = centerX - spanX;
    const right = centerX + spanX;
    const top = centerY - spanY;
    const bottom = centerY + spanY;
    const dx = right - left;
    const dy = bottom - top;
    let frameAcc = frame + 1;
    for (let y = 0; y < height; y += 1) {
      const cy = top + (y * dy) / (height - 1);
      for (let x = 0; x < width; x += 1) {
        const cx = left + (x * dx) / (width - 1);
        const it = mandelIter(cx, cy, maxIt);
        frameAcc = (frameAcc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) % MOD;
      }
    }
    acc = (acc + frameAcc) % MOD;
    spanX = (spanX * 97.0) / 100.0;
    spanY = (spanY * 97.0) / 100.0;
    if (spanX < 0.03125) {
      centerX = CX;
      centerY = CY;
      spanX = SX;
      spanY = (spanX * height) / width;
    }
  }
  return acc;
}

local function mandel_iter(cx, cy, max_it)
  local zx = 0.0
  local zy = 0.0
  local iteration = 0
  local mag2 = 0.0
  while iteration < max_it and mag2 < 4.0 do
    local x2 = zx * zx
    local y2 = zy * zy
    local xy2 = 2.0 * zx * zy
    zy = xy2 + cy
    zx = x2 - y2 + cx
    mag2 = zx * zx + zy * zy
    iteration = iteration + 1
  end
  return iteration
end

local function mandel(frames, width, height, max_it)
  local center_x = CX
  local center_y = CY
  local span_x = SX
  local span_y = (span_x * height) / width
  local acc = 0
  for frame = 0, frames - 1 do
    local left = center_x - span_x
    local right = center_x + span_x
    local top = center_y - span_y
    local bottom = center_y + span_y
    local dx = right - left
    local dy = bottom - top
    local frame_acc = frame + 1
    for y = 0, height - 1 do
      local cy = top + (y * dy) / (height - 1)
      for x = 0, width - 1 do
        local cx = left + (x * dx) / (width - 1)
        local it = mandel_iter(cx, cy, max_it)
        frame_acc = (frame_acc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) % MOD
      end
    end
    acc = (acc + frame_acc) % MOD
    span_x = (span_x * 97.0) / 100.0
    span_y = (span_y * 97.0) / 100.0
    if span_x < 0.03125 then
      center_x = CX
      center_y = CY
      span_x = SX
      span_y = (span_x * height) / width
    end
  end
  return acc
end

Mandelbrot Zoom / Decimal / OCaml

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/ocaml/workloads/mandel_dec.ml 

let mod_value = 100000007
let cx0 = -1.482421875
let cy0 = 0.0
let sx0 = 1.5

let mandel_iter cx cy max_it =
  let zx = ref 0.0 in
  let zy = ref 0.0 in
  let iteration = ref 0 in
  let mag2 = ref 0.0 in
  while !iteration < max_it && !mag2 < 4.0 do
    let x2 = !zx *. !zx in
    let y2 = !zy *. !zy in
    let xy2 = 2.0 *. !zx *. !zy in
    zy := xy2 +. cy;
    zx := x2 -. y2 +. cx;
    mag2 := (!zx *. !zx) +. (!zy *. !zy);
    incr iteration
  done;
  !iteration

let mandel frames width height max_it =
  let center_x = ref cx0 in
  let center_y = ref cy0 in
  let span_x = ref sx0 in
  let span_y = ref ((!span_x *. float_of_int height) /. float_of_int width) in
  let acc = ref 0 in
  for frame = 0 to frames - 1 do
    let left = !center_x -. !span_x in
    let right = !center_x +. !span_x in
    let top = !center_y -. !span_y in
    let bottom = !center_y +. !span_y in
    let dx = right -. left in
    let dy = bottom -. top in
    let frame_acc = ref (frame + 1) in
    for y = 0 to height - 1 do
      let cy = top +. ((float_of_int y *. dy) /. float_of_int (height - 1)) in
      for x = 0 to width - 1 do
        let cx = left +. ((float_of_int x *. dx) /. float_of_int (width - 1)) in
        let it = mandel_iter cx cy max_it in
        frame_acc := (!frame_acc + (it * (x + 1 + (y * width))) + 1) mod mod_value
      done
    done;
    acc := (!acc + !frame_acc) mod mod_value;
    span_x := (!span_x *. 97.0) /. 100.0;
    span_y := (!span_y *. 97.0) /. 100.0;
    if !span_x < 0.03125 then (
      center_x := cx0;
      center_y := cy0;
      span_x := sx0;
      span_y := (!span_x *. float_of_int height) /. float_of_int width
    )
  done;
  !acc

let () =
  let frames = 80 in
  let width = 100 in
  let height = 36 in
  let max_iter = 64 in
  let result = string_of_int (mandel frames width height max_iter) in
  print_endline result

Mandelbrot Zoom / Decimal / Perl

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/perl/workloads/mandel_dec.pl 

use strict;
use warnings;

use constant MOD => 100000007;
use constant CX => -1.482421875;
use constant CY => 0.0;
use constant SX => 1.5;

sub mandel_iter {
    my ($cx, $cy, $max_it) = @_;
    my $zx = 0.0;
    my $zy = 0.0;
    my $iter = 0;
    my $mag2 = 0.0;
    while ($iter < $max_it && $mag2 < 4.0) {
        my $x2 = $zx * $zx;
        my $y2 = $zy * $zy;
        my $xy2 = 2.0 * $zx * $zy;
        $zy = $xy2 + $cy;
        $zx = $x2 - $y2 + $cx;
        $mag2 = $zx * $zx + $zy * $zy;
        $iter += 1;
    }
    return $iter;
}

sub mandel {
    my ($frames, $width, $height, $max_it) = @_;
    my $center_x = CX;
    my $center_y = CY;
    my $span_x = SX;
    my $span_y = ($span_x * $height) / $width;
    my $acc = 0;
    for (my $frame = 0; $frame < $frames; $frame += 1) {
        my $left = $center_x - $span_x;
        my $right = $center_x + $span_x;
        my $top = $center_y - $span_y;
        my $bottom = $center_y + $span_y;
        my $dx = $right - $left;
        my $dy = $bottom - $top;
        my $frame_acc = $frame + 1;
        for (my $y = 0; $y < $height; $y += 1) {
            my $cy = $top + ($y * $dy) / ($height - 1);
            for (my $x = 0; $x < $width; $x += 1) {
                my $cx = $left + ($x * $dx) / ($width - 1);
                my $it = mandel_iter($cx, $cy, $max_it);
                $frame_acc = ($frame_acc + $it * ($x + 1 + $y * $width) + 1) % MOD;
            }
        }
        $acc = ($acc + $frame_acc) % MOD;
        $span_x = ($span_x * 97.0) / 100.0;
        $span_y = ($span_y * 97.0) / 100.0;
        if ($span_x < 0.03125) {
            $center_x = CX;
            $center_y = CY;
            $span_x = SX;
            $span_y = ($span_x * $height) / $width;
        }
    }
    return $acc;
}

my $FRAMES = 80;
my $WIDTH = 100;
my $HEIGHT = 36;
my $MAX_ITER = 64;
my $result = mandel($FRAMES, $WIDTH, $HEIGHT, $MAX_ITER);
print "$result\n";

<?php

const MOD = 100000007;
const CX = -1.482421875;
const CY = 0.0;
const SX = 1.5;

function mandel_iter(float $cx, float $cy, int $max_it): int {
    $zx = 0.0;
    $zy = 0.0;
    $iter = 0;
    $mag2 = 0.0;
    while ($iter < $max_it && $mag2 < 4.0) {
        $x2 = $zx * $zx;
        $y2 = $zy * $zy;
        $xy2 = 2.0 * $zx * $zy;
        $zy = $xy2 + $cy;
        $zx = $x2 - $y2 + $cx;
        $mag2 = $zx * $zx + $zy * $zy;
        $iter += 1;
    }
    return $iter;
}

function mandel(int $frames, int $width, int $height, int $max_it): int {
    $centerX = CX;
    $centerY = CY;
    $spanX = SX;
    $spanY = ($spanX * $height) / $width;
    $acc = 0;
    for ($frame = 0; $frame < $frames; $frame += 1) {
        $left = $centerX - $spanX;
        $right = $centerX + $spanX;
        $top = $centerY - $spanY;
        $bottom = $centerY + $spanY;
        $dx = $right - $left;
        $dy = $bottom - $top;
        $frameAcc = $frame + 1;
        for ($y = 0; $y < $height; $y += 1) {
            $cy = $top + ($y * $dy) / ($height - 1);
            for ($x = 0; $x < $width; $x += 1) {
                $cx = $left + ($x * $dx) / ($width - 1);
                $it = mandel_iter($cx, $cy, $max_it);
                $frameAcc = ($frameAcc + $it * ($x + 1 + $y * $width) + 1) % MOD;
            }
        }
        $acc = ($acc + $frameAcc) % MOD;
        $spanX = ($spanX * 97.0) / 100.0;
        $spanY = ($spanY * 97.0) / 100.0;
        if ($spanX < 0.03125) {
            $centerX = CX;
            $centerY = CY;
            $spanX = SX;
            $spanY = ($spanX * $height) / $width;
        }
    }
    return $acc;
}

$HEIGHT = 36;
$MAX_ITER = 64;

Mandelbrot Zoom / Decimal / Que (my language)

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/que/mandel-dec.que 


  (let MOD 100000007)

  (let CX -1.482421875)
  (let CY 0.0)
  (let SX 1.5)

  (let mandel-iter
    (lambda cx cy max-it
      (do
        (mut zx 0.0)
        (mut zy 0.0)
        (mut iter 0)
        (mut mag2 0.0)
        (while (and (< iter max-it) (<. mag2 4.0)) (do
          (let x2 (*. zx zx))
          (let y2 (*. zy zy))
          (let xy2 (*. 2.0 (*. zx zy)))
          (alter! zy (+. xy2 cy))
          (alter! zx (+. (-. x2 y2) cx))
          (alter! mag2 (+. (*. zx zx) (*. zy zy)))
          (alter! iter (+ iter 1))))
        iter)))

  (let render-frame-hash
    (lambda width height center-x center-y span-x span-y max-it weight
      (do
        (let left (-. center-x span-x))
        (let right (+. center-x span-x))
        (let top (-. center-y span-y))
        (let bottom (+. center-y span-y))
        (let dx (-. right left))
        (let dy (-. bottom top))
        (let width-1 (Int->Dec (- width 1)))
        (let height-1 (Int->Dec (- height 1)))
        (mut acc weight)
        (mut y 0)
        (while (< y height) (do
          (let cy (+. top (/. (*. (Int->Dec y) dy) height-1)))
          (mut x 0)
          (while (< x width) (do
            (let cx (+. left (/. (*. (Int->Dec x) dx) width-1)))
            (let it (mandel-iter cx cy max-it))
            (alter! acc (mod (+ acc (* it (+ 1 x (* y width))) 1) MOD))
            (alter! x (+ x 1))))
          (alter! y (+ y 1))))
        (mod acc MOD))))

  (let FRAMES 80)
  (let WIDTH 100)
  (let HEIGHT 36)
  (let WIDTHD (Int->Dec WIDTH))
  (let HEIGHTD (Int->Dec HEIGHT))
  (let MAX-ITER 64)

  (mut center-x CX)
  (mut center-y CY)
  (mut span-x SX)
  (mut span-y (/. (*. span-x HEIGHTD) WIDTHD))
  (mut frame 0)
  (mut acc 0)
 
  (while (< frame FRAMES) (do
    (alter! acc
      (mod
        (+ acc
           (render-frame-hash
             WIDTH HEIGHT center-x center-y span-x span-y MAX-ITER (+ frame 1)))
        MOD))
    (alter! span-x (/. (*. span-x 97.0) 100.0))
    (alter! span-y (/. (*. span-y 97.0) 100.0))
    (if (<. span-x 0.03125)
        (do
          (alter! center-x CX)
          (alter! center-y CY)
          (alter! span-x SX)
          (alter! span-y (/. (*. span-x HEIGHTD) WIDTHD)))
        nil)
    (alter! frame (+ frame 1))))

  acc

Mandelbrot Zoom / Decimal / R

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/r/workloads/mandel_dec.R 

#!/usr/bin/env Rscript

MOD <- 100000007
CX <- -1.482421875
CY <- 0.0
SX <- 1.5

mandel_iter <- function(cx, cy, max_it) {
  zx <- 0.0
  zy <- 0.0
  iteration <- 0
  mag2 <- 0.0
  while (iteration < max_it && mag2 < 4.0) {
    x2 <- zx * zx
    y2 <- zy * zy
    xy2 <- 2.0 * zx * zy
    zy <- xy2 + cy
    zx <- x2 - y2 + cx
    mag2 <- zx * zx + zy * zy
    iteration <- iteration + 1
  }
  iteration
}

mandel <- function(frames, width, height, max_it) {
  center_x <- CX
  center_y <- CY
  span_x <- SX
  span_y <- (span_x * height) / width
  acc <- 0
  for (frame in 0:(frames - 1)) {
    left <- center_x - span_x
    right <- center_x + span_x
    top <- center_y - span_y
    bottom <- center_y + span_y
    dx <- right - left
    dy <- bottom - top
    frame_acc <- frame + 1
    for (y in 0:(height - 1)) {
      cy <- top + (y * dy) / (height - 1)
      for (x in 0:(width - 1)) {
        cx <- left + (x * dx) / (width - 1)
        it <- mandel_iter(cx, cy, max_it)
        frame_acc <- (frame_acc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) %% MOD
      }
    }
    acc <- (acc + frame_acc) %% MOD
    span_x <- (span_x * 97.0) / 100.0
    span_y <- (span_y * 97.0) / 100.0
    if (span_x < 0.03125) {
      center_x <- CX
      center_y <- CY
      span_x <- SX
      span_y <- (span_x * height) / width
    }
  }
  acc
}

frames <- 80
width <- 100
height <- 36
max_it <- 64
result <- mandel(frames, width, height, max_it)
cat(as.integer(result), "\n", sep = "")

Mandelbrot Zoom / Decimal / Rust

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/rust/src/bin/mandel_dec.rs 

const MOD: i32 = 100_000_007;
const CX: f64 = -1.482421875;
const CY: f64 = 0.0;
const SX: f64 = 1.5;

fn mandel_iter(cx: f64, cy: f64, max_it: i32) -> i32 {
    let mut zx = 0.0_f64;
    let mut zy = 0.0_f64;
    let mut iter = 0_i32;
    let mut mag2 = 0.0_f64;
    while iter < max_it && mag2 < 4.0 {
        let x2 = zx * zx;
        let y2 = zy * zy;
        let xy2 = 2.0 * zx * zy;
        zy = xy2 + cy;
        zx = x2 - y2 + cx;
        mag2 = zx * zx + zy * zy;
        iter += 1;
    }
    iter
}

fn mandel(frames: i32, width: i32, height: i32, max_it: i32) -> i32 {
    let mut center_x = CX;
    let mut center_y = CY;
    let mut span_x = SX;
    let mut span_y = (span_x * f64::from(height)) / f64::from(width);
    let mut acc = 0_i32;
    for frame in 0..frames {
        let left = center_x - span_x;
        let right = center_x + span_x;
        let top = center_y - span_y;
        let bottom = center_y + span_y;
        let dx = right - left;
        let dy = bottom - top;
        let mut frame_acc = frame + 1;
        for y in 0..height {
            let cy = top + (f64::from(y) * dy) / f64::from(height - 1);
            for x in 0..width {
                let cx = left + (f64::from(x) * dx) / f64::from(width - 1);
                let it = mandel_iter(cx, cy, max_it);
                frame_acc = (frame_acc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) % MOD;
            }
        }
        acc = (acc + frame_acc) % MOD;
        span_x = (span_x * 97.0) / 100.0;
        span_y = (span_y * 97.0) / 100.0;
        if span_x < 0.03125 {
            center_x = CX;
            center_y = CY;
            span_x = SX;
            span_y = (span_x * f64::from(height)) / f64::from(width);
        }
    }
    acc
}

fn main() {
    let frames = 80;
    let width = 100;
    let height = 36;
    let max_it = 64;
    let result = mandel(frames, width, height, max_it);
    println!("{}", result);
}

Mandelbrot Zoom / Decimal / Scala

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/scala/workloads/MandelDec.scala 

object MandelDec {
  private final val Mod = 100000007
  private final val Cx0 = -1.482421875
  private final val Cy0 = 0.0
  private final val Sx0 = 1.5

  private def mandelIter(cx: Double, cy: Double, maxIter: Int): Int = {
    var zx = 0.0
    var zy = 0.0
    var iter = 0
    var mag2 = 0.0
    while (iter < maxIter && mag2 < 4.0) {
      val x2 = zx * zx
      val y2 = zy * zy
      val xy2 = 2.0 * zx * zy
      zy = xy2 + cy
      zx = x2 - y2 + cx
      mag2 = zx * zx + zy * zy
      iter += 1
    }
    iter
  }

  private def mandel(frames: Int, width: Int, height: Int, maxIter: Int): Int = {
    var centerX = Cx0
    var centerY = Cy0
    var spanX = Sx0
    var spanY = (spanX * height) / width
    var acc = 0
    var frame = 0
    while (frame < frames) {
      val left = centerX - spanX
      val right = centerX + spanX
      val top = centerY - spanY
      val bottom = centerY + spanY
      val dx = right - left
      val dy = bottom - top
      var frameAcc = frame + 1
      var y = 0
      while (y < height) {
        val cy = top + (y * dy) / (height - 1)
        var x = 0
        while (x < width) {
          val cx = left + (x * dx) / (width - 1)
          val it = mandelIter(cx, cy, maxIter)
          frameAcc = (frameAcc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) % Mod
          x += 1
        }
        y += 1
      }
      acc = (acc + frameAcc) % Mod
      spanX = (spanX * 97.0) / 100.0
      spanY = (spanY * 97.0) / 100.0
      if (spanX < 0.03125) {
        centerX = Cx0
        centerY = Cy0
        spanX = Sx0
        spanY = (spanX * height) / width
      }
      frame += 1
    }
    acc
  }

  def main(args: Array[String]): Unit = {
    val frames = 80
    val width = 100
    val height = 36
    val maxIter = 64
    val result = mandel(frames, width, height, maxIter)
    println(result)
  }
}

let mod = 100000007
let cx0 = -1.482421875
let cy0 = 0.0
let sx0 = 1.5

func mandelIter(_ cx: Double, _ cy: Double, _ maxIter: Int) -> Int {
    var zx = 0.0
    var zy = 0.0
    var iter = 0
    var mag2 = 0.0
    while iter < maxIter && mag2 < 4.0 {
        let x2 = zx * zx
        let y2 = zy * zy
        let xy2 = 2.0 * zx * zy
        zy = xy2 + cy
        zx = x2 - y2 + cx
        mag2 = zx * zx + zy * zy
        iter += 1
    }
    return iter
}

func mandel(_ frames: Int, _ width: Int, _ height: Int, _ maxIter: Int) -> Int {
    var centerX = cx0
    var centerY = cy0
    var spanX = sx0
    var spanY = (spanX * Double(height)) / Double(width)
    var acc = 0
    for frame in 0..<frames {
        let left = centerX - spanX
        let right = centerX + spanX
        let top = centerY - spanY
        let bottom = centerY + spanY
        let dx = right - left
        let dy = bottom - top
        var frameAcc = frame + 1
        for y in 0..<height {
            let cy = top + (Double(y) * dy) / Double(height - 1)
            for x in 0..<width {
                let cx = left + (Double(x) * dx) / Double(width - 1)
                let it = mandelIter(cx, cy, maxIter)
                frameAcc = (frameAcc + it * (x + 1 + y * width) + 1) % mod
            }
        }
        acc = (acc + frameAcc) % mod
        spanX = (spanX * 97.0) / 100.0
        spanY = (spanY * 97.0) / 100.0
        if spanX < 0.03125 {
            centerX = cx0
            centerY = cy0
            spanX = sx0
            spanY = (spanX * Double(height)) / Double(width)
        }
    }
    return acc
}

let height = 36

(let MOD 100000007)
(let WIDTH 80)
(let HEIGHT 25)
(let BUFFER-SIZE (* WIDTH HEIGHT))
(let PALETTE-MAX 11)
(let R1 1)
(let R2 2048)
(let K2 (* 5120 1024))

(let make-buffer (lambda n value (do
  (let out [])
  (mut i 0)
  (while (< i n) (do
    (set! out (length out) value)
    (alter! i (+ i 1))))
  out)))

(let clear-buffer! (lambda buffer value (do
  (mut i 0)
  (while (< i BUFFER-SIZE) (do
    (set! buffer i value)
    (alter! i (+ i 1))))
  nil)))

(let frame-hash (lambda output zbuffer weight (do
  (mut acc weight)
  (mut i 0)
  (while (< i BUFFER-SIZE) (do
    (alter! acc (mod (+ acc (* (+ i 1) (get output i)) (+ (get zbuffer i) 256)) MOD))
    (alter! i (+ i 1))))
  acc)))

(let FRAMES 160)

(let zbuffer (make-buffer BUFFER-SIZE 127))
(mut sA 1024)
(mut cA 0)
(mut sB 1024)
(mut cB 0)
(mut frame 0)
(mut acc 0)

(while (< frame FRAMES) (do
  (clear-buffer! output 0)
  (clear-buffer! zbuffer 127)

  (mut sj 0)
  (mut cj 1024)
  (mut j 0)
  (while (< j 90) (do
    (mut si 0)
    (mut ci 1024)
    (mut i 0)
    (while (< i 324) (do
      (let x0 (+ (* R1 cj) R2))
      (let x1 (>> (* ci x0) 10))
      (let x2 (>> (* cA sj) 10))
      (let x3 (>> (* si x0) 10))
      (let x4 (- (* R1 x2) (>> (* sA x3) 10)))
      (let x5 (>> (* sA sj) 10))
      (let x6 (+ K2 (* R1 1024 x5) (* cA x3)))
      (let x7 (>> (* cj si) 10))

      (let x (+ 40 (/ (* 30 (- (* cB x1) (* sB x4))) x6)))
      (let y (+ 12 (/ (* 15 (+ (* cB x4) (* sB x1))) x6)))

      (let n0 (- 0
                 (* cA x7)
                 (* cB (+ (>> (- 0 (* sA x7)) 10) x2))
                 (* ci (>> (* cj sB) 10))))
      (let n1 (>> n0 10))
      (let N (>> (- n1 x5) 7))

      (if (and (> HEIGHT y) (> y 0) (> x 0) (> WIDTH x))
          (do
            (let o (+ x (* WIDTH y)))
            (let zz (>> (- x6 K2) 15))
            (if (< zz (get zbuffer o))
                (do
                  (set! zbuffer o zz)
                  (mut shade (if (> N 0) N 0))
                  (if (> shade PALETTE-MAX) (alter! shade PALETTE-MAX) nil)
                  (set! output o (+ shade 1)))
                nil))
          nil)

      (let tmp0 ci)
      (alter! ci (- ci (>> (* 5 si) 8)))
      (alter! si (+ si (>> (* 5 tmp0) 8)))
      (let norm0 (>> (- 3145728 (* ci ci) (* si si)) 11))
      (alter! ci (>> (* ci norm0) 10))
      (alter! si (>> (* si norm0) 10))
      (alter! i (+ i 1))))

    (let tmp1 cj)
    (alter! cj (- cj (>> (* 9 sj) 7)))
    (alter! sj (+ sj (>> (* 9 tmp1) 7)))
    (let norm1 (>> (- 3145728 (* cj cj) (* sj sj)) 11))
    (alter! cj (>> (* cj norm1) 10))
    (alter! sj (>> (* sj norm1) 10))
    (alter! j (+ j 1))))

  (alter! acc (mod (+ acc (frame-hash output zbuffer (+ frame 1))) MOD))

  (let tmp2 cA)
  (alter! cA (- cA (>> (* 5 sA) 7)))
  (alter! sA (+ sA (>> (* 5 tmp2) 7)))
  (let norm2 (>> (- 3145728 (* cA cA) (* sA sA)) 11))
  (alter! cA (>> (* cA norm2) 10))
  (alter! sA (>> (* sA norm2) 10))

  (let tmp3 cB)
  (alter! cB (- cB (>> (* 5 sB) 8)))
  (alter! sB (+ sB (>> (* 5 tmp3) 8)))
  (let norm3 (>> (- 3145728 (* cB cB) (* sB sB)) 11))
  (alter! cB (>> (* cB norm3) 10))
  (alter! sB (>> (* sB norm3) 10))

  (alter! frame (+ frame 1))))
acc

ASCII Donut / Clojure

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/clojure/workloads/donut.clj 

(def mod-value 100000007)
(def width 80)
(def height 25)
(def buffer-size (* width height))
(def palette-max 11)
(def r1 1)
(def r2 2048)
(def k2 (* 5120 1024))

(defn parse-int [text]
  (Integer/parseInt text))

(defn donut [frames]
  (let [output (int-array buffer-size)
        zbuffer (int-array buffer-size)]
    (loop [frame 0
           s-a 1024
           c-a 0
           s-b 1024
           c-b 0
           acc 0]
      (if (= frame frames)
        acc
        (do
          (java.util.Arrays/fill output (int 0))
          (java.util.Arrays/fill zbuffer (int 127))
          (let [[next-acc next-s-a next-c-a next-s-b next-c-b]
                (loop [j 0
                       sj 0
                       cj 1024]
                  (if (= j 90)
                    (let [frame-acc
                          (loop [i 0
                                 acc1 (inc frame)]
                            (if (= i buffer-size)
                              acc1
                              (recur (inc i)
                                     (mod (+ acc1 (* (inc i) (aget output i)) (aget zbuffer i) 256)
                                          mod-value))))
                          total-acc (mod (+ acc frame-acc) mod-value)
                          tmp2 c-a
                          nc-a (- c-a (bit-shift-right (* 5 s-a) 7))
                          ns-a (+ s-a (bit-shift-right (* 5 tmp2) 7))
                          norm2 (bit-shift-right (- 3145728 (* nc-a nc-a) (* ns-a ns-a)) 11)
                          norm-c-a (bit-shift-right (* nc-a norm2) 10)
                          norm-s-a (bit-shift-right (* ns-a norm2) 10)
                          tmp3 c-b
                          nc-b (- c-b (bit-shift-right (* 5 s-b) 8))
                          ns-b (+ s-b (bit-shift-right (* 5 tmp3) 8))
                          norm3 (bit-shift-right (- 3145728 (* nc-b nc-b) (* ns-b ns-b)) 11)
                          norm-c-b (bit-shift-right (* nc-b norm3) 10)
                          norm-s-b (bit-shift-right (* ns-b norm3) 10)]
                      [total-acc norm-s-a norm-c-a norm-s-b norm-c-b])
                    (let [[next-sj next-cj]
                          (loop [i 0
                                 si 0
                                 ci 1024]
                            (if (= i 324)
                              (let [tmp1 cj
                                    cj2 (- cj (bit-shift-right (* 9 sj) 7))
                                    sj2 (+ sj (bit-shift-right (* 9 tmp1) 7))
                                    norm1 (bit-shift-right (- 3145728 (* cj2 cj2) (* sj2 sj2)) 11)
                                    out-cj (bit-shift-right (* cj2 norm1) 10)
                                    out-sj (bit-shift-right (* sj2 norm1) 10)]
                                [out-sj out-cj])
                              (let [x0 (+ (* r1 cj) r2)
                                    x1 (bit-shift-right (* ci x0) 10)
                                    x2 (bit-shift-right (* c-a sj) 10)
                                    x3 (bit-shift-right (* si x0) 10)
                                    x4 (- (* r1 x2) (bit-shift-right (* s-a x3) 10))
                                    x5 (bit-shift-right (* s-a sj) 10)
                                    x6 (+ k2 (* r1 1024 x5) (* c-a x3))
                                    x7 (bit-shift-right (* cj si) 10)
                                    x (+ 40 (quot (* 30 (- (* c-b x1) (* s-b x4))) x6))
                                    y (+ 12 (quot (* 15 (+ (* c-b x4) (* s-b x1))) x6))
                                    n0 (- 0
                                          (* c-a x7)
                                          (* c-b (+ (bit-shift-right (- 0 (* s-a x7)) 10) x2))
                                          (* ci (bit-shift-right (* cj s-b) 10)))
                                    n1 (bit-shift-right n0 10)
                                    n (bit-shift-right (- n1 x5) 7)
                                    _ (when (and (< y height) (> y 0) (> x 0) (< x width))
                                        (let [o (+ x (* width y))
                                              zz (bit-shift-right (- x6 k2) 15)]
                                          (when (< zz (aget zbuffer o))
                                            (aset-int zbuffer o zz)
                                            (let [shade (min palette-max (max n 0))]
                                              (aset-int output o (inc shade))))))
                                    tmp0 ci
                                    ci2 (- ci (bit-shift-right (* 5 si) 8))
                                    si2 (+ si (bit-shift-right (* 5 tmp0) 8))
                                    norm0 (bit-shift-right (- 3145728 (* ci2 ci2) (* si2 si2)) 11)
                                    next-ci (bit-shift-right (* ci2 norm0) 10)
                                    next-si (bit-shift-right (* si2 norm0) 10)]
                                (recur (inc i) next-si next-ci))))]
                      (recur (inc j) next-sj next-cj))))]
            (recur (inc frame) next-s-a next-c-a next-s-b next-c-b next-acc)))))))

(let [frames 160
      result (donut frames)]
  (println result))

ASCII Donut / C++

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/cpp/workloads/donut.cpp 

#include <cstdint>
#include <iostream>
#include <stdexcept>
#include <string>
#include <vector>

namespace {

constexpr int MOD = 100000007;
constexpr int WIDTH = 80;
constexpr int HEIGHT = 25;
constexpr int BUFFER_SIZE = WIDTH * HEIGHT;
constexpr int PALETTE_MAX = 11;
constexpr int R1 = 1;
constexpr int R2 = 2048;
constexpr int K2 = 5120 * 1024;

int donut(int frames) {
    std::vector<int> output(BUFFER_SIZE, 0);
    std::vector<int> zbuffer(BUFFER_SIZE, 127);
    int s_a = 1024;
    int c_a = 0;
    int s_b = 1024;
    int c_b = 0;
    int acc = 0;

    for (int frame = 0; frame < frames; ++frame) {
        for (int i = 0; i < BUFFER_SIZE; ++i) {
            output[i] = 0;
            zbuffer[i] = 127;
        }

        int sj = 0;
        int cj = 1024;
        int j = 0;
        while (j < 90) {
            int si = 0;
            int ci = 1024;
            int i = 0;
            while (i < 324) {
                int x0 = R1 * cj + R2;
                int x1 = (ci * x0) >> 10;
                int x2 = (c_a * sj) >> 10;
                int x3 = (si * x0) >> 10;
                int x4 = R1 * x2 - ((s_a * x3) >> 10);
                int x5 = (s_a * sj) >> 10;
                int x6 = K2 + R1 * 1024 * x5 + c_a * x3;
                int x7 = (cj * si) >> 10;

                int x = 40 + (30 * (c_b * x1 - s_b * x4)) / x6;
                int y = 12 + (15 * (c_b * x4 + s_b * x1)) / x6;

                int n0 = 0 - c_a * x7 - c_b * (((0 - s_a * x7) >> 10) + x2) - ci * ((cj * s_b) >> 10);
                int n1 = n0 >> 10;
                int shade_n = (n1 - x5) >> 7;

                if (y < HEIGHT && y > 0 && x > 0 && x < WIDTH) {
                    int o = x + WIDTH * y;
                    int zz = (x6 - K2) >> 15;
                    if (zz < zbuffer[o]) {
                        zbuffer[o] = zz;
                        int shade = shade_n;
                        if (shade < 0) {
                            shade = 0;
                        }
                        if (shade > PALETTE_MAX) {
                            shade = PALETTE_MAX;
                        }
                        output[o] = shade + 1;
                    }
                }

                int tmp0 = ci;
                ci = ci - ((5 * si) >> 8);
                si = si + ((5 * tmp0) >> 8);
                int norm0 = (3145728 - ci * ci - si * si) >> 11;
                ci = (ci * norm0) >> 10;
                si = (si * norm0) >> 10;
                ++i;
            }

            int tmp1 = cj;
            cj = cj - ((9 * sj) >> 7);
            sj = sj + ((9 * tmp1) >> 7);
            int norm1 = (3145728 - cj * cj - sj * sj) >> 11;
            cj = (cj * norm1) >> 10;
            sj = (sj * norm1) >> 10;
            ++j;
        }

        int frame_acc = frame + 1;
        for (int i = 0; i < BUFFER_SIZE; ++i) {
            frame_acc = (frame_acc + (i + 1) * output[i] + zbuffer[i] + 256) % MOD;
        }
        acc = (acc + frame_acc) % MOD;

        int tmp2 = c_a;
        c_a = c_a - ((5 * s_a) >> 7);
        s_a = s_a + ((5 * tmp2) >> 7);
        int norm2 = (3145728 - c_a * c_a - s_a * s_a) >> 11;
        c_a = (c_a * norm2) >> 10;
        s_a = (s_a * norm2) >> 10;

        int tmp3 = c_b;
        c_b = c_b - ((5 * s_b) >> 8);
        s_b = s_b + ((5 * tmp3) >> 8);
        int norm3 = (3145728 - c_b * c_b - s_b * s_b) >> 11;
        c_b = (c_b * norm3) >> 10;
        s_b = (s_b * norm3) >> 10;
    }

    return acc;
}

}  // namespace

int main() {
    constexpr int frames = 160;
    int result = donut(frames);
    std::cout << result << '\n';
    return 0;
}

using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;

public static class Donut
{
    private const int Mod = 100000007;
    private const int Width = 80;
    private const int Height = 25;
    private const int BufferSize = Width * Height;
    private const int PaletteMax = 11;
    private const int R1 = 1;
    private const int R2 = 2048;
    private const int K2 = 5120 * 1024;


    private static int Benchmark(int frames)
    {
        var output = new int[BufferSize];
        var zbuffer = new int[BufferSize];
        var sA = 1024;
        var cA = 0;
        var sB = 1024;
        var cB = 0;
        var acc = 0;

        for (var frame = 0; frame < frames; frame += 1)
        {
            Array.Fill(output, 0);
            Array.Fill(zbuffer, 127);

            var sj = 0;
            var cj = 1024;
            var j = 0;
            while (j < 90)
            {
                var si = 0;
                var ci = 1024;
                var i = 0;
                while (i < 324)
                {
                    var x0 = R1 * cj + R2;
                    var x1 = (ci * x0) >> 10;
                    var x2 = (cA * sj) >> 10;
                    var x3 = (si * x0) >> 10;
                    var x4 = R1 * x2 - ((sA * x3) >> 10);
                    var x5 = (sA * sj) >> 10;
                    var x6 = K2 + R1 * 1024 * x5 + cA * x3;
                    var x7 = (cj * si) >> 10;

                    var x = 40 + (30 * (cB * x1 - sB * x4)) / x6;
                    var y = 12 + (15 * (cB * x4 + sB * x1)) / x6;

                    var n0 = 0 - cA * x7 - cB * (((0 - sA * x7) >> 10) + x2) - ci * ((cj * sB) >> 10);
                    var n1 = n0 >> 10;
                    var shadeN = (n1 - x5) >> 7;

                    if (y < Height && y > 0 && x > 0 && x < Width)
                    {
                        var o = x + Width * y;
                        var zz = (x6 - K2) >> 15;
                        if (zz < zbuffer[o])
                        {
                            zbuffer[o] = zz;
                            var shade = shadeN;
                            if (shade < 0) shade = 0;
                            if (shade > PaletteMax) shade = PaletteMax;
                            output[o] = shade + 1;
                        }
                    }

                    var tmp0 = ci;
                    ci = ci - ((5 * si) >> 8);
                    si = si + ((5 * tmp0) >> 8);
                    var norm0 = (3145728 - ci * ci - si * si) >> 11;
                    ci = (ci * norm0) >> 10;
                    si = (si * norm0) >> 10;
                    i += 1;
                }

                var tmp1 = cj;
                cj = cj - ((9 * sj) >> 7);
                sj = sj + ((9 * tmp1) >> 7);
                var norm1 = (3145728 - cj * cj - sj * sj) >> 11;
                cj = (cj * norm1) >> 10;
                sj = (sj * norm1) >> 10;
                j += 1;
            }

            var frameAcc = frame + 1;
            for (var i = 0; i < BufferSize; i += 1)
            {
                frameAcc = (frameAcc + (i + 1) * output[i] + zbuffer[i] + 256) % Mod;
            }
            acc = (acc + frameAcc) % Mod;

            var tmp2 = cA;
            cA = cA - ((5 * sA) >> 7);
            sA = sA + ((5 * tmp2) >> 7);
            var norm2 = (3145728 - cA * cA - sA * sA) >> 11;
            cA = (cA * norm2) >> 10;
            sA = (sA * norm2) >> 10;

            var tmp3 = cB;
            cB = cB - ((5 * sB) >> 8);
            sB = sB + ((5 * tmp3) >> 8);
            var norm3 = (3145728 - cB * cB - sB * sB) >> 11;
            cB = (cB * norm3) >> 10;
            sB = (sB * norm3) >> 10;
        }

        return acc;
    }

    public static void Main(string[] args)
    {
        const int frames = 160;
        var result = Benchmark(frames);
        Console.WriteLine(result);
    }
}
