import 'dart:io';

const int modValue = 100000007;
const int width = 80;
const int height = 25;
const int bufferSize = width * height;
const int paletteMax = 11;
const int r1 = 1;
const int r2 = 2048;
const int k2 = 5120 * 1024;

int donut(int frames) {
  final output = List<int>.filled(bufferSize, 0);
  final zbuffer = List<int>.filled(bufferSize, 127);
  var sA = 1024;
  var cA = 0;
  var sB = 1024;
  var cB = 0;
  var acc = 0;

  var frame = 0;
  while (frame < frames) {
    var i = 0;
    while (i < bufferSize) {
      output[i] = 0;
      zbuffer[i] = 127;
      i += 1;
    }

    var sj = 0;
    var cj = 1024;
    var j = 0;
    while (j < 90) {
      var si = 0;
      var ci = 1024;
      i = 0;
      while (i < 324) {
        final x0 = r1 * cj + r2;
        final x1 = (ci * x0) >> 10;
        final x2 = (cA * sj) >> 10;
        final x3 = (si * x0) >> 10;
        final x4 = r1 * x2 - ((sA * x3) >> 10);
        final x5 = (sA * sj) >> 10;
        final x6 = k2 + r1 * 1024 * x5 + cA * x3;
        final x7 = (cj * si) >> 10;

        final x = 40 + ((30 * (cB * x1 - sB * x4)) ~/ x6);
        final y = 12 + ((15 * (cB * x4 + sB * x1)) ~/ x6);

        final n0 = 0 - cA * x7 - cB * ((((0 - sA * x7) >> 10) + x2)) - ci * ((cj * sB) >> 10);
        final n1 = n0 >> 10;
        final shadeN = (n1 - x5) >> 7;

        if (y < height && y > 0 && x > 0 && x < width) {
          final o = x + width * y;
          final zz = (x6 - k2) >> 15;
          if (zz < zbuffer[o]) {
            zbuffer[o] = zz;
            var shade = shadeN;
            if (shade < 0) {
              shade = 0;
            }
            if (shade > paletteMax) {
              shade = paletteMax;
            }
            output[o] = shade + 1;
          }
        }

        final tmp0 = ci;
        ci = ci - ((5 * si) >> 8);
        si = si + ((5 * tmp0) >> 8);
        final norm0 = (3145728 - ci * ci - si * si) >> 11;
        ci = (ci * norm0) >> 10;
        si = (si * norm0) >> 10;
        i += 1;
      }

      final tmp1 = cj;
      cj = cj - ((9 * sj) >> 7);
      sj = sj + ((9 * tmp1) >> 7);
      final norm1 = (3145728 - cj * cj - sj * sj) >> 11;
      cj = (cj * norm1) >> 10;
      sj = (sj * norm1) >> 10;
      j += 1;
    }

    var frameAcc = frame + 1;
    i = 0;
    while (i < bufferSize) {
      frameAcc = (frameAcc + (i + 1) * output[i] + zbuffer[i] + 256) % modValue;
      i += 1;
    }
    acc = (acc + frameAcc) % modValue;

    final tmp2 = cA;
    cA = cA - ((5 * sA) >> 7);
    sA = sA + ((5 * tmp2) >> 7);
    final norm2 = (3145728 - cA * cA - sA * sA) >> 11;
    cA = (cA * norm2) >> 10;
    sA = (sA * norm2) >> 10;

    final tmp3 = cB;
    cB = cB - ((5 * sB) >> 8);
    sB = sB + ((5 * tmp3) >> 8);
    final norm3 = (3145728 - cB * cB - sB * sB) >> 11;
    cB = (cB * norm3) >> 10;
    sB = (sB * norm3) >> 10;

    frame += 1;
  }

  return acc;
}

void main(List<String> argv) {
  const frames = 160;
  final result = donut(frames);
  stdout.writeln(result);
}

ASCII Donut / Go

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/go/workloads/donut.go 

package main

import (
	"fmt"
)

const (
	mod        = 100000007
	width      = 80
	height     = 25
	bufferSize = width * height
	paletteMax = 11
	r1         = 1
	r2         = 2048
	k2         = 5120 * 1024
)

func donut(frames int) int {
	output := make([]int, bufferSize)
	zbuffer := make([]int, bufferSize)
	sA := 1024
	cA := 0
	sB := 1024
	cB := 0
	acc := 0

	for frame := 0; frame < frames; frame++ {
		for i := 0; i < bufferSize; i++ {
			output[i] = 0
			zbuffer[i] = 127
		}

		sj := 0
		cj := 1024
		j := 0
		for j < 90 {
			si := 0
			ci := 1024
			i := 0
			for i < 324 {
				x0 := r1*cj + r2
				x1 := (ci * x0) >> 10
				x2 := (cA * sj) >> 10
				x3 := (si * x0) >> 10
				x4 := r1*x2 - ((sA * x3) >> 10)
				x5 := (sA * sj) >> 10
				x6 := k2 + r1*1024*x5 + cA*x3
				x7 := (cj * si) >> 10

				x := 40 + (30*(cB*x1-sB*x4))/x6
				y := 12 + (15*(cB*x4+sB*x1))/x6

				n0 := 0 - cA*x7 - cB*(((0-sA*x7)>>10)+x2) - ci*((cj*sB)>>10)
				n1 := n0 >> 10
				shadeN := (n1 - x5) >> 7

				if y < height && y > 0 && x > 0 && x < width {
					o := x + width*y
					zz := (x6 - k2) >> 15
					if zz < zbuffer[o] {
						zbuffer[o] = zz
						shade := shadeN
						if shade < 0 {
							shade = 0
						}
						if shade > paletteMax {
							shade = paletteMax
						}
						output[o] = shade + 1
					}
				}

				tmp0 := ci
				ci = ci - ((5 * si) >> 8)
				si = si + ((5 * tmp0) >> 8)
				norm0 := (3145728 - ci*ci - si*si) >> 11
				ci = (ci * norm0) >> 10
				si = (si * norm0) >> 10
				i++
			}

			tmp1 := cj
			cj = cj - ((9 * sj) >> 7)
			sj = sj + ((9 * tmp1) >> 7)
			norm1 := (3145728 - cj*cj - sj*sj) >> 11
			cj = (cj * norm1) >> 10
			sj = (sj * norm1) >> 10
			j++
		}

		frameAcc := frame + 1
		for i := 0; i < bufferSize; i++ {
			frameAcc = (frameAcc + (i+1)*output[i] + zbuffer[i] + 256) % mod
		}
		acc = (acc + frameAcc) % mod

		tmp2 := cA
		cA = cA - ((5 * sA) >> 7)
		sA = sA + ((5 * tmp2) >> 7)
		norm2 := (3145728 - cA*cA - sA*sA) >> 11
		cA = (cA * norm2) >> 10
		sA = (sA * norm2) >> 10

		tmp3 := cB
		cB = cB - ((5 * sB) >> 8)
		sB = sB + ((5 * tmp3) >> 8)
		norm3 := (3145728 - cB*cB - sB*sB) >> 11
		cB = (cB * norm3) >> 10
		sB = (sB * norm3) >> 10
	}

	return acc
}


func main() {
	const frames = 160
	result := donut(frames)
	fmt.Println(result)
}

ASCII Donut / Haskell

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/haskell/workloads/donut.hs 

{-# LANGUAGE BangPatterns #-}

module Main where

import Control.Monad (when)
import Data.Array.IO (IOUArray)
import Data.Array.MArray (newArray, readArray, writeArray)
import Data.Bits (shiftR)

modValue :: Int
modValue = 100000007

width :: Int
width = 80

height :: Int
height = 25

bufferSize :: Int
bufferSize = width * height

paletteMax :: Int
paletteMax = 11

r1 :: Int
r1 = 1

r2 :: Int
r2 = 2048

k2 :: Int
k2 = 5120 * 1024

donut :: Int -> IO Int
donut frames = do
  output <- newArray (0, bufferSize - 1) 0 :: IO (IOUArray Int Int)
  zbuffer <- newArray (0, bufferSize - 1) 127 :: IO (IOUArray Int Int)
  frameLoop 0 1024 0 1024 0 0 output zbuffer
  where
    frameLoop !frame !sA !cA !sB !cB !acc output zbuffer
      | frame >= frames = pure acc
      | otherwise = do
          clearBuffers 0 output zbuffer
          innerJ 0 0 1024 output zbuffer sA cA sB cB
          frameAcc <- hashFrame frame 0 (frame + 1) output zbuffer
          let acc' = (acc + frameAcc) `mod` modValue
              tmp2 = cA
              cA1 = cA - shiftR (5 * sA) 7
              sA1 = sA + shiftR (5 * tmp2) 7
              norm2 = shiftR (3145728 - cA1 * cA1 - sA1 * sA1) 11
              cA2 = shiftR (cA1 * norm2) 10
              sA2 = shiftR (sA1 * norm2) 10
              tmp3 = cB
              cB1 = cB - shiftR (5 * sB) 8
              sB1 = sB + shiftR (5 * tmp3) 8
              norm3 = shiftR (3145728 - cB1 * cB1 - sB1 * sB1) 11
              cB2 = shiftR (cB1 * norm3) 10
              sB2 = shiftR (sB1 * norm3) 10
          frameLoop (frame + 1) sA2 cA2 sB2 cB2 acc' output zbuffer

    clearBuffers i output zbuffer
      | i >= bufferSize = pure ()
      | otherwise = do
          writeArray output i 0
          writeArray zbuffer i 127
          clearBuffers (i + 1) output zbuffer

    innerJ !j !sj !cj output zbuffer sA cA sB cB
      | j >= 90 = pure ()
      | otherwise = do
          innerI 0 0 1024 output zbuffer sj cj sA cA sB cB
          let tmp1 = cj
              cj1 = cj - shiftR (9 * sj) 7
              sj1 = sj + shiftR (9 * tmp1) 7
              norm1 = shiftR (3145728 - cj1 * cj1 - sj1 * sj1) 11
              cj2 = shiftR (cj1 * norm1) 10
              sj2 = shiftR (sj1 * norm1) 10
          innerJ (j + 1) sj2 cj2 output zbuffer sA cA sB cB

    innerI !i !si !ci output zbuffer sj cj sA cA sB cB
      | i >= 324 = pure ()
      | otherwise = do
          let x0 = r1 * cj + r2
              x1 = shiftR (ci * x0) 10
              x2 = shiftR (cA * sj) 10
              x3 = shiftR (si * x0) 10
              x4 = r1 * x2 - shiftR (sA * x3) 10
              x5 = shiftR (sA * sj) 10
              x6 = k2 + r1 * 1024 * x5 + cA * x3
              x7 = shiftR (cj * si) 10
              x = 40 + quot (30 * (cB * x1 - sB * x4)) x6
              y = 12 + quot (15 * (cB * x4 + sB * x1)) x6
              n0 = 0 - cA * x7 - cB * (shiftR (0 - sA * x7) 10 + x2) - ci * shiftR (cj * sB) 10
              n1 = shiftR n0 10
              shadeN = shiftR (n1 - x5) 7
          if y < height && y > 0 && x > 0 && x < width
            then do
              let o = x + width * y
                  zz = shiftR (x6 - k2) 15
              currentZ <- readArray zbuffer o
              when (zz < currentZ) $ do
                writeArray zbuffer o zz
                let shade = max 0 (min paletteMax shadeN)
                writeArray output o (shade + 1)
            else pure ()
          let tmp0 = ci
              ci1 = ci - shiftR (5 * si) 8
              si1 = si + shiftR (5 * tmp0) 8
              norm0 = shiftR (3145728 - ci1 * ci1 - si1 * si1) 11
              ci2 = shiftR (ci1 * norm0) 10
              si2 = shiftR (si1 * norm0) 10
          innerI (i + 1) si2 ci2 output zbuffer sj cj sA cA sB cB

    hashFrame frame i !frameAcc output zbuffer
      | i >= bufferSize = pure frameAcc
      | otherwise = do
          out <- readArray output i
          zz <- readArray zbuffer i
          let frameAcc' = (frameAcc + (i + 1) * out + zz + 256) `mod` modValue
          hashFrame frame (i + 1) frameAcc' output zbuffer

main :: IO ()
main = do
  let frames = 160
  result <- donut frames
  print result

ASCII Donut / Java

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/java/workloads/Donut.java 

public final class Donut {
    private static final int MOD = 100000007;
    private static final int WIDTH = 80;
    private static final int HEIGHT = 25;
    private static final int BUFFER_SIZE = WIDTH * HEIGHT;
    private static final int PALETTE_MAX = 11;
    private static final int R1 = 1;
    private static final int R2 = 2048;
    private static final int K2 = 5120 * 1024;

    private Donut() {}

    private static int donut(int frames) {
        final int[] output = new int[BUFFER_SIZE];
        final int[] zbuffer = new int[BUFFER_SIZE];
        int sA = 1024;
        int cA = 0;
        int sB = 1024;
        int cB = 0;
        int acc = 0;

        for (int frame = 0; frame < frames; frame += 1) {
            for (int i = 0; i < BUFFER_SIZE; i += 1) {
                output[i] = 0;
                zbuffer[i] = 127;
            }

            int sj = 0;
            int cj = 1024;
            int j = 0;
            while (j < 90) {
                int si = 0;
                int ci = 1024;
                int i = 0;
                while (i < 324) {
                    final int x0 = R1 * cj + R2;
                    final int x1 = (ci * x0) >> 10;
                    final int x2 = (cA * sj) >> 10;
                    final int x3 = (si * x0) >> 10;
                    final int x4 = R1 * x2 - ((sA * x3) >> 10);
                    final int x5 = (sA * sj) >> 10;
                    final int x6 = K2 + R1 * 1024 * x5 + cA * x3;
                    final int x7 = (cj * si) >> 10;

                    final int x = 40 + (30 * (cB * x1 - sB * x4)) / x6;
                    final int y = 12 + (15 * (cB * x4 + sB * x1)) / x6;

                    final int n0 = 0 - cA * x7 - cB * (((0 - sA * x7) >> 10) + x2) - ci * ((cj * sB) >> 10);
                    final int n1 = n0 >> 10;
                    final int n = (n1 - x5) >> 7;

                    if (y < HEIGHT && y > 0 && x > 0 && x < WIDTH) {
                        final int o = x + WIDTH * y;
                        final int zz = (x6 - K2) >> 15;
                        if (zz < zbuffer[o]) {
                            zbuffer[o] = zz;
                            int shade = n > 0 ? n : 0;
                            if (shade > PALETTE_MAX) {
                                shade = PALETTE_MAX;
                            }
                            output[o] = shade + 1;
                        }
                    }

                    final int tmp0 = ci;
                    ci = ci - ((5 * si) >> 8);
                    si = si + ((5 * tmp0) >> 8);
                    final int norm0 = (3145728 - ci * ci - si * si) >> 11;
                    ci = (ci * norm0) >> 10;
                    si = (si * norm0) >> 10;
                    i += 1;
                }

                final int tmp1 = cj;
                cj = cj - ((9 * sj) >> 7);
                sj = sj + ((9 * tmp1) >> 7);
                final int norm1 = (3145728 - cj * cj - sj * sj) >> 11;
                cj = (cj * norm1) >> 10;
                sj = (sj * norm1) >> 10;
                j += 1;
            }

            int frameAcc = frame + 1;
            for (int i = 0; i < BUFFER_SIZE; i += 1) {
                frameAcc = (frameAcc + (i + 1) * output[i] + zbuffer[i] + 256) % MOD;
            }
            acc = (acc + frameAcc) % MOD;

            final int tmp2 = cA;
            cA = cA - ((5 * sA) >> 7);
            sA = sA + ((5 * tmp2) >> 7);
            final int norm2 = (3145728 - cA * cA - sA * sA) >> 11;
            cA = (cA * norm2) >> 10;
            sA = (sA * norm2) >> 10;

            final int tmp3 = cB;
            cB = cB - ((5 * sB) >> 8);
            sB = sB + ((5 * tmp3) >> 8);
            final int norm3 = (3145728 - cB * cB - sB * sB) >> 11;
            cB = (cB * norm3) >> 10;
            sB = (sB * norm3) >> 10;
        }

        return acc;
    }
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        final int frames = 160;
        final int result = donut(frames);
        System.out.println(result);
    }
}

const MOD = 100000007;
const WIDTH = 80;
const HEIGHT = 25;
const BUFFER_SIZE = WIDTH * HEIGHT;
const PALETTE_MAX = 11;
const R1 = 1;
const R2 = 2048;
const K2 = 5120 * 1024;

function idiv(a, b) {
  return Math.trunc(a / b);
}

function donut(frames) {
  const output = Array(BUFFER_SIZE).fill(0);
  const zbuffer = Array(BUFFER_SIZE).fill(127);
  let sA = 1024;
  let cA = 0;
  let sB = 1024;
  let cB = 0;
  let acc = 0;

  for (let frame = 0; frame < frames; frame += 1) {
    output.fill(0);
    zbuffer.fill(127);

    let sj = 0;
    let cj = 1024;
    let j = 0;
    while (j < 90) {
      let si = 0;
      let ci = 1024;
      let i = 0;
      while (i < 324) {
        const x0 = R1 * cj + R2;
        const x1 = (ci * x0) >> 10;
        const x2 = (cA * sj) >> 10;
        const x3 = (si * x0) >> 10;
        const x4 = R1 * x2 - ((sA * x3) >> 10);
        const x5 = (sA * sj) >> 10;
        const x6 = K2 + R1 * 1024 * x5 + cA * x3;
        const x7 = (cj * si) >> 10;

        const x = 40 + idiv(30 * (cB * x1 - sB * x4), x6);
        const y = 12 + idiv(15 * (cB * x4 + sB * x1), x6);

        const n0 =
          0 -
          cA * x7 -
          cB * (((0 - sA * x7) >> 10) + x2) -
          ci * ((cj * sB) >> 10);
        const n1 = n0 >> 10;
        const N = (n1 - x5) >> 7;

        if (y < HEIGHT && y > 0 && x > 0 && x < WIDTH) {
          const o = x + WIDTH * y;
          const zz = (x6 - K2) >> 15;
          if (zz < zbuffer[o]) {
            zbuffer[o] = zz;
            let shade = N > 0 ? N : 0;
            if (shade > PALETTE_MAX) shade = PALETTE_MAX;
            output[o] = shade + 1;
          }
        }

        const tmp0 = ci;
        ci = ci - ((5 * si) >> 8);
        si = si + ((5 * tmp0) >> 8);
        const norm0 = (3145728 - ci * ci - si * si) >> 11;
        ci = (ci * norm0) >> 10;
        si = (si * norm0) >> 10;
        i += 1;
      }

      const tmp1 = cj;
      cj = cj - ((9 * sj) >> 7);
      sj = sj + ((9 * tmp1) >> 7);
      const norm1 = (3145728 - cj * cj - sj * sj) >> 11;
      cj = (cj * norm1) >> 10;
      sj = (sj * norm1) >> 10;
      j += 1;
    }

    let frameAcc = frame + 1;
    for (let i = 0; i < BUFFER_SIZE; i += 1) {
      frameAcc = (frameAcc + (i + 1) * output[i] + zbuffer[i] + 256) % MOD;
    }
    acc = (acc + frameAcc) % MOD;

    const tmp2 = cA;
    cA = cA - ((5 * sA) >> 7);
    sA = sA + ((5 * tmp2) >> 7);
    const norm2 = (3145728 - cA * cA - sA * sA) >> 11;
    cA = (cA * norm2) >> 10;
    sA = (sA * norm2) >> 10;

    const tmp3 = cB;
    cB = cB - ((5 * sB) >> 8);
    sB = sB + ((5 * tmp3) >> 8);
    const norm3 = (3145728 - cB * cB - sB * sB) >> 11;
    cB = (cB * norm3) >> 10;
    sB = (sB * norm3) >> 10;
  }

  return acc;
}

process.stdout.write(`${result}
`);

ASCII Donut / Lua

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/lua/workloads/donut.lua 

local MOD = 100000007
local WIDTH = 80
local HEIGHT = 25
local BUFFER_SIZE = WIDTH * HEIGHT
local PALETTE_MAX = 11
local R1 = 1
local R2 = 2048
local K2 = 5120 * 1024

local function i32(n)
  n = n % 4294967296
  if n >= 2147483648 then
    n = n - 4294967296
  end
  return n
end

-- signed arithmetic right shift, matching Java/JS/C++ signed >>
local function sar(n, bits)
  n = i32(n)
  return math.floor(n / (2 ^ bits))
end

-- truncates toward zero, matching Java/C++ integer division and JS Math.trunc
local function idiv(a, b)
  local q = a / b
  if q < 0 then
    return math.ceil(q)
  end
  return math.floor(q)
end

local function donut(frames)
  frames = tonumber(frames)

  local output = {}
  local zbuffer = {}

  local s_a = 1024
  local c_a = 0
  local s_b = 1024
  local c_b = 0
  local acc = 0

  for i = 1, BUFFER_SIZE do
    output[i] = 0
    zbuffer[i] = 127
  end

  for frame = 0, frames - 1 do
    for i = 1, BUFFER_SIZE do
      output[i] = 0
      zbuffer[i] = 127
    end

    local sj = 0
    local cj = 1024
    local j = 0

    while j < 90 do
      local si = 0
      local ci = 1024
      local i = 0

      while i < 324 do
        local x0 = R1 * cj + R2
        local x1 = sar(ci * x0, 10)
        local x2 = sar(c_a * sj, 10)
        local x3 = sar(si * x0, 10)
        local x4 = R1 * x2 - sar(s_a * x3, 10)
        local x5 = sar(s_a * sj, 10)
        local x6 = K2 + R1 * 1024 * x5 + c_a * x3
        local x7 = sar(cj * si, 10)

        local x = 40 + idiv(30 * (c_b * x1 - s_b * x4), x6)
        local y = 12 + idiv(15 * (c_b * x4 + s_b * x1), x6)

        local n0 =
          0
          - c_a * x7
          - c_b * (sar(0 - s_a * x7, 10) + x2)
          - ci * sar(cj * s_b, 10)

        local n1 = sar(n0, 10)
        local shade_n = sar(n1 - x5, 7)

        if y < HEIGHT and y > 0 and x > 0 and x < WIDTH then
          local o = x + WIDTH * y + 1
          local zz = sar(x6 - K2, 15)

          if zz < zbuffer[o] then
            zbuffer[o] = zz

            local shade = shade_n
            if shade < 0 then
              shade = 0
            end
            if shade > PALETTE_MAX then
              shade = PALETTE_MAX
            end

            output[o] = shade + 1
          end
        end

        local tmp0 = ci
        ci = ci - sar(5 * si, 8)
        si = si + sar(5 * tmp0, 8)

        local norm0 = sar(3145728 - ci * ci - si * si, 11)
        ci = sar(ci * norm0, 10)
        si = sar(si * norm0, 10)

        i = i + 1
      end

      local tmp1 = cj
      cj = cj - sar(9 * sj, 7)
      sj = sj + sar(9 * tmp1, 7)

      local norm1 = sar(3145728 - cj * cj - sj * sj, 11)
      cj = sar(cj * norm1, 10)
      sj = sar(sj * norm1, 10)

      j = j + 1
    end

    local frame_acc = frame + 1
    for i = 1, BUFFER_SIZE do
      frame_acc = (frame_acc + i * output[i] + zbuffer[i] + 256) % MOD
    end
    acc = (acc + frame_acc) % MOD

    local tmp2 = c_a
    c_a = c_a - sar(5 * s_a, 7)
    s_a = s_a + sar(5 * tmp2, 7)

    local norm2 = sar(3145728 - c_a * c_a - s_a * s_a, 11)
    c_a = sar(c_a * norm2, 10)
    s_a = sar(s_a * norm2, 10)

    local tmp3 = c_b
    c_b = c_b - sar(5 * s_b, 8)
    s_b = s_b + sar(5 * tmp3, 8)

    local norm3 = sar(3145728 - c_b * c_b - s_b * s_b, 11)
    c_b = sar(c_b * norm3, 10)
    s_b = sar(s_b * norm3, 10)
  end

  return acc
end

local FRAMES = 160
local result = donut(FRAMES)
print(result)

let mod_value = 100000007

let width = 80

let height = 25

let buffer_size = width * height

let palette_max = 11

let r1 = 1

let r2 = 2048

let k2 = 5120 * 1024

let imod x = x mod mod_value

let donut frames =
  let output = Array.make buffer_size 0 in
  let zbuffer = Array.make buffer_size 127 in
  let s_a = ref 1024 in
  let c_a = ref 0 in
  let s_b = ref 1024 in
  let c_b = ref 0 in
  let acc = ref 0 in
  for frame = 0 to frames - 1 do
    Array.fill output 0 buffer_size 0;
    Array.fill zbuffer 0 buffer_size 127;
    let sj = ref 0 in
    let cj = ref 1024 in
    let j = ref 0 in
    while !j < 90 do
      let si = ref 0 in
      let ci = ref 1024 in
      let i = ref 0 in
      while !i < 324 do
        let x0 = (r1 * !cj) + r2 in
        let x1 = (!ci * x0) asr 10 in
        let x2 = (!c_a * !sj) asr 10 in
        let x3 = (!si * x0) asr 10 in
        let x4 = (r1 * x2) - ((!s_a * x3) asr 10) in
        let x5 = (!s_a * !sj) asr 10 in
        let x6 = k2 + (r1 * 1024 * x5) + (!c_a * x3) in
        let x7 = (!cj * !si) asr 10 in
        let x = 40 + ((30 * ((!c_b * x1) - (!s_b * x4))) / x6) in
        let y = 12 + ((15 * ((!c_b * x4) + (!s_b * x1))) / x6) in
        let n0 = 0 - (!c_a * x7) - (!c_b * (((0 - (!s_a * x7)) asr 10) + x2)) - (!ci * ((!cj * !s_b) asr 10)) in
        let n1 = n0 asr 10 in
        let n = (n1 - x5) asr 7 in
        if y < height && y > 0 && x > 0 && x < width then (
          let o = x + (width * y) in
          let zz = (x6 - k2) asr 15 in
          if zz < zbuffer.(o) then (
            zbuffer.(o) <- zz;
            let shade = ref (if n > 0 then n else 0) in
            if !shade > palette_max then shade := palette_max;
            output.(o) <- !shade + 1))
        ;
        let tmp0 = !ci in
        ci := !ci - ((5 * !si) asr 8);
        si := !si + ((5 * tmp0) asr 8);
        let norm0 = (3145728 - (!ci * !ci) - (!si * !si)) asr 11 in
        ci := (!ci * norm0) asr 10;
        si := (!si * norm0) asr 10;
        incr i
      done;
      let tmp1 = !cj in
      cj := !cj - ((9 * !sj) asr 7);
      sj := !sj + ((9 * tmp1) asr 7);
      let norm1 = (3145728 - (!cj * !cj) - (!sj * !sj)) asr 11 in
      cj := (!cj * norm1) asr 10;
      sj := (!sj * norm1) asr 10;
      incr j
    done;
    let frame_acc = ref (frame + 1) in
    for i = 0 to buffer_size - 1 do
      frame_acc := imod (!frame_acc + ((i + 1) * output.(i)) + zbuffer.(i) + 256)
    done;
    acc := imod (!acc + !frame_acc);
    let tmp2 = !c_a in
    c_a := !c_a - ((5 * !s_a) asr 7);
    s_a := !s_a + ((5 * tmp2) asr 7);
    let norm2 = (3145728 - (!c_a * !c_a) - (!s_a * !s_a)) asr 11 in
    c_a := (!c_a * norm2) asr 10;
    s_a := (!s_a * norm2) asr 10;
    let tmp3 = !c_b in
    c_b := !c_b - ((5 * !s_b) asr 8);
    s_b := !s_b + ((5 * tmp3) asr 8);
    let norm3 = (3145728 - (!c_b * !c_b) - (!s_b * !s_b)) asr 11 in
    c_b := (!c_b * norm3) asr 10;
    s_b := (!s_b * norm3) asr 10
  done;
  !acc

let parse_int s = int_of_string s

  let result = string_of_int (donut frames) in
  print_endline result

ASCII Donut / Perl

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/perl/workloads/donut.pl 

use strict;
use warnings;
use POSIX qw(floor);

use constant MOD => 100000007;
use constant WIDTH => 80;
use constant HEIGHT => 25;
use constant BUFFER_SIZE => WIDTH * HEIGHT;
use constant PALETTE_MAX => 11;
use constant R1 => 1;
use constant R2 => 2048;
use constant K2 => 5120 * 1024;
use constant U32 => 4294967296;
use constant I32 => 2147483648;

sub parse_args {
    my (@argv) = @_;
    return \@argv;
}

sub idiv {
    my ($a, $b) = @_;
    my $q = $a / $b;
    return $q < 0 ? int($q + 0.0) : int($q);
}

sub i32 {
    my ($n) = @_;
    $n %= U32;
    $n -= U32 if $n >= I32;
    return $n;
}

sub sar {
    my ($n, $bits) = @_;
    $n = i32($n);
    return floor($n / (2 ** $bits));
}

sub donut {
    my ($frames) = @_;
    my @output = (0) x BUFFER_SIZE;
    my @zbuffer = (127) x BUFFER_SIZE;
    my $s_a = 1024;
    my $c_a = 0;
    my $s_b = 1024;
    my $c_b = 0;
    my $acc = 0;

    for (my $frame = 0; $frame < $frames; $frame += 1) {
        for (my $i = 0; $i < BUFFER_SIZE; $i += 1) {
            $output[$i] = 0;
            $zbuffer[$i] = 127;
        }

        my $sj = 0;
        my $cj = 1024;
        my $j = 0;
        while ($j < 90) {
            my $si = 0;
            my $ci = 1024;
            my $i = 0;
            while ($i < 324) {
                my $x0 = R1 * $cj + R2;
                my $x1 = sar($ci * $x0, 10);
                my $x2 = sar($c_a * $sj, 10);
                my $x3 = sar($si * $x0, 10);
                my $x4 = R1 * $x2 - sar($s_a * $x3, 10);
                my $x5 = sar($s_a * $sj, 10);
                my $x6 = K2 + R1 * 1024 * $x5 + $c_a * $x3;
                my $x7 = sar($cj * $si, 10);

                my $x = 40 + idiv(30 * ($c_b * $x1 - $s_b * $x4), $x6);
                my $y = 12 + idiv(15 * ($c_b * $x4 + $s_b * $x1), $x6);

                my $n0 = 0 - $c_a * $x7 - $c_b * (sar(0 - $s_a * $x7, 10) + $x2) - $ci * sar($cj * $s_b, 10);
                my $n1 = sar($n0, 10);
                my $shade_n = sar($n1 - $x5, 7);

                if ($y < HEIGHT && $y > 0 && $x > 0 && $x < WIDTH) {
                    my $o = $x + WIDTH * $y;
                    my $zz = sar($x6 - K2, 15);
                    if ($zz < $zbuffer[$o]) {
                        $zbuffer[$o] = $zz;
                        my $shade = $shade_n > 0 ? $shade_n : 0;
                        $shade = PALETTE_MAX if $shade > PALETTE_MAX;
                        $output[$o] = $shade + 1;
                    }
                }

                my $tmp0 = $ci;
                $ci = $ci - sar(5 * $si, 8);
                $si = $si + sar(5 * $tmp0, 8);
                my $norm0 = sar(3145728 - $ci * $ci - $si * $si, 11);
                $ci = sar($ci * $norm0, 10);
                $si = sar($si * $norm0, 10);
                $i += 1;
            }

            my $tmp1 = $cj;
            $cj = $cj - sar(9 * $sj, 7);
            $sj = $sj + sar(9 * $tmp1, 7);
            my $norm1 = sar(3145728 - $cj * $cj - $sj * $sj, 11);
            $cj = sar($cj * $norm1, 10);
            $sj = sar($sj * $norm1, 10);
            $j += 1;
        }

        my $frame_acc = $frame + 1;
        for (my $i = 0; $i < BUFFER_SIZE; $i += 1) {
            $frame_acc = ($frame_acc + ($i + 1) * $output[$i] + $zbuffer[$i] + 256) % MOD;
        }
        $acc = ($acc + $frame_acc) % MOD;

        my $tmp2 = $c_a;
        $c_a = $c_a - sar(5 * $s_a, 7);
        $s_a = $s_a + sar(5 * $tmp2, 7);
        my $norm2 = sar(3145728 - $c_a * $c_a - $s_a * $s_a, 11);
        $c_a = sar($c_a * $norm2, 10);
        $s_a = sar($s_a * $norm2, 10);

        my $tmp3 = $c_b;
        $c_b = $c_b - sar(5 * $s_b, 8);
        $s_b = $s_b + sar(5 * $tmp3, 8);
        my $norm3 = sar(3145728 - $c_b * $c_b - $s_b * $s_b, 11);
        $c_b = sar($c_b * $norm3, 10);
        $s_b = sar($s_b * $norm3, 10);
    }

    return $acc;
}

my $FRAMES = 160;
my $result = donut(0 + $FRAMES);
print "$result\n";

ASCII Donut / PHP

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/php/workloads/donut.php 

<?php

const MOD = 100000007;
const WIDTH = 80;
const HEIGHT = 25;
const BUFFER_SIZE = WIDTH * HEIGHT;
const PALETTE_MAX = 11;
const R1 = 1;
const R2 = 2048;
const K2 = 5120 * 1024;

function donut(int $frames): int {
    $output = array_fill(0, BUFFER_SIZE, 0);
    $zbuffer = array_fill(0, BUFFER_SIZE, 127);
    $sA = 1024;
    $cA = 0;
    $sB = 1024;
    $cB = 0;
    $acc = 0;

    for ($frame = 0; $frame < $frames; $frame += 1) {
        for ($i = 0; $i < BUFFER_SIZE; $i += 1) {
            $output[$i] = 0;
            $zbuffer[$i] = 127;
        }

        $sj = 0;
        $cj = 1024;
        $j = 0;
        while ($j < 90) {
            $si = 0;
            $ci = 1024;
            $i = 0;
            while ($i < 324) {
                $x0 = R1 * $cj + R2;
                $x1 = ($ci * $x0) >> 10;
                $x2 = ($cA * $sj) >> 10;
                $x3 = ($si * $x0) >> 10;
                $x4 = R1 * $x2 - (($sA * $x3) >> 10);
                $x5 = ($sA * $sj) >> 10;
                $x6 = K2 + R1 * 1024 * $x5 + $cA * $x3;
                $x7 = ($cj * $si) >> 10;

                $x = 40 + intdiv(30 * ($cB * $x1 - $sB * $x4), $x6);
                $y = 12 + intdiv(15 * ($cB * $x4 + $sB * $x1), $x6);

                $n0 = 0 - $cA * $x7 - $cB * (((0 - $sA * $x7) >> 10) + $x2) - $ci * (($cj * $sB) >> 10);
                $n1 = $n0 >> 10;
                $shadeN = ($n1 - $x5) >> 7;

                if ($y < HEIGHT && $y > 0 && $x > 0 && $x < WIDTH) {
                    $o = $x + WIDTH * $y;
                    $zz = ($x6 - K2) >> 15;
                    if ($zz < $zbuffer[$o]) {
                        $zbuffer[$o] = $zz;
                        $shade = $shadeN;
                        if ($shade < 0) {
                            $shade = 0;
                        }
                        if ($shade > PALETTE_MAX) {
                            $shade = PALETTE_MAX;
                        }
                        $output[$o] = $shade + 1;
                    }
                }

                $tmp0 = $ci;
                $ci = $ci - ((5 * $si) >> 8);
                $si = $si + ((5 * $tmp0) >> 8);
                $norm0 = (3145728 - $ci * $ci - $si * $si) >> 11;
                $ci = ($ci * $norm0) >> 10;
                $si = ($si * $norm0) >> 10;
                $i += 1;
            }

            $tmp1 = $cj;
            $cj = $cj - ((9 * $sj) >> 7);
            $sj = $sj + ((9 * $tmp1) >> 7);
            $norm1 = (3145728 - $cj * $cj - $sj * $sj) >> 11;
            $cj = ($cj * $norm1) >> 10;
            $sj = ($sj * $norm1) >> 10;
            $j += 1;
        }

        $frameAcc = $frame + 1;
        for ($i = 0; $i < BUFFER_SIZE; $i += 1) {
            $frameAcc = ($frameAcc + ($i + 1) * $output[$i] + $zbuffer[$i] + 256) % MOD;
        }
        $acc = ($acc + $frameAcc) % MOD;

        $tmp2 = $cA;
        $cA = $cA - ((5 * $sA) >> 7);
        $sA = $sA + ((5 * $tmp2) >> 7);
        $norm2 = (3145728 - $cA * $cA - $sA * $sA) >> 11;
        $cA = ($cA * $norm2) >> 10;
        $sA = ($sA * $norm2) >> 10;

        $tmp3 = $cB;
        $cB = $cB - ((5 * $sB) >> 8);
        $sB = $sB + ((5 * $tmp3) >> 8);
        $norm3 = (3145728 - $cB * $cB - $sB * $sB) >> 11;
        $cB = ($cB * $norm3) >> 10;
        $sB = ($sB * $norm3) >> 10;
    }

    return $acc;
}

$FRAMES = 160;
$result = donut((int) $FRAMES);
echo $result, PHP_EOL;

#!/usr/bin/env python3

from __future__ import annotations

import sys


MOD = 100000007
WIDTH = 80
HEIGHT = 25
BUFFER_SIZE = WIDTH * HEIGHT
PALETTE_MAX = 11
R1 = 1
R2 = 2048
K2 = 5120 * 1024


def idiv(a: int, b: int) -> int:
    return int(a / b)


def donut(frames: int) -> int:
    output = [0] * BUFFER_SIZE
    zbuffer = [127] * BUFFER_SIZE
    s_a = 1024
    c_a = 0
    s_b = 1024
    c_b = 0
    acc = 0

    for frame in range(frames):
        for i in range(BUFFER_SIZE):
            output[i] = 0
            zbuffer[i] = 127

        sj = 0
        cj = 1024
        j = 0
        while j < 90:
            si = 0
            ci = 1024
            i = 0
            while i < 324:
                x0 = R1 * cj + R2
                x1 = (ci * x0) >> 10
                x2 = (c_a * sj) >> 10
                x3 = (si * x0) >> 10
                x4 = R1 * x2 - ((s_a * x3) >> 10)
                x5 = (s_a * sj) >> 10
                x6 = K2 + R1 * 1024 * x5 + c_a * x3
                x7 = (cj * si) >> 10

                x = 40 + idiv(30 * (c_b * x1 - s_b * x4), x6)
                y = 12 + idiv(15 * (c_b * x4 + s_b * x1), x6)

                n0 = 0 - c_a * x7 - c_b * (((0 - s_a * x7) >> 10) + x2) - ci * ((cj * s_b) >> 10)
                n1 = n0 >> 10
                shade_n = (n1 - x5) >> 7

                if y < HEIGHT and y > 0 and x > 0 and x < WIDTH:
                    o = x + WIDTH * y
                    zz = (x6 - K2) >> 15
                    if zz < zbuffer[o]:
                        zbuffer[o] = zz
                        shade = shade_n if shade_n > 0 else 0
                        if shade > PALETTE_MAX:
                            shade = PALETTE_MAX
                        output[o] = shade + 1

                tmp0 = ci
                ci = ci - ((5 * si) >> 8)
                si = si + ((5 * tmp0) >> 8)
                norm0 = (3145728 - ci * ci - si * si) >> 11
                ci = (ci * norm0) >> 10
                si = (si * norm0) >> 10
                i += 1

            tmp1 = cj
            cj = cj - ((9 * sj) >> 7)
            sj = sj + ((9 * tmp1) >> 7)
            norm1 = (3145728 - cj * cj - sj * sj) >> 11
            cj = (cj * norm1) >> 10
            sj = (sj * norm1) >> 10
            j += 1

        frame_acc = frame + 1
        for i in range(BUFFER_SIZE):
            frame_acc = (frame_acc + (i + 1) * output[i] + zbuffer[i] + 256) % MOD
        acc = (acc + frame_acc) % MOD

        tmp2 = c_a
        c_a = c_a - ((5 * s_a) >> 7)
        s_a = s_a + ((5 * tmp2) >> 7)
        norm2 = (3145728 - c_a * c_a - s_a * s_a) >> 11
        c_a = (c_a * norm2) >> 10
        s_a = (s_a * norm2) >> 10

        tmp3 = c_b
        c_b = c_b - ((5 * s_b) >> 8)
        s_b = s_b + ((5 * tmp3) >> 8)
        norm3 = (3145728 - c_b * c_b - s_b * s_b) >> 11
        c_b = (c_b * norm3) >> 10
        s_b = (s_b * norm3) >> 10

    return acc

ASCII Donut / R

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/r/workloads/donut.R 

#!/usr/bin/env Rscript

MOD <- 100000007
WIDTH <- 80
HEIGHT <- 25
BUFFER_SIZE <- WIDTH * HEIGHT
PALETTE_MAX <- 11
R1 <- 1
R2 <- 2048
K2 <- 5120 * 1024

idiv <- function(a, b) {
  trunc(a / b)
}

shr <- function(n, bits) {
  floor(n / (2 ^ bits))
}

donut <- function(frames) {
  output <- integer(BUFFER_SIZE)
  zbuffer <- integer(BUFFER_SIZE)
  s_a <- 1024
  c_a <- 0
  s_b <- 1024
  c_b <- 0
  acc <- 0

  for (frame in 0:(frames - 1)) {
    output[] <- 0L
    zbuffer[] <- 127L

    sj <- 0
    cj <- 1024
    j <- 0
    while (j < 90) {
      si <- 0
      ci <- 1024
      i <- 0
      while (i < 324) {
        x0 <- R1 * cj + R2
        x1 <- shr(ci * x0, 10)
        x2 <- shr(c_a * sj, 10)
        x3 <- shr(si * x0, 10)
        x4 <- R1 * x2 - shr(s_a * x3, 10)
        x5 <- shr(s_a * sj, 10)
        x6 <- K2 + R1 * 1024 * x5 + c_a * x3
        x7 <- shr(cj * si, 10)

        x <- 40 + idiv(30 * (c_b * x1 - s_b * x4), x6)
        y <- 12 + idiv(15 * (c_b * x4 + s_b * x1), x6)

        n0 <- 0 - c_a * x7 - c_b * (shr(0 - s_a * x7, 10) + x2) - ci * shr(cj * s_b, 10)
        n1 <- shr(n0, 10)
        shade_n <- shr(n1 - x5, 7)

        if (y < HEIGHT && y > 0 && x > 0 && x < WIDTH) {
          o0 <- x + WIDTH * y
          zz <- shr(x6 - K2, 15)
          if (zz < zbuffer[[o0 + 1]]) {
            zbuffer[[o0 + 1]] <- zz
            shade <- if (shade_n > 0) shade_n else 0
            if (shade > PALETTE_MAX) shade <- PALETTE_MAX
            output[[o0 + 1]] <- shade + 1
          }
        }

        tmp0 <- ci
        ci <- ci - shr(5 * si, 8)
        si <- si + shr(5 * tmp0, 8)
        norm0 <- shr(3145728 - ci * ci - si * si, 11)
        ci <- shr(ci * norm0, 10)
        si <- shr(si * norm0, 10)
        i <- i + 1
      }

      tmp1 <- cj
      cj <- cj - shr(9 * sj, 7)
      sj <- sj + shr(9 * tmp1, 7)
      norm1 <- shr(3145728 - cj * cj - sj * sj, 11)
      cj <- shr(cj * norm1, 10)
      sj <- shr(sj * norm1, 10)
      j <- j + 1
    }

    frame_acc <- frame + 1
    for (i0 in 0:(BUFFER_SIZE - 1)) {
      frame_acc <- (frame_acc + (i0 + 1) * output[[i0 + 1]] + zbuffer[[i0 + 1]] + 256) %% MOD
    }
    acc <- (acc + frame_acc) %% MOD

    tmp2 <- c_a
    c_a <- c_a - shr(5 * s_a, 7)
    s_a <- s_a + shr(5 * tmp2, 7)
    norm2 <- shr(3145728 - c_a * c_a - s_a * s_a, 11)
    c_a <- shr(c_a * norm2, 10)
    s_a <- shr(s_a * norm2, 10)

    tmp3 <- c_b
    c_b <- c_b - shr(5 * s_b, 8)
    s_b <- s_b + shr(5 * tmp3, 8)
    norm3 <- shr(3145728 - c_b * c_b - s_b * s_b, 11)
    c_b <- shr(c_b * norm3, 10)
    s_b <- shr(s_b * norm3, 10)
  }

  acc
}

args <- commandArgs(trailingOnly = TRUE)
frames <- 160
result <- donut(frames)
cat(as.integer(result), "\n", sep = "")

MOD = 100_000_007
WIDTH = 80
HEIGHT = 25
BUFFER_SIZE = WIDTH * HEIGHT
PALETTE_MAX = 11
R1 = 1
R2 = 2048
K2 = 5120 * 1024

def idiv(a, b)
  quotient = a / b
  remainder = a % b
  return quotient if remainder.zero? || (a >= 0) == (b >= 0)

  quotient + 1
end

def donut(frames)
  output = Array.new(BUFFER_SIZE, 0)
  zbuffer = Array.new(BUFFER_SIZE, 127)
  s_a = 1024
  c_a = 0
  s_b = 1024
  c_b = 0
  acc = 0
  frame = 0

    output.fill(0)
    zbuffer.fill(127)
    sj = 0
    cj = 1024
    j = 0
    while j < 90
      si = 0
      ci = 1024
      i = 0
      while i < 324
        x0 = R1 * cj + R2
        x1 = (ci * x0) >> 10
        x2 = (c_a * sj) >> 10
        x3 = (si * x0) >> 10
        x4 = R1 * x2 - ((s_a * x3) >> 10)
        x5 = (s_a * sj) >> 10
        x6 = K2 + (R1 * 1024 * x5) + (c_a * x3)
        x7 = (cj * si) >> 10
        x = 40 + idiv(30 * (c_b * x1 - s_b * x4), x6)
        y = 12 + idiv(15 * (c_b * x4 + s_b * x1), x6)
        n0 = -c_a * x7 - c_b * (((-s_a * x7) >> 10) + x2) - ci * ((cj * s_b) >> 10)
        n1 = n0 >> 10
        n = (n1 - x5) >> 7
        if y < HEIGHT && y > 0 && x > 0 && x < WIDTH
          o = x + WIDTH * y
          zz = (x6 - K2) >> 15
          if zz < zbuffer[o]
            zbuffer[o] = zz
            shade = n > 0 ? n : 0
            shade = PALETTE_MAX if shade > PALETTE_MAX
            output[o] = shade + 1
          end
        end
        tmp0 = ci
        ci -= (5 * si) >> 8
        si += (5 * tmp0) >> 8
        norm0 = (3_145_728 - ci * ci - si * si) >> 11
        ci = (ci * norm0) >> 10
        si = (si * norm0) >> 10
        i += 1
      end
      tmp1 = cj
      cj -= (9 * sj) >> 7
      sj += (9 * tmp1) >> 7
      norm1 = (3_145_728 - cj * cj - sj * sj) >> 11
      cj = (cj * norm1) >> 10
      sj = (sj * norm1) >> 10
      j += 1
    end
    frame_acc = frame + 1
    i = 0
    while i < BUFFER_SIZE
      frame_acc = (frame_acc + (i + 1) * output[i] + zbuffer[i] + 256) % MOD
      i += 1
    end
    acc = (acc + frame_acc) % MOD
    tmp2 = c_a
    c_a -= (5 * s_a) >> 7
    s_a += (5 * tmp2) >> 7
    norm2 = (3_145_728 - c_a * c_a - s_a * s_a) >> 11
    c_a = (c_a * norm2) >> 10
    s_a = (s_a * norm2) >> 10
    tmp3 = c_b
    c_b -= (5 * s_b) >> 8
    s_b += (5 * tmp3) >> 8
    norm3 = (3_145_728 - c_b * c_b - s_b * s_b) >> 11
    c_b = (c_b * norm3) >> 10
    s_b = (s_b * norm3) >> 10
    frame += 1
  end
  acc
end

ASCII Donut / Rust

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/rust/src/bin/donut.rs 

const MOD: i32 = 100_000_007;
const WIDTH: i32 = 80;
const HEIGHT: i32 = 25;
const BUFFER_SIZE: usize = (WIDTH as usize) * (HEIGHT as usize);
const PALETTE_MAX: i32 = 11;
const R1: i32 = 1;
const R2: i32 = 2048;
const K2: i32 = 5120 * 1024;

fn donut(frames: i32) -> i32 {
    let mut output = vec![0_i32; BUFFER_SIZE];
    let mut zbuffer = vec![127_i32; BUFFER_SIZE];
    let mut s_a = 1024_i32;
    let mut c_a = 0_i32;
    let mut s_b = 1024_i32;
    let mut c_b = 0_i32;
    let mut acc = 0_i32;

    for frame in 0..frames {
        output.fill(0);
        zbuffer.fill(127);

        let mut sj = 0_i32;
        let mut cj = 1024_i32;
        let mut j = 0_i32;
        while j < 90 {
            let mut si = 0_i32;
            let mut ci = 1024_i32;
            let mut i = 0_i32;
            while i < 324 {
                let x0 = R1 * cj + R2;
                let x1 = (ci * x0) >> 10;
                let x2 = (c_a * sj) >> 10;
                let x3 = (si * x0) >> 10;
                let x4 = R1 * x2 - ((s_a * x3) >> 10);
                let x5 = (s_a * sj) >> 10;
                let x6 = K2 + R1 * 1024 * x5 + c_a * x3;
                let x7 = (cj * si) >> 10;

                let x = 40 + (30 * (c_b * x1 - s_b * x4)) / x6;
                let y = 12 + (15 * (c_b * x4 + s_b * x1)) / x6;

                let n0 =
                    0 - c_a * x7 - c_b * (((0 - s_a * x7) >> 10) + x2) - ci * ((cj * s_b) >> 10);
                let n1 = n0 >> 10;
                let n = (n1 - x5) >> 7;

                if y < HEIGHT && y > 0 && x > 0 && x < WIDTH {
                    let o = (x + WIDTH * y) as usize;
                    let zz = (x6 - K2) >> 15;
                    if zz < zbuffer[o] {
                        zbuffer[o] = zz;
                        let mut shade = if n > 0 { n } else { 0 };
                        if shade > PALETTE_MAX {
                            shade = PALETTE_MAX;
                        }
                        output[o] = shade + 1;
                    }
                }

                let tmp0 = ci;
                ci = ci - ((5 * si) >> 8);
                si = si + ((5 * tmp0) >> 8);
                let norm0 = (3_145_728 - ci * ci - si * si) >> 11;
                ci = (ci * norm0) >> 10;
                si = (si * norm0) >> 10;
                i += 1;
            }

            let tmp1 = cj;
            cj = cj - ((9 * sj) >> 7);
            sj = sj + ((9 * tmp1) >> 7);
            let norm1 = (3_145_728 - cj * cj - sj * sj) >> 11;
            cj = (cj * norm1) >> 10;
            sj = (sj * norm1) >> 10;
            j += 1;
        }

        let mut frame_acc = frame + 1;
        for i in 0..BUFFER_SIZE {
            frame_acc = (frame_acc + ((i as i32) + 1) * output[i] + zbuffer[i] + 256) % MOD;
        }
        acc = (acc + frame_acc) % MOD;

        let tmp2 = c_a;
        c_a = c_a - ((5 * s_a) >> 7);
        s_a = s_a + ((5 * tmp2) >> 7);
        let norm2 = (3_145_728 - c_a * c_a - s_a * s_a) >> 11;
        c_a = (c_a * norm2) >> 10;
        s_a = (s_a * norm2) >> 10;

        let tmp3 = c_b;
        c_b = c_b - ((5 * s_b) >> 8);
        s_b = s_b + ((5 * tmp3) >> 8);
        let norm3 = (3_145_728 - c_b * c_b - s_b * s_b) >> 11;
        c_b = (c_b * norm3) >> 10;
        s_b = (s_b * norm3) >> 10;
    }

    acc
}


fn main() {
    let frames = 160;
    let result = donut(frames);
    println!("{}", result);
}

object Donut {
  private final val Mod = 100000007
  private final val Width = 80
  private final val Height = 25
  private final val BufferSize = Width * Height
  private final val PaletteMax = 11
  private final val R1 = 1
  private final val R2 = 2048
  private final val K2 = 5120 * 1024

  private def donut(frames: Int): Int = {
    val output = Array.fill(BufferSize)(0)
    val zbuffer = Array.fill(BufferSize)(127)
    var sA = 1024
    var cA = 0
    var sB = 1024
    var cB = 0
    var acc = 0
    var frame = 0

    while (frame < frames) {
      var i = 0
      while (i < BufferSize) {
        output(i) = 0
        zbuffer(i) = 127
        i += 1
      }

      var sj = 0
      var cj = 1024
      var j = 0
      while (j < 90) {
        var si = 0
        var ci = 1024
        i = 0
        while (i < 324) {
          val x0 = R1 * cj + R2
          val x1 = (ci * x0) >> 10
          val x2 = (cA * sj) >> 10
          val x3 = (si * x0) >> 10
          val x4 = R1 * x2 - ((sA * x3) >> 10)
          val x5 = (sA * sj) >> 10
          val x6 = K2 + R1 * 1024 * x5 + cA * x3
          val x7 = (cj * si) >> 10

          val x = 40 + (30 * (cB * x1 - sB * x4)) / x6
          val y = 12 + (15 * (cB * x4 + sB * x1)) / x6

          val n0 = 0 - cA * x7 - cB * (((0 - sA * x7) >> 10) + x2) - ci * ((cj * sB) >> 10)
          val n1 = n0 >> 10
          val n = (n1 - x5) >> 7

          if (y < Height && y > 0 && x > 0 && x < Width) {
            val o = x + Width * y
            val zz = (x6 - K2) >> 15
            if (zz < zbuffer(o)) {
              zbuffer(o) = zz
              var shade = if (n > 0) n else 0
              if (shade > PaletteMax) shade = PaletteMax
              output(o) = shade + 1
            }
          }

          val tmp0 = ci
          ci = ci - ((5 * si) >> 8)
          si = si + ((5 * tmp0) >> 8)
          val norm0 = (3145728 - ci * ci - si * si) >> 11
          ci = (ci * norm0) >> 10
          si = (si * norm0) >> 10
          i += 1
        }

        val tmp1 = cj
        cj = cj - ((9 * sj) >> 7)
        sj = sj + ((9 * tmp1) >> 7)
        val norm1 = (3145728 - cj * cj - sj * sj) >> 11
        cj = (cj * norm1) >> 10
        sj = (sj * norm1) >> 10
        j += 1
      }

      var frameAcc = frame + 1
      i = 0
      while (i < BufferSize) {
        frameAcc = (frameAcc + (i + 1) * output(i) + zbuffer(i) + 256) % Mod
        i += 1
      }
      acc = (acc + frameAcc) % Mod

      val tmp2 = cA
      cA = cA - ((5 * sA) >> 7)
      sA = sA + ((5 * tmp2) >> 7)
      val norm2 = (3145728 - cA * cA - sA * sA) >> 11
      cA = (cA * norm2) >> 10
      sA = (sA * norm2) >> 10

      val tmp3 = cB
      cB = cB - ((5 * sB) >> 8)
      sB = sB + ((5 * tmp3) >> 8)
      val norm3 = (3145728 - cB * cB - sB * sB) >> 11
      cB = (cB * norm3) >> 10
      sB = (sB * norm3) >> 10

      frame += 1
    }

    acc
  }

  def main(args: Array[String]): Unit = {
    val frames = 160
    val result = donut(frames)
    println(result)
  }
}

ASCII Donut / Swift

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/swift/workloads/donut.swift 

let mod = 100_000_007
let width = 80
let height = 25
let bufferSize = width * height
let paletteMax = 11
let r1 = 1
let r2 = 2048
let k2 = 5120 * 1024

func donut(_ frames: Int) -> Int {
    var output = Array(repeating: 0, count: bufferSize)
    var zbuffer = Array(repeating: 127, count: bufferSize)
    var sA = 1024
    var cA = 0
    var sB = 1024
    var cB = 0
    var acc = 0

    var frame = 0
    while frame < frames {
        var i = 0
        while i < bufferSize {
            output[i] = 0
            zbuffer[i] = 127
            i += 1
        }

        var sj = 0
        var cj = 1024
        var j = 0
        while j < 90 {
            var si = 0
            var ci = 1024
            i = 0
            while i < 324 {
                let x0 = r1 * cj + r2
                let x1 = (ci * x0) >> 10
                let x2 = (cA * sj) >> 10
                let x3 = (si * x0) >> 10
                let x4 = r1 * x2 - ((sA * x3) >> 10)
                let x5 = (sA * sj) >> 10
                let x6 = k2 + r1 * 1024 * x5 + cA * x3
                let x7 = (cj * si) >> 10

                let x = 40 + (30 * (cB * x1 - sB * x4)) / x6
                let y = 12 + (15 * (cB * x4 + sB * x1)) / x6

                let n0 = 0 - cA * x7 - cB * (((0 - sA * x7) >> 10) + x2) - ci * ((cj * sB) >> 10)
                let n1 = n0 >> 10
                let shadeN = (n1 - x5) >> 7

                if y < height && y > 0 && x > 0 && x < width {
                    let o = x + width * y
                    let zz = (x6 - k2) >> 15
                    if zz < zbuffer[o] {
                        zbuffer[o] = zz
                        var shade = shadeN
                        if shade < 0 {
                            shade = 0
                        }
                        if shade > paletteMax {
                            shade = paletteMax
                        }
                        output[o] = shade + 1
                    }
                }

                let tmp0 = ci
                ci = ci - ((5 * si) >> 8)
                si = si + ((5 * tmp0) >> 8)
                let norm0 = (3145728 - ci * ci - si * si) >> 11
                ci = (ci * norm0) >> 10
                si = (si * norm0) >> 10
                i += 1
            }

            let tmp1 = cj
            cj = cj - ((9 * sj) >> 7)
            sj = sj + ((9 * tmp1) >> 7)
            let norm1 = (3145728 - cj * cj - sj * sj) >> 11
            cj = (cj * norm1) >> 10
            sj = (sj * norm1) >> 10
            j += 1
        }

        var frameAcc = frame + 1
        i = 0
        while i < bufferSize {
            frameAcc = (frameAcc + (i + 1) * output[i] + zbuffer[i] + 256) % mod
            i += 1
        }
        acc = (acc + frameAcc) % mod

        let tmp2 = cA
        cA = cA - ((5 * sA) >> 7)
        sA = sA + ((5 * tmp2) >> 7)
        let norm2 = (3145728 - cA * cA - sA * sA) >> 11
        cA = (cA * norm2) >> 10
        sA = (sA * norm2) >> 10

        let tmp3 = cB
        cB = cB - ((5 * sB) >> 8)
        sB = sB + ((5 * tmp3) >> 8)
        let norm3 = (3145728 - cB * cB - sB * sB) >> 11
        cB = (cB * norm3) >> 10
        sB = (sB * norm3) >> 10

        frame += 1
    }

    return acc
}

let frames = 160
let result = donut(frames)
print(result)

Reverse Complement / Que (my language)

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/que/reverse_complement.que 

(let MOD 100000007)

(let base-at
  (lambda (i)
    (cond
      (= (mod (+ (* i 7) 3) 4) 0) 'A'
      (= (mod (+ (* i 7) 3) 4) 1) 'C'
      (= (mod (+ (* i 7) 3) 4) 2) 'G'
      'T')))

(let complement-score
  (lambda (c)
    (cond
      (=# c 'A') 4
      (=# c 'C') 3
      (=# c 'G') 2
      1)))

(let make-dna
  (lambda (n)
    (do
      (let xs [])
      (mut i 0)
      (while (< i n)
        (do
          (set! xs (length xs) (base-at i))
          (alter! i (+ i 1))))
      xs)))

(let reverse-complement/checksum
  (lambda (xs)
    (do
      (mut i (- (length xs) 1))
      (mut pos 1)
      (mut acc 0)
      (while (>= i 0)
        (do
          (alter! acc
            (mod (+ acc (* pos (complement-score (get xs i)))) MOD))
          (alter! pos (+ pos 1))
          (alter! i (- i 1))))
      acc)))

(let N 1000000)

(reverse-complement/checksum (make-dna N))

Reverse Complement / Clojure

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/clojure/workloads/reverse_complement.clj 

(set! *unchecked-math* true)

(def mod-value 100000007)

(defn parse-int ^long [^String text]
  (Long/parseLong text))

(defn base-byte [^long i]
  (case (mod (+ (* i 7) 3) 4)
    0 (byte 65)
    1 (byte 67)
    2 (byte 71)
    (byte 84)))

(defn complement-score ^long [^long code]
  (cond
    (= code 65) 4
    (= code 67) 3
    (= code 71) 2
    :else 1))

(defn make-dna ^bytes [^long length]
  (let [data (byte-array (int length))]
    (loop [i 0]
      (when (< i length)
        (aset-byte data (int i) (base-byte i))
        (recur (unchecked-inc-int i))))
    data))

(defn reverse-complement-checksum ^long [^bytes data]
  (loop [i (dec (alength data))
         pos 1
         acc 0]
    (if (< i 0)
      acc
      (recur
        (unchecked-dec-int i)
        (unchecked-inc-int pos)
        (mod (+ acc (* pos (complement-score (bit-and 255 (aget data i))))) mod-value)))))

(let [n 1000000
      result (reverse-complement-checksum (make-dna n))]
  (println result))

Reverse Complement / C++

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/cpp/workloads/reverse_complement.cpp 

#include <cstdint>
#include <iostream>
#include <stdexcept>
#include <string>
#include <vector>

namespace {

constexpr int MOD = 100000007;
constexpr unsigned char BASES[4] = {'A', 'C', 'G', 'T'};

std::vector<unsigned char> make_dna(int length) {
    std::vector<unsigned char> data(static_cast<std::size_t>(length));
    for (int i = 0; i < length; ++i) {
        data[static_cast<std::size_t>(i)] = BASES[((i * 7) + 3) % 4];
    }
    return data;
}

int complement_score(unsigned char code) {
    if (code == 'A') return 4;
    if (code == 'C') return 3;
    if (code == 'G') return 2;
    return 1;
}

int reverse_complement_checksum(const std::vector<unsigned char>& data) {
    int acc = 0;
    int pos = 1;
    for (int i = static_cast<int>(data.size()) - 1; i >= 0; --i) {
        acc = (acc + pos * complement_score(data[static_cast<std::size_t>(i)])) % MOD;
        ++pos;
    }
    return acc;
}

}  // namespace

int main() {
    constexpr int n = 1000000;
    int result = reverse_complement_checksum(make_dna(n));
    std::cout << result << '\n';
    return 0;
}

Reverse Complement / C#

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/csharp/workloads/reverse_complement.cs 

using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;

public static class ReverseComplement
{
    private const int Mod = 100000007;
    private static readonly byte[] Bases = {65, 67, 71, 84};


    private static byte[] MakeDna(int length)
    {
        var data = new byte[length];
        for (var i = 0; i < length; i += 1)
        {
            data[i] = Bases[((i * 7) + 3) % 4];
        }
        return data;
    }

    private static int ComplementScore(byte code)
    {
        if (code == 65) return 4;
        if (code == 67) return 3;
        if (code == 71) return 2;
        return 1;
    }

    private static int ReverseComplementChecksum(byte[] data)
    {
        var acc = 0;
        var pos = 1;
        for (var i = data.Length - 1; i >= 0; i -= 1)
        {
            acc = (acc + pos * ComplementScore(data[i])) % Mod;
            pos += 1;
        }
        return acc;
    }

    public static void Main(string[] args)
    {
        const int n = 1000000;
        var result = ReverseComplementChecksum(MakeDna(n));
        Console.WriteLine(result);
    }
}

import 'dart:io';

const int modValue = 100000007;
const List<int> bases = <int>[65, 67, 71, 84];

List<int> makeDna(int length) {
  final data = List<int>.filled(length, 0);
  var i = 0;
  while (i < length) {
    data[i] = bases[(i * 7 + 3) % 4];
    i += 1;
  }
  return data;
}

int complementScore(int code) {
  if (code == 65) {
    return 4;
  }
  if (code == 67) {
    return 3;
  }
  if (code == 71) {
    return 2;
  }
  return 1;
}

int reverseComplementChecksum(List<int> data) {
  var acc = 0;
  var pos = 1;
  var i = data.length - 1;
  while (i >= 0) {
    acc = (acc + pos * complementScore(data[i])) % modValue;
    pos += 1;
    i -= 1;
  }
  return acc;
}

  const n = 1000000;
  final result = reverseComplementChecksum(makeDna(n));

}

Reverse Complement / Go

package main

import (
	"fmt"
)

const reverseComplementMod = 100000007

var reverseComplementBases = []byte{65, 67, 71, 84}

func makeDNA(length int) []byte {
	data := make([]byte, length)
	for i := 0; i < length; i += 1 {
		data[i] = reverseComplementBases[(i*7+3)%4]
	}
	return data
}

func complementScore(code byte) int {
	if code == 65 {
		return 4
	}
	if code == 67 {
		return 3
	}
	if code == 71 {
		return 2
	}
	return 1
}

func reverseComplementChecksum(data []byte) int {
	acc := 0
	pos := 1
	for i := len(data) - 1; i >= 0; i -= 1 {
		acc = (acc + pos*complementScore(data[i])) % reverseComplementMod
		pos += 1
	}
	return acc
}


func main() {
	const n = 1000000
	result := reverseComplementChecksum(makeDNA(n))
	fmt.Println(result)
}

Reverse Complement / Haskell

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/haskell/workloads/reverse_complement.hs 

module Main where

import Data.Array.IArray (bounds)
import Data.Array.Unboxed (UArray, listArray, (!))
import Data.Bits ((.&.))
import Data.Char (ord)

modValue :: Int
modValue = 100000007

bases :: UArray Int Int
bases = listArray (0, 3) [ord 'A', ord 'C', ord 'G', ord 'T']

makeDna :: Int -> UArray Int Int
makeDna lengthValue =
  listArray (0, lengthValue - 1) [bases ! (((i * 7) + 3) .&. 3) | i <- [0 .. lengthValue - 1]]

complementScore :: Int -> Int
complementScore code
  | code == ord 'A' = 4
  | code == ord 'C' = 3
  | code == ord 'G' = 2
  | otherwise = 1

reverseComplementChecksum :: UArray Int Int -> Int
reverseComplementChecksum dna = go (snd (bounds dna)) 1 0
  where
    go i pos acc
      | i < 0 = acc
      | otherwise =
          let acc' = (acc + pos * complementScore (dna ! i)) `mod` modValue
           in go (i - 1) (pos + 1) acc'

main :: IO ()
main = do
  let n = 1000000
      result = reverseComplementChecksum (makeDna n)
  print result

public final class ReverseComplement {
    private static final int MOD = 100000007;
    private static final byte[] BASES = {'A', 'C', 'G', 'T'};

    private ReverseComplement() {}

    private static byte[] makeDna(int length) {
        final byte[] data = new byte[length];
        for (int i = 0; i < length; i += 1) {
            data[i] = BASES[((i * 7) + 3) % 4];
        }
        return data;
    }

    private static int complementScore(byte code) {
        if (code == 'A') {
            return 4;
        }
        if (code == 'C') {
            return 3;
        }
        if (code == 'G') {
            return 2;
        }
        return 1;
    }

    private static int reverseComplementChecksum(byte[] data) {
        int acc = 0;
        int pos = 1;
        for (int i = data.length - 1; i >= 0; i -= 1) {
            acc = (acc + pos * complementScore(data[i])) % MOD;
            pos += 1;
        }
        return acc;
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        final int n = 1000000;
        final int result = reverseComplementChecksum(makeDna(n));
        System.out.println(result);
    }
}

    i = i + 1
  end
  return data
end

local function complement_score(code)
  if code == 65 then
    return 4
  end
  if code == 67 then
    return 3
  end
  if code == 71 then
    return 2
  end
  return 1
end

  local acc = 0
  local pos = 1
  local i = #data
  while i >= 1 do
    acc = (acc + pos * complement_score(data[i])) % MOD
    pos = pos + 1
    i = i - 1
  end

Reverse Complement / OCaml

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/ocaml/workloads/reverse_complement.ml 

let mod_value = 100000007

let imod x = x mod mod_value

let parse_int s = int_of_string s

let base_at i =
  match ((i * 7) + 3) mod 4 with
  | 0 -> 'A'
  | 1 -> 'C'
  | 2 -> 'G'
  | _ -> 'T'

let complement_score = function
  | 'A' -> 4
  | 'C' -> 3
  | 'G' -> 2
  | _ -> 1

let make_dna length =
  let data = Bytes.create length in
  let i = ref 0 in
  while !i < length do
    Bytes.set data !i (base_at !i);
    incr i
  done;
  data

let reverse_complement_checksum data =
  let acc = ref 0 in
  let pos = ref 1 in
  let i = ref (Bytes.length data - 1) in
  while !i >= 0 do
    acc := imod (!acc + (!pos * complement_score (Bytes.get data !i)));
    incr pos;
    decr i
  done;
  !acc

let () =
  let n = 1000000 in
  let result = string_of_int (reverse_complement_checksum (make_dna n)) in
  print_endline result

Reverse Complement / Perl

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/perl/workloads/reverse_complement.pl 

use strict;
use warnings;

use constant MOD => 100000007;
my @BASES = (65, 67, 71, 84);

sub parse_args {
    my (@argv) = @_;
    return \@argv;
}

sub make_dna {
    my ($length) = @_;
    my $dna = "\0" x $length;
    for (my $i = 0; $i < $length; $i += 1) {
        substr($dna, $i, 1) = chr($BASES[(($i * 7) + 3) % 4]);
    }
    return $dna;
}

sub complement_score {
    my ($code) = @_;
    return 4 if $code == 65;
    return 3 if $code == 67;
    return 2 if $code == 71;
    return 1;
}

sub reverse_complement_checksum {
    my ($dna) = @_;
    my $acc = 0;
    my $pos = 1;
    for (my $i = length($dna) - 1; $i >= 0; $i -= 1) {
        $acc = ($acc + $pos * complement_score(ord(substr($dna, $i, 1)))) % MOD;
        $pos += 1;
    }
    return $acc;
}

my $N = 1000000;
my $result = reverse_complement_checksum(make_dna(0 + $N));
print "$result\n";

function make_dna(int $length): string {
    $dna = str_repeat("\0", $length);
    for ($i = 0; $i < $length; $i += 1) {
        $dna[$i] = chr(BASES[(($i * 7) + 3) % 4]);
    }
    return $dna;
}

    if ($code === 65) {
        return 4;
    }
    if ($code === 67) {
        return 3;
    }
    if ($code === 71) {
        return 2;
    }
    return 1;
}

function reverse_complement_checksum(string $dna): int {
    $acc = 0;
    $pos = 1;
    for ($i = strlen($dna) - 1; $i >= 0; $i -= 1) {
        $acc = ($acc + $pos * complement_score(ord($dna[$i]))) % MOD;
        $pos += 1;
    }
    return $acc;
}

#!/usr/bin/env python3

from __future__ import annotations

import sys


MOD = 100000007
BASES = (65, 67, 71, 84)


def make_dna(length: int) -> bytearray:
    data = bytearray(length)
    i = 0
    while i < length:
        data[i] = BASES[(i * 7 + 3) % 4]
        i += 1
    return data


def complement_score(code: int) -> int:
    if code == 65:
        return 4
    if code == 67:
        return 3
    if code == 71:
        return 2
    return 1


def reverse_complement_checksum(data: bytearray) -> int:
    acc = 0
    pos = 1
    i = len(data) - 1
    while i >= 0:
        acc = (acc + pos * complement_score(data[i])) % MOD
        pos += 1
        i -= 1
    return acc


if __name__ == '__main__':
    n = 1000000
    result = reverse_complement_checksum(make_dna(n))
    print(result)

Reverse Complement / R

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/r/workloads/reverse_complement.R 

#!/usr/bin/env Rscript

MOD <- 100000007
BASES <- c(65L, 67L, 71L, 84L)

make_dna <- function(length_value) {
  data <- raw(length_value)
  i <- 0L
  while (i < length_value) {
    data[[i + 1L]] <- as.raw(BASES[[((i * 7L + 3L) %% 4L) + 1L]])
    i <- i + 1L
  }
  data
}

complement_score <- function(code) {
  if (code == 65L) return(4L)
  if (code == 67L) return(3L)
  if (code == 71L) return(2L)
  1L
}

reverse_complement_checksum <- function(data) {
  acc <- 0
  pos <- 1
  i <- length(data) - 1
  while (i >= 0) {
    code <- as.integer(data[[i + 1]])
    acc <- (acc + pos * complement_score(code)) %% MOD
    pos <- pos + 1
    i <- i - 1
  }
  acc
}

args <- commandArgs(trailingOnly = TRUE)
length_value <- 1000000
result <- reverse_complement_checksum(make_dna(length_value))
cat(as.integer(result), "\n", sep = "")

    i += 1
  end

  return 3 if code == 67
  return 2 if code == 71

  1

  pos = 1

Reverse Complement / Rust

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/rust/src/bin/reverse_complement.rs 

const MOD: i32 = 100_000_007;
const BASES: [u8; 4] = [b'A', b'C', b'G', b'T'];

fn make_dna(length: i32) -> Vec<u8> {
    let mut data = vec![0_u8; length as usize];
    let mut i = 0_i32;
    while i < length {
        data[i as usize] = BASES[((i * 7 + 3) % 4) as usize];
        i += 1;
    }
    data
}

fn complement_score(code: u8) -> i32 {
    match code {
        b'A' => 4,
        b'C' => 3,
        b'G' => 2,
        _ => 1,
    }
}

fn reverse_complement_checksum(data: &[u8]) -> i32 {
    let mut acc = 0_i32;
    let mut pos = 1_i32;
    let mut i = data.len();
    while i > 0 {
        let index = i - 1;
        acc = (acc + pos * complement_score(data[index])) % MOD;
        pos += 1;
        i = index;
    }
    acc
}


fn main() {
    let n = 1_000_000;
    let result = reverse_complement_checksum(&make_dna(n));
    println!("{}", result);
}

Reverse Complement / Scala

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/scala/workloads/ReverseComplement.scala 

object ReverseComplement {
  private final val Mod = 100000007
  private final val Bases = Array[Byte]('A', 'C', 'G', 'T')

  private def makeDna(length: Int): Array[Byte] = {
    val data = new Array[Byte](length)
    var i = 0
    while (i < length) {
      data(i) = Bases(((i * 7) + 3) % 4)
      i += 1
    }
    data
  }

  private def complementScore(code: Byte): Int = {
    if (code == 'A') 4
    else if (code == 'C') 3
    else if (code == 'G') 2
    else 1
  }

  private def reverseComplementChecksum(data: Array[Byte]): Int = {
    var acc = 0
    var pos = 1
    var i = data.length - 1
    while (i >= 0) {
      acc = (acc + pos * complementScore(data(i))) % Mod
      pos += 1
      i -= 1
    }
    acc
  }

  def main(args: Array[String]): Unit = {
    val n = 1000000
    val result = reverseComplementChecksum(makeDna(n))
    println(result)
  }
}

Reverse Complement / Swift

/Users/anthony/Desktop/scripts/scripts/benchmark/languages/swift/workloads/reverse_complement.swift 

let mod = 100_000_007
let bases: [UInt8] = [65, 67, 71, 84]

func makeDna(_ length: Int) -> [UInt8] {
    var data = [UInt8](repeating: 0, count: length)
    var i = 0
    while i < length {
        data[i] = bases[(i * 7 + 3) % 4]
        i += 1
    }
    return data
}

func complementScore(_ code: UInt8) -> Int {
    if code == 65 {
        return 4
    }
    if code == 67 {
        return 3
    }
    if code == 71 {
        return 2
    }
    return 1
}

func reverseComplementChecksum(_ data: [UInt8]) -> Int {
    var acc = 0
    var pos = 1
    var i = data.count
    while i > 0 {
        let index = i - 1
        acc = (acc + pos * complementScore(data[index])) % mod
        pos += 1
        i = index
    }
    return acc
}

let n = 1000000
let result = reverseComplementChecksum(makeDna(n))
print(result)
